Chapter 703: The Excited Old Horse

The clay statue was overwhelmed with emotions upon seeing the old horse, and the old horse was even more overwhelmed with emotions upon seeing the clay statue.

It’s really not easy! I can finally act as a guardian for once!

How often does one encounter a Fusion Stage opponent?

This kid Meng Jingzhou has finally attracted a Fusion Stage enemy, and only one at that.

When the old horse sensed the commotion outside the city from the stable, he had rushed over immediately, fearful that enemies beyond his capabilities would show up later.

This is a once-in-a-millennia opportunity; I absolutely can’t miss this!

The clay statue stared at the old horse. The other party’s bloodline is pure; he’s definitely a Great Demon king from the Dragon-Horse Tribe living in the East Sea!

“You...”

The clay statue had barely uttered one word when the old horse stamped on space, a pristinely white true dragon phantom appearing behind him—the sign of a pure-blooded dragon-horse!

The white true dragon phantom coiled into a circle, resembling the moon in the sky.

How could the old horse give the clay statue a chance to speak? The longer the night, the more the nightmares; delays breed trouble—I must settle this battle quickly!

The clay statue didn’t expect the old horse to blatantly disregard rules and customs, not even exchanging a few courteous words before starting the battle.

He was a Great Yu cultivator. During the long span of several hundred thousand years, a problem had arisen with his method of slumber. When he woke up, he found his body had decayed, leaving only his soul.

He had no other choice. Taking over another body would mean starting over, and he had no idea how long that would take. He opted for the Faith-Molded Body-Forming Art passed down from the Great Qian Dynasty and chose an inconspicuous city like Lintian City.

I thought I'd been cautious enough. This place may not even see a Fusion cultivator for decades. How could I run into a Fusion Stage Great Demon King on an ordinary night for no rhyme or reason?

Where did this demon pop up from? Does Great Xia not care?

With an excited dragon-like roar, the old horse shook his mane and leaped into the air. His qi and blood transformed into blazing flames as he charged into the clay statue while treading on auspicious clouds and fire.

Horse Trampling the World!

The clay statue extended all ten fingers. An endless amount of water materialized out of thin air and formed a wall that pressed toward the old horse.

The old horse grinned widely, the dragon scales on its brow flashing twice. The water wall split down the middle, and the old horse galloped through.

Water-Splitting Technique!

I’d lived in the East Sea for years; manipulating seawater is child’s play. Yet the other party dares to play with water in front of me? He really doesn’t know how the character for “death” is written!

The clay statue never expected the old horse to pass through the water wall so easily and disrupt its attacks. All four hooves slammed into the clay statue simultaneously like four immense mountains, directly cracking it.

“The bullying has gone too far!” The clay statue flew into a rage. Even if I haven’t recovered to my peak, I shouldn’t be beaten so badly by a demon king of the same cultivation realm.

The clay statue’s brow split open, revealing a third eye. This was an innate divine eye. Although it couldn’t compare to the Immortal Dao Heavenly Eye, it held many mysteries and had helped him stand out among Fusion cultivators.

The third eye released a beam of golden light, immobilizing the old horse in that space.

The old horse showed no panic. Instead, it revealed a delighted smile.

Two mystical horns appeared on the old horse’s head—the dragon horns unique to the Dragon race!

He let out a long neigh, exhaling a puff of demon qi from its nostrils. His sweat flowed and evaporated, turning into mist.

The clay statue gritted its teeth and tried to forcibly suppress the old horse. But with the dragon horns revealed, how could the old horse be suppressed by the flag statue?

The old horse was as swift as lightning. Riding on light, he lowered his neck slightly and rammed into the clay statue with his horns!

“Golden Armor Protector Divine Seal!”

The clay statue delivered a seal strike from its brow. This is a Buddhist seal I learned from the Buddhist Kingdom. It’s immensely powerful!

But before the old horse, the Buddhist seal was like a pane of paper, easily pierced. The clay statue was struck by the dragon horns, and its lower body shattered. The dragon horns shot forth thousands of streams of metallic qi, slashing the lower body to smithereens.

The clay statue used its third eye to cast numerous divine abilities, illuminating the sky until it was as bright as day, but everything was neutralized by the old horse. Forced into a passive defense, the clay statue kept retreating.

“The old horse is pretty excited,” Meng Jingzhou mumbled.

It’s been nearly three years since I’ve seen the old horse this active.

“I don’t care who you are! Regardless of the outcome today, you will definitely be hunted down in the future!” the clay statue yelled. It was hard to discern if it was a bluff or a genuine threat.

The old horse grew even more excited. This means the clay statue has no helpers now.

Then why not fight with all my might?

The white dragon phantom behind the old horse merged with him. Dragon blood boiled, surging toward the heavens. The old horse transformed into a hundred-zhang tall dragon-horse, the dragon scales from his brow spreading across his entire body like pristine white armor.

Any cultivator who had exchanged blows with the old horse before would run as far as they could at the sight of this move.

Dragon Battles in the Wild—this was a move even Meng Jingzhou’s father wouldn’t dare to face head-on.

”No!” the clay statue let out a despairing roar.

Boom!

Under the impact, the clay statue turned to dust, dying without an intact corpse.

The old horse snorted triumphantly and returned to his normal size.

Comfortable.

The commotion quickly drew the attention of the authorities. The city lord hastily brought people over to investigate.

“City Lord, you’ve arrived just in time. This person called Mu Xi was casting curses on people, and we caught her red-handed.” Lu Yang pulled Mu Xi out. If not for Lu Yang’s protection earlier, it was uncertain whether Mu Xi would have survived.

At the same time, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou flashed their Dao-Seeking Sect identity jade tablets to prove their identities.

The city lord looked at them with shock and bewilderment. So these are Dao-Seeking Sect disciples? Catching a single mortal could cause such a huge commotion?

““Ahem, it wasn’t just catching this mortal. There was originally a Deity Temple here, which housed an ancient Fusion cultivator,” Meng Jingzhou explained awkwardly. The Deity Temple had been leveled during the battle earlier."

After hearing Meng Jingzhou recount the event, the city lord felt a wave of lingering fear. An ancient Fusion cultivator had been hiding so close to the area under my jurisdiction.

“Many thanks to you both for your assistance.”

“Just doing our duty. We have other matters to attend to and will have to take our leave first.” The two cupped their fists and handed Mu Xi to the city lord before returning to the city with the old horse.

They still had unfinished business.

“Should we test Gu Junye’s spirit root?” Lu Yang suggested.

If Gu Junye had a Triple Spirit Root or better, he could participate in the Dao-Seeking Sect’s entrance trials.

It was currently late at night, a time originally meant for sleep. However, the commotion from the battle this time had been so enormous that it roused everyone, including Gu Junye.

Gu Junye stood in his courtyard with his hands clasped behind his back, the cool breeze rustling his hair. He stared intently in the direction of the battle.

“The enemies...are they coming?”

Meng Jingzhou concealed himself and shook the Bone Foundation Stone near Gu Junye. Inside the stone, a pure, flawless circular mass of water appeared, about half the size of a fist.

“Whoa, a Water Spirit Root. This kid really has something.”

Since both his character and aptitude were satisfactory, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou revealed themselves, startling Gu Junye.

Fortunately, Gu Junye possessed an eternally steadfast Dao heart and quickly recovered.

He gazed at the two quietly and sighed softly. “Has this day finally come?”

“...We are disciples of the Dao-Seeking Sect. Perhaps you have heard our names. I am Lu Yang, and he is Meng Jingzhou.”

Both were frequently recurring characters in storytelling performances.

Hearing their names, Gu Junye’s expression changed. “Xuanyuan Sword Master, Unbreakable Saint, I never imagined you two to have also reincarnated.”

Lu Yang, “...”

Meng Jingzhou, “...”

After a moment of silence, Meng Jingzhou said, “...After our observation, we unanimously agreed that your character and aptitude meet our Dao-Seeking Sect’s entry requirements. On the second day of the second month next year, you may come to the Dao-Seeking Sect to participate in the entrance examinations.

“Here is a map to the sect and travel expenses.” Meng Jingzhou gave Gu Junye a map and some spirit stones.

After that, the two intended to leave, but Gu Junye stopped them.

“Wait a moment. Could you grant me one wish? I’ll do anything.”

~~~

The next day, the academy was abuzz with various discussions about the previous night’s battle. Some said it was a fight between great cultivators, others claimed it was someone undergoing a lightning tribulation, while others insisted demons had invaded.

During class, people noticed Mu Xi was absent.

Mu Yu recalled the authorities searching her home last night and was somewhat distracted.

Gu Junye sat in his corner seat, listening to the lesson as attentively as ever.

Suddenly, two tall, slender figures appeared at the classroom’s door. With their backs faced to the light, their features were unclear.

The teacher and the students below the platform were momentarily taken aback, unsure who these two people were.

“Who are you?!” the teacher demanded.

The two figures walked into the classroom as if they hadn’t heard the teacher. Then, they walked straight to the stunned Gu Junye and cupped their fists, saying earnestly, “Fellow Daoist, we’ve finally found you! We encountered an unprecedented crisis. Only you can resolve it. This world needs you!”

Chapter 704: The World Needs You to Save It

The students and the teacher in the academy turned around in astonishment, watching the two mysterious figures enter.

These two mysterious figures seemed to possess an innate enigmatic aura. They exuded a powerful oppressive pressure merely by standing there.

Gu Junye was not surprised to see these two seek him out. He sighed softly, “So you still found me.”

One of the mysterious figures had a hoarse voice, which didn’t match his youthful appearance. “Fellow Daoist, I know that you have lost trust in the organization since that incident and have lived in seclusion here. But I beg you to believe in the organization.”

The mysterious figure’s words seemed to trigger a taboo memory in Gu Junye. He clenched his fists tightly and looked up abruptly, his eyes seeming to contain a supreme true dragon roaring within.

“Believe in the organization? Then why did the organization send us on that kind of mission? It was a suicide mission!

“Can you imagine it? One moment, a friend is laughing and chatting; the next, they are pierced by tentacles and turned into a desiccated corpse!

“Endless enemies surged forth like a tide. The Sacred Lord, claimed to embody eternal light, died. The Pan God, capable of splitting heaven and earth apart, died...

“Everyone died, everyone died! Only I survived!

“Didn’t the organization know the situation there? Where was the organization when we were trapped? Where was the support? Where were the reinforcements?!”

The other mysterious man’s face was covered in scars, as if he had endured countless bloody battles, his Dao heart firm as iron. But his heart still trembled when he looked into Gu Junye’s eyes.

The mysterious man recalled the various deeds of the person before him. Those were like myths and legends to them.

This person had wandered through the long river of history, leaving his legends at every juncture. Across nine cycles of reincarnation, he challenged immortals with sheer strength, balancing the three realms of Heaven, Earth, and Mortal single-handedly.

The mysterious man explained, his tone tinged with bitterness. “The organization was held back by enemies from the heavens and couldn’t come to your aid.” He pointed to the scars on his face. “These injuries were sustained during that time.

“Fellow Daoist, those monsters from the earth abyss are climbing out again! The organization needs you to step in! The world needs you to save it!”

Gu Junye stared at the two mysterious figures, feeling like he could see the shadows of his old friends in them.

He slowly stood up and sighed, as if resigning himself to fate. “Very well. Then I shall make this journey.”

The two mysterious men’s icy faces involuntarily broke into smiles.

“Fellow Daoist, after you!”

Gu Junye showed no intention of explaining to the others. Under everyone’s eyes, he was escorted out of the classroom by the two mysterious figures.

Then, he looked up at the sky and took a huge leap, vanishing into thin air.

~~~

“So you’ll just stay here for half a day and go home directly after school?” The two mysterious men brought Gu Junye outside the city, their faces changing to reveal their true appearances.

They were actually Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou!

“Many thanks, senior brothers.” Gu Junye cupped his fists, his face flushed with excitement.

Meng Jingzhou waved his hand. “It’s nothing.”

Lu Yang patted Gu Junye’s shoulder. “You must come in the second month next year. I have high hopes for you!”

With that, the two boarded the carriage and headed for the next location.

“You know, that was actually quite fun.”

“Right? I think so too.”

~~~

After the two left, roughly half a day later, two figures flew from the distance and landed at the ruins of the Deity Temple.

Staring at the collapsed temple and the clay statue shattered on the ground, the two figures furrowed their brows tightly.

“The Life Tablet wasn’t wrong. Wang Chuan has truly perished.”

“But how is that possible? Although he was still in the phase of reforming his physical body, he was still a Fusion cultivator. The strongest cultivator in this city is only at the Nascent Soul Stage. How could they have harmed Wang Chuan?”

“Could it have been a Great Xia Fusion cultivator passing by who discovered him?”

“That shouldn’t be it either. Wang Chuan was formidable. Unless he encountered a top-tier Fusion cultivator, he should have been able to escape.”

“Strange.”

“Let’s see what happened then; everything will become clear.”

One of them chanted an incantation inwardly. The faith power scattered around recoalesced. Although it couldn’t resurrect Wang Chuan, it could replay the events of the previous night. Fragments of last night appeared in his palm.

Two Nascent Soul prodigies had discovered Wang Chuan. The latter intended to attack them, but was suppressed by a white horse descending from the sky. In an exchange that was as fast as lightning, Wang Chuan was annihilated by the white horse, his soul disintegrating.

Even though they were just phantom images, the two figures shuddered upon seeing the white horse execute “Dragon-Horse Unification, Dragon Battles in the Wild.”

If it were us, we probably couldn’t have withstood this move either.

“These two Nascent Soul cultivators look familiar... I remember! Aren’t these two the rising stars of the Dao-Seeking Sect? This one is Lu Yang, who once fought the young creed leader of the Heavenly Court Creed to a draw.” One of them suddenly realized. If not for the Heavenly Court Creed, they wouldn’t have even paid attention to Lu Yang’s existence.

“Who is that white horse?”

“No idea. I haven’t seen it before.”

“Let’s bring this piece of intelligence back and show it to His Excellency.”

The two immediately flew back to their headquarters.

~~~

The headquarters was located in a newly opened dimension. The two knocked on the door, verified their identities with their mental power, and entered the space.

Inside the space, powerful experts were as numerous as clouds. Each possessed unique skills and had left their mark in history. Although the two were Fusion cultivators, they ranked at the bottom here and were responsible for errands.

“Your Excellency, this is the scene from before Wang Chuan perished.” The two deferentially presented a magical artifact that was temporarily forged from faith power.

The leader was a youth who appeared even younger than Lu Yang.

Wang Chuan held considerable influence among Fusion cultivators. His demise was beyond everyone’s expectations, so they regarded it extremely seriously. If possible, they wanted to avenge him.

Otherwise, if subordinates casually died outside and he remained indifferent, his other subordinates would be disillusioned, and they might defect to Wu Youdao.

This was the headquarters of the Great Yu Alliance, aimed at gathering all sleeping cultivators from the Great Yu era. Great Xia’s strength exceeded their expectations, so some advocated for strength in numbers and that everyone should act together. Moreover, they believed that following Wu Youdao, the sixth Yu Emperor, held no future. Hence, they formed this separate faction.

It had been a long time since they heard any news about Wu Youdao. They had no idea what he was secretly plotting.

The Imperial Preceptor always planned meticulously before acting. The long silence might imply he was preparing for some heaven-shocking event.

The youth carefully watched the recording of Wang Chuan’s final moments. Suddenly, his eyes lit up, and he even temporarily tossed aside the thought of avenging Wang Chuan.

He stared fixedly at the sword in Lu Yang’s hand and became extremely agitated, greed glinting from the bottom of his eyes. “The Yu Emperor’s personal sword!” Although its appearance differed from the original sword, he still recognized the Qingfeng Sword’s origin at a glance.

Everyone was stunned. They all knew the youth looked down on Wu Youdao. The only person he would call “Yu Emperor” was the founding monarch of the Great Yu Dynasty—Wu Yao.

Chapter 705: Sacrificed the Great Yu Dynasty

How did the Yu Emperor’s personal sword end up in the hands of this minor cultivator? Was it dug up from an ancient tomb?

Everyone’s mind raced with speculation.

The youth’s close aide was privy to more information. He had heard the youth mention that the Yu Emperor, Wu Yao, had become an immortal long ago, just that the world didn’t know about it.

What does the Yu Emperor’s personal sword signify? It signifies an immortal sword! This is something all half-immortals dream of.

No wonder His Excellency is so excited.

“Does anyone know who the person holding the immortal sword is?” The youth hadn’t paid attention to the younger generation. He didn’t see the need to focus on geniuses before they matured.

There are so many geniuses in this world. I was one of them back then. But how many are still alive? Only I remain.

“Your Excellency, this person’s name is Lu Yang. He is a disciple of the Dao-Seeking Sect Leader. He once fought the Heavenly Court Young Creed Leader to a draw.”

Hearing this, the youth began to regard Lu Yang with slight importance.

But only slightly.

“The Dao-Seeking Sect, one of the Five Great Immortal Sects huh...”

Noticing the youth seemed tempted, a close aide transmitted an auditory message to remind him. “Your Excellency, the Yu Emperor’s personal sword that Lu Yang possesses might have been bestowed by the Yu Emperor. We must not act rashly.”

This person called Lu Yang might be a personal disciple of the Yu Emperor. How else would he have obtained the Yu Emperor’s personal sword?

Furthermore, Lu Yang could fight the Heavenly Court Young Creed Leader to a draw. It’s said that this young creed leader’s shifu is the Heavenly Court’s ruler, Dou Heavenly Sovereign, a bona fide ancient immortal.

A draw between an ancient immortal’s disciple and the Yu Emperor’s disciple—perfectly reasonable.

The youth did not get angry at his aide’s reminder. Instead, he laughed heartily and said meaningfully, “If I didn’t know the inside story, your story would indeed make sense. Unfortunately, your speculation is impossible. The Yu Emperor is no longer around.”

The aide was flabbergasted. The Yu Emperor is no longer around? What does that mean? The Yu Emperor is an immortal; how could he be gone?

“Why do you think the Yu Emperor allowed his dynasty to be destroyed?” the youth countered, though it sounded more like he was murmuring to himself. “He was seeking an opportunity—a chance to leave this world.”

The youth revealed a reminiscent expression. “Since ancient times, this world has been sealed. No one can leave, and no one can enter. The Yu Emperor rose during the late Great Qian era, vied for supremacy with various heroes, and established the Great Yu Dynasty. His power and influence were immense, and his cultivation was that of an immortal. Whether in terms of influence, territory, cultivation, or life experience, he had reached the zenith. There was no room for further advancement.

“Thus, he always wanted to leave this world and see what lay outside.

“Did the Yu Emperor not know about Wu Youdao’s slogan of restoring Great Yu? Of course, he knew. He simply saw no need to intervene.

“Rather than saying the Great Yu Dynasty was destroyed, it’s perhaps more accurate to say the Yu Emperor personally sacrificed his own dynasty. As for the method he used, you don’t need to know. It involves the power of a Dao Fruit. You won’t remember even if I tell you.

“After Great Yu’s fall, I saw the Yu Emperor a few times. He hadn’t left yet, maybe because certain conditions weren’t met. It was only recently that I sensed his aura for an instant, as if it erupted then dissipated. He no longer exists in this world. I believe that was when the Yu Emperor left this world.

“That is why you needn’t worry about the Yu Emperor showing up again. He has already left this world. This kid named Lu Yang merely obtained the Yu Emperor’s personal sword by chance.

“Immortal items belong to the capable. Lu Yang is a mere Nascent Soul cultivator. How could he be qualified to hold such an immortal artifact?

“I reckon the conditions for the Yu Emperor to leave this world were harsh. Perhaps it required not only sacrificing the Great Yu Dynasty but also sacrificing himself. In the end, only he could leave, unable to take anything, which is why the sword was left behind.

“Therefore, what I value is not a single sword, but everything the Yu Emperor left behind!

“And the clues lie with this kid named Lu Yang.”

The youth stared at the recording of Lu Yang again, muttering incantations and calculating Lu Yang’s location. Suddenly, his body trembled inexplicably, as if slapped by someone.

“Strange.” The youth hissed and glanced around suspiciously, wondering whether he should recalculate, but eventually decided against it.

“Your Excellency, what’s the matter?”

“I actually couldn’t calculate this kid’s location. Not just him, but the kid beside him and the old horse too... Right, legends say the Yu Emperor’s personal sword can sever anything. It must be the immortal sword severing my connection to Lu Yang. Or perhaps this kid obtained some other immortal artifact that blocks divination.”

The youth’s expression grew even greedier. “This kid has considerable fortuitous opportunities. I’m afraid it will be very difficult to track down his location.”

“Your Excellency, I have a plan,” his aide said. He was responsible for collecting intelligence on Great Xia and was well-versed in the situations of its major sects.

“Let’s hear it.”

The aide elaborated, “From what I know, the second day of the second month next year is the Dao-Seeking Sect’s recruitment day. That Lu Yang will definitely be at the Dao-Seeking Sect then.

“Moreover, the Dao-Seeking Sect will be busy organizing the exams. They will be too preoccupied to pay him much mind, and their defenses will be lax. We can seize this opportunity to launch a major assault on the sect and catch him completely off guard!

“At that time, it won’t be just a mere Lu Yang—the entire Dao-Seeking Sect will be within your pocket, Your Excellency!”

The youth’s eyes lit up. This is a good idea. Destroying the Dao-Seeking Sect will also establish our authority. Perhaps the immortal artifacts left by the Yu Emperor were acquired by the Dao-Seeking Sect and then bestowed upon Lu Yang.

The Yu Emperor’s immortal relics! We might even find the legendary Immortal-Exterminating Sword Array in the Dao-Seeking Sect! Rumors say this sword array originated from ancient times, and after modifications from the Yu Emperor, its power was so great that it could force immortals to kneel!

“You sometimes come up with good ideas too.”

The aide bowed obsequiously, “I’ve merely learned a fraction from you, Your Excellency.”

The youth was very satisfied with his subordinate’s boot-licking.

~~~

“Strange,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy mumbled.

“Immortal Fairy, what’s wrong?” Lu Yang asked.

“It seemed someone tried to calculate your karma just now. This immortal casually blocked it. I’m not sure who wants to scheme against you.

“When they couldn’t calculate your karma, they tried to indirectly target you through the Meng boy and the little white horse. This immortal blocked that too.”

Lu Yang was equally befuddled. I’d strictly followed Senior Brother Dai’s teachings to be honest and well-behaved throughout this journey. All the flashy deeds were done by the old horse. Why would anyone still want to scheme against me? He asked, “Is the other party strong?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy tilted her head and stroked her chin. “Judging by the fact that I blocked it with a wave of my hand, they are definitely weaker than me.”

Lu Yang, “...”

I mean, isn’t that stating the obvious? Immortal Fairy, in your worldview, is there anyone stronger than you?

“Although there’s no one stronger than this immortal, there are those on a similar level, like Lass Yun. The other party’s strength is definitely weaker than Lass Yun’s too.”

Chapter 706: Golden Cicada Shell

The old horse pulled the two to their third destination—Yanshan City[1] in Quan Province.

“The third person is named Tao Tingfeng,[2] fifteen years old, and from Yanshan City, Quan Province. Uh, Man Gu discovered him when he passed through Yanshan City after descending from Mount Yan, where he had gone to slay demons.”

“How did Junior Brother Man evaluate him?” Lu Yang asked curiously.

Meng Jingzhou looked at the words in the booklet with a peculiar expression. “He said Tao Tingfeng is timid, doesn’t dare to stir up trouble, and that his character is far inferior to Brother Lu’s and Brother Meng’s.”

“...Is Junior Brother Man praising us?”

Meng Jingzhou couldn’t figure it out either. “Judging by the overall context, he should be praising us.”

Tao Tingfeng was born into a Nascent Soul ancestral clan, a prominent local clan.

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou easily found the Tao residence.

The Tao family had hired a teacher, so their descendants didn’t need to attend the city’s private school. Moreover, unlike private schools, the Tao Family not only had their disciples study the Words of Sages but also taught cultivation knowledge.

When Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou stealthily sneaked into the Tao residence, Tao Tingfeng and the other Tao Family disciples were listening to a lecture from a clan uncle.

The Tao Family disciples regarded this clan uncle as an idol. He had considerable talent in cultivation, already reaching the Intermediate Foundation Establishment Stage by just thirty years old. The clan members believed he had the potential to attempt a breakthrough to the Nascent Soul Stage, becoming the Tao Family’s second Nascent Soul old ancestor.

“The path of cultivation fears impatience most. Before cultivating, one must cultivate the mind and heart. Those who are often restless while cultivating are prone to qi deviation...

“Qi Training, Foundation Establishment, Golden Core, Nascent Soul... each cultivation realm is a massive step. If you can ascend one major step, your status and standing will undergo a tremendous transformation.

“Don’t think that our Tao Family being a Nascent Soul ancestral clan and having some say in this small patch of area in Yanshan City means anything much. If you leave Yanshan City and meet a Divine Transfiguration ancestral clan, you’ll realize our proud Nascent Soul ancestral clan is nothing special.

“When I traveled through Quan Province in my youth, I once witnessed an Apex Nascent Soul expert make a move. It felt like the mountains were shaking and ocean waves were roaring, sweeping everything with its dominance and stirring people’s hearts.”

The Tao Family’s old ancestor was only at the Basic Nascent Soul Stage.

“Another example is the great battle in Yanshan City half a month ago. A demon secretly infiltrated Great Xia and hid in Mount Yan. Fortunately, a righteous expert stepped in and killed it; otherwise, who knows what disaster might have happened.

“If I’m not mistaken, that was likely a legendary Divine Transfiguration expert.”

The Tao Family disciples gasped upon hearing the words “Divine Transfiguration.”

“This Nascent Soul cultivator of the Tao Family...”

Lu Yang was bored by the lecture and split off a wisp of his spiritual consciousness to scout out the Tao Family old ancestor’s condition.

The Tao Family old ancestor and Lu Yang were both at the Basic Nascent Soul Stage. Logically, those at the same level couldn’t probe each other with spiritual consciousness, but Lu Yang was clearly beyond logic.

“What about the Tao Family old ancestor?” Unlike Lu Yang, Meng Jingzhou was listening to the lesson attentively.

“Rather than a true Nascent Soul cultivator, he’s more like a Half-Step Nascent Soul cultivator. It’s probably a side effect of a forced breakthrough. He has the power of a Nascent Soul cultivator but with a limit on how many times he can use it.”

Isn’t calling yourself a “Nascent Soul ancestral clan” a bit too forced?

“What is this?” Meng Jingzhou waved his hand. As the young master of the world’s number one ancestral clan, he had seen all kinds of clans. “I’ve even seen a Golden Core cultivator getting his fortune told, and the fortune teller said he would definitely reach the Nascent Soul Stage. Afterward, he made his family call themselves a ‘Nascent Soul ancestral clan’ publicly.”

After all, ancestral clans weren’t organizations that required annual assessments to get certified by the imperial court. Their perceived strength relied entirely on their reputation in the local community and could largely be inflated.

Of course, the Meng Family’s reputation was not inflated in the least. If their strength had any exaggeration, they wouldn’t still be thriving in the imperial city.

“Class is over.”

“Come, let’s go out and play.” Children at this age were fond of playing, and Tao Tingfeng was no exception.

Having heard the clan uncle describe the battle on Mount Yan, Tao Tingfeng felt an itch in his heart to go check out the situation for himself.

I’m going to take a look.

Tao Tingfeng was conflicted for a moment but quickly made up his mind to head to Mount Yan.

Although Mount Yan had already been sealed off by the authorities and entry was forbidden, he had played there since childhood and knew a small path.

This small path is indeed not blocked. Tao Tingfeng effortlessly made his way to the site of the battle on Mount Yan.

The depths of Mount Yan were filled with deep craters punched out by Man Gu’s fists. Lu Yang could recognize them at a glance.

Upon seeing these craters, Tao Tingfeng’s eyes widened, his mouth agape. So this is what a battle at the Divine Transfiguration Stage is like?

Suddenly, something flashed across the sky and crashed toward Mount Yan with a whoosh. It landed not far from Tao Tingfeng, startling him greatly.

Tao Tingfeng originally didn’t dare approach, but his curiosity got the better of him, and he decided to head over to take a look.

“It’s a person!” Tao Tingfeng finally saw what had fallen. It was actually a cultivator, severely injured and barely breathing.

The gravely wounded cultivator tensed up upon seeing someone approach, but relaxed upon realizing it was a mortal who posed no threat.

Then, he remembered something. So what if he is a cultivator or a mortal? Even if he holds malicious intent, what can I do? My injuries are beyond saving; there’s no point in killing me—I’m going to die anyway.

“Are you alright?” Tao Tingfeng cautiously approached the cultivator, who clearly didn’t seem alright.

The cultivator gave a bitter laugh. “To think that I, Chess-Observing True Lord, would meet a boy like you at my life’s end. Despite all my calculations, I ultimately couldn’t out-calculate fate.”

“Chess-Observing True Lord?” Lu Yang mumbled softly. In his recollection, there seemed to have been such a Fusion cultivator during the Great Qian Era.

“Never mind, it seems that I’m destined to have no affinity with this item.”

Only then did Tao Tingfeng notice the wooden box that the Chess-Observing True Lord was clutching tightly against his chest.

“This item is called the Golden Cicada Shell. I seized it from an intractable opponent at a heavy cost. I never imagined it would end up benefiting a kid like you in the end.

“It appears this item has an affinity with you.

“Kid, this item is incredibly rare. Once you obtain it, you must be extremely cautious. Never let a second person know you possess it!”

With that, the Chess-Observing True Lord closed his eyes peacefully. His body gradually turned to dust and dissipated, leaving only the wooden box.

Tao Tingfeng was bewildered by this turn of events. He pressed his palms together and bowed twice toward where the Chess-Observing True Lord had vanished. Trembling, he opened the wooden box and found it contained a Golden Cicada Shell that was shining brightly.

“Immortal Fairy, what is the Golden Cicada Shell?” Lu Yang asked.

“In ancient times, there was a cicada demon who cultivated to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage, a level the cicada race had never attained before. His entire body turned golden, and he comprehended a divine ability called ‘Golden Cicada Sheds Its Shell,’ which could be used to improve one’s aptitude. It was precisely by relying on this divine ability that he cultivated to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage.

“The shell he left behind after his transformation is called the ‘Golden Cicada Shell.’ It’s a top-tier treasure for improving one’s aptitude.”

“What happened to that cicada demon after that?”

“This immortal squashed him to death.”

1. “Yanshan” could translate to “swallow mountain” or the Yan mountain range in Hebei Province. ☜

2. “Tingfeng” translates literally to “listen to the wind.” ☜

Chapter 707: Chess-Observing True Lord

Hearing how abruptly the cicada demon died, Lu Yang fell silent for a moment. I didn’t even get to find out the golden cicada’s name.

Noticing his silence, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy guessed what he was thinking. Adopting the demeanor of a seasoned veteran, she advised earnestly, “This is merely a glimpse of the brutal battles of antiquity. You need to adapt.

“The cruel things this immortal has experienced far exceed your imagination. Even now, I am unwilling to recall them.”

Lu Yang gained some insights. Indeed, the Battle of the Great Era in ancient times was a matter of life and death, absolutely not as casual as the Everlasting Immortal Fairy described. They must have involved bloody slaughter.

These aren’t pleasant memories for the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, which is why she’s reluctant to recall them.

“Back then, this immortal even used Cosmos in Palm to squash that golden cicada. Its juices stained all my fingers, and the sensation still feels disgusting even when I think back about it now.” Remembering that battle, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy revealed a look of disdain and flicked her hand to shake off the lingering revulsion.

She stood up from the bed. The mattress was soft and bounced a couple of times as she rose.

“You’ve seen Cosmos in Palm before, right? The Cosmos in Palm I used back then was thiiiiis big.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy spread her arms wide, vigorously outlining a circle.

She then extended one finger. “It was like this back then.” As she spoke, she poked Lu Yang a few times.

Lu Yang, “...”

Immortal Fairy, isn’t your gesture a bit too abstract?

~~~

Tao Tingfeng carefully examined the cicada exoskeleton in the box. It looked like it was cast from gold and appeared to be an impressive treasure. He had heard his clan uncle mention that only Fusion experts could be addressed with the title “true lord.”

This means that the Chess-Observing True Lord was a Fusion cultivator.

A treasure a Fusion cultivator was only willing to relinquish at death—one can only imagine how precious it is.

“What should I do with this thing? Should I try to make it recognize me as its master?” Tao Tingfeng was somewhat tempted. This is a heaven-sent great fortuitous opportunity.

Meng Jingzhou glanced down at Man Gu’s evaluation in the booklet. Recalling Tao Tingfeng’s recent actions—sneaking into the mountain and approaching the Chess-Observing True Lord—he mumbled quietly, “He doesn’t look like someone timid at all.”

Lu Yang stroked his chin and speculated, “Do you think it’s possible that Junior Brother Man used us as the reference for his evaluation?”

Meng Jingzhou pondered and felt Lu Yang had a point. Compared to Old Lu and my styles, this kid Tao Tingfeng can indeed be considered as timid as a mouse.

While the two were conversing, Tao Tingfeng followed his clan uncle’s past teachings. He bit his finger and dripped a drop of blood onto the Golden Cicada Shell. After the blood fell onto the shell, it quickly vanished.

“It worked?”

Delighted, Tao Tingfeng continued dripping blood until his face turned pale, nearing anemia. Only then did the Golden Cicada Shell stop absorbing blood. Instead, it hovered in the air and suddenly darted into Tao Tingfeng’s body, giving him a huge fright.

He hastily touched the spot where the Golden Cicada Shell had entered but found nothing. His body showed no adverse reactions either.

“Does this mean I have successfully become its master?” Tao Tingfeng wasn’t very sure.

“...Isn’t this master-recognition method a bit too simple?” Lu Yang remarked.

“This is called ‘the Great Dao is supremely simple, returning to simplicity and truth,’” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy said, using two idioms in one go.

“But is the Chess-Observing True Lord really gone just like that?” Meng Jingzhou was somewhat baffled.

We had only been squatting here for a while, and an archaic Fusion cultivator just died like that? Wasn’t that too easy?

Judging by the Chess-Observing True Lord’s injuries, he had experienced fierce battles before death—possibly more than one. The internals weren’t just external; even his soul was severely damaged, like a candle flickering in the wind, ready to die out at any moment.

And now, it really has died out.

“He’s not dead. The Everlasting Immortal Fairy says the Chess-Observing True Lord imprinted his last faint wisp of consciousness onto the Golden Cicada Shell. And now, he’s already in Tao Tingfeng’s mental space.”

~~~

Inside Tao Tingfeng’s mental space, a weak voice sounded. “Kid...I didn’t expect...you to know the master-recognition method.”

The Chess-Observing True Lord’s original plan was for Tao Tingfeng to safeguard the Golden Cicada Shell while he hid inside it and quietly recovered. I never expected this kid to directly drip blood onto the Golden Cicada Shell and make it recognize him as its master!

He was forced to enter Tao Tingfeng’s mental space along with the cicada shell.

Forget it. Perhaps I truly have no affinity with the Golden Cicada Shell.

Tao Tingfeng was startled at the voice. “Ah, y-you’re still alive?”

The Chess-Observing True Lord stopped speaking. His current condition was too terrible, and he needed to recuperate.

Tao Tingfeng was at a loss for what to do. He could only return home and fall asleep in his panicked state, his mind filled with the events on Mount Yan.

After resting the whole night, the Chess-Observing True Lord finally caught his breath and could speak proper sentences. “I didn’t expect I’m still alive. Kid, where is this place?”

Hearing the Chess-Observing True Lord speak again, Tao Tingfeng was mentally prepared this time and didn’t appear overly flustered. “True Lord, this is Yanshan City in Quan Province.”

“So it’s Quan province.”

Although Tao Tingfeng couldn’t see the Chess-Observing True Lord, he felt the latter must be wearing a ruminating expression now.

“True Lord, you are...” Tao Tingfeng tried to recall the historical figures he had studied, and there didn’t seem to be anyone called the Chess-Observing True Lord among them.

The Chess-Observing True Lord was somewhat displeased about not being recognized. “Junior, you are quite ignorant. This esteemed one is the Chess-Observing True Lord from Great Qian. My cultivation is at the Fusion Stage, and I am proficient in all hundred arts of cultivation.”

Although Tao Tingfeng had already figured out that the Chess-Observing True Lord was a Fusion cultivator, hearing the person in question admit to it still threw him into astonishment.

Goodness gracious! Fusion Stage?! The strongest person clan uncle has ever seen was only at the Apex Nascent Soul Stage.

Tao Tingfeng remembered another matter. “True Lord, what exactly is this Golden Cicada Shell? Why is there no change after it entered my body?”

The Chess-Observing True Lord snorted coldly. “Undiscerning kid. If not for fighting over this Golden Cicada Shell, I wouldn’t have been hunted and ended up in this plight.

“This Golden Cicada Shell is a supreme treasure. It would still be effective even if I cultivated to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage.

“I seized it from a Great Yu cultivator. Originally, I had an agreement with two others I was working with—they would help, while I’d give them benefits, and the item would be mine. Who knew those two would be untrustworthy and break our agreement, succumbing to greed and attempting to seize the Golden Cicada Shell?

“How dare those two steal from me? They really don’t know their place.” The Chess-Observing True Lord revealed a cruel smile, though his situation wasn’t much better.

“Alright, I still need to rest.” He had exhausted all his strength to say this much.

~~~

Borrowing the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s immortal consciousness, Lu Yang could observe Tao Tingfeng’s mental space. It was his first time seeing such a weak Fusion cultivator.

In contrast, the one residing in my mental space has been lively and energetic since her resurrection, even capable of exchanging a few moves with Big Senior Sister.

Chapter 708: Broadening Horizons

Half a month had passed since the Chess-Observing True Lord resided in Tao Tingfeng’s mental space. During this time, Tao Tingfeng studied cultivation knowledge from his clan uncle at the academy and the Chess-Observing True Lord, which naturally involved the latter’s scolding.

“Garbage, it’s all garbage. What nonsense is he teaching?

“How can one draw qi into the body with such a method? No wonder your family’s cultivation realms are so low.

“You must calm your mind and feel the omnipresent spirit energy. Then, use the first rays of dawn as a catalyst to mobilize the heaven and earth spirit energy around you, guiding both the dawn light and the spirit energy into your body. During this process, the higher the spirit energy concentration in your surroundings, the better!” the Chess-Observing True Lord ranted.

“When you draw qi into your body, don’t use the method your clan uncle taught. It’s too lousy.”

On the platform, the Intermediate Foundation Establishment Stage clan uncle paused and said, “Of course, the method for drawing qi into the body I’m teaching is just one of many. You may enter various sects in the future, and you can use the methods they teach then.”

Hearing this, Lu Yang shuddered. He recalled the brutal experience where Yun Zhi made him draw qi into the body when he first joined the sect—juggling water vats, grabbing tofu, eating tofu... He developed a psychological trauma toward tofu before successfully guiding qi into his body and stepping into the Qi Training Stage.

It was said that this was the method the ancient forebears initially used to draw qi into the body—simple yet effective.

“Immortal Fairy, how did you draw qi into your body back then? Did you use the ancient forebears’ method?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was quite surprised. “Huh? What method does drawing qi into the body need? Isn’t just sleeping once enough? Didn’t you do it that way?”

Lu Yang, “...”

He turned and asked Meng Jingzhou, “Old Meng, how did you draw qi into your body back then?”

Meng Jingzhou stroked his chin. “Let me think. Back then, before the matter was exposed, my dad was on better terms with me. He told me that the most important thing for drawing qi into the body is the concentration of spirit energy—the thicker the better.

“After joining the sect, I placed a circle of top-grade spirit stones around me, shattered them, and filled the cave abode with dense spirit energy. Then, I randomly absorbed a wisp.”

Lu Yang, “...”

Even the only son of a Fusion cultivator wouldn’t dare use such an extravagant method.

“Do you have some conflict with your dad?” Lu Yang had never asked Meng Jingzhou why he ran away from home back then, assuming the latter had nothing better to do.

Now it seems like there is more to the story.

Meng Jingzhou waved his hand dismissively. “They’re all trivial matters not worth mentioning. There are too many to count.”

Lu Yang felt that the day Meng Jingzhou returned home seemed endlessly far off.

~~~

After school, Tao Tingfeng jogged to a large shop. A long queue had formed at the entrance, and people wore excited smiles.

A wooden sign was propped at the shop entrance. It read: Longevity Affinity.

“What kind of place is this?” The Chess-Observing True Lord frowned. He had no memory of such a place. Is it some new popular plaything among mortals?

“Dreamlike Bubble Mirage! True Lord, have you not heard of it?” Tao Tingfeng stared at the Chess-Obsering True Lord in utter shock. There’s still someone who doesn’t know about the Dreamlike Bubble Mirage?

“Dreamlike Bubble Mirage?” The Chess-Observing True Lord rummaged through his memories but indeed had no such recollection.

“It’s said to be created by a mighty expert from the Dao-Seeking Sect. It lets you enter an illusory domain and experience a different life.”

The Chess-Observing True Lord sneered. I’m proficient in all hundred cultivation arts; I can grasp this thing’s principle just from the description. “I thought it was something special. So it’s just an illusion. A frivolous trick, a mere plaything.”

“The Dreamlike Bubble Mirage isn’t a mere plaything! It’s very popular! The entire continent watches it,” Tao Tingfeng corrected him as he paid for a ticket.

The shop’s interior and walls were set up with arrays that required activation with the ticket.

“Wait, you’re saying the entire Great Xia has this thing?” The Chess-Observing True Lord seemed to have stumbled upon an astonishing fact.

“That’s right, and every shop has this many people.” Tao Tingfeng pointed at the sea of heads inside the shop.

The Chess-Observing True Lord’s heart trembled slightly. The ticket price Tao Tingfeng paid, multiplied by the number of people in the shop, multiplied by the number of shops across the continent...

With a rough estimate, that could earn more spirit stones in four months than I had in my entire lifetime!

Just how many spirit stones has the creator of the Dreamlike Bubble Mirage amassed by now?

I’m afraid it’s enough to buy the lives of several Fusion cultivators!

The Chess-Observing True Lord shivered, wishing he could reverse time back to the Great Qian era and use this method to make money.

If I had this many spirit stones back then, I would have broken through to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage long ago! Why would I have needed to slumber until now, having to rob and getting hunted down?

Tao Tingfeng tore the ticket, and the array under his feet activated. His consciousness emptied as he entered the illusory domain.

The first thing he saw was a sunny, handsome cultivator holding a barbeque skewer in his left hand and another in his right. Someone beside him was grilling more skewers. The cultivator ate one skewer, and the view zoomed in, clearly showing the barbeque skewer bursting with juices.

The cultivator’s mouth glistened with oil. He let out an exaggerated “Wow!” and gave a thumbs-up. “One More Time Barbeque Shop, so delicious!”

The Chess-Observing True Lord, “...”

What exactly is this nonsense?

Longevity Affinity officially began.

The story’s male lead was a disciple of a major sect. He had a childhood sweetheart junior sister and met another junior sister from a different sect during a mission. Coincidentally, both junior sisters fell for the male disciple.

The plot revolved around these three. After a series of trials, the male disciple finally recognized his true feelings. He rescued his childhood sweetheart from a horde of demons and devils and confessed his love. The childhood sweetheart accepted his confession with tears in her eyes. The two went on to enjoy blissful, long lives together.

The end.

After watching the Dreamlike Bubble Mirage, Tao Feng felt a craving. “Let’s go eat barbeque skewers.”

The Chess-Observing True Lord turned his nose up at Tao Tingfeng’s behavior. “Indulging in desires of the palate makes it difficult to attain the Great Dao.”

On the way to the barbeque shop, they passed by the Luodi Merchant Guild. A display stand at the entrance featured the latest flying carriage models. Tao Tingfeng could only gaze at them enviously; he couldn’t afford them.

The Chess-Observing True Lord also gazed at them enviously. The profit margin on these “flying carriages” is extremely high; my eyes are red with envy.

They’re clearly simple things. Why hadn’t I thought of them during the Great Qian era?!

Oh right, inventing these things in Great Qian would have been useless; they didn’t protect intellectual property.

One More Time Barbeque Shop was as popular as ever. Rumor had it that even the Divine Transfiguration expert who recently cleared the mountain of demons had visited.

The Chess-Observing True Lord’s eyes grew even redder with envy.

He secretly resolved to steal the barbeque shop’s secret recipe once his cultivation was restored!

“How’s the observation going? What kind of person is this Chess-Observing True Lord?” Meng Jingzhou asked Lu Yang. He couldn’t see into Tao Tingfeng’s mental space.

Lu Yang mulled over it for a moment and replied, “A pauper.”

Chapter 709: The Chess-Observing True Lord’s Pursuers

While Tao Tingfeng was eating his barbeque skewers, he happened to see a youth around his age enter the barbeque shop. The youth was filthy, his clothes ragged, like a street beggar.

“Shopkeeper, are you still hiring here?” the grimy boy asked. “I'm not asking for much, just the minimum wage will do.” Seeing how business was booming, the youth figured they must be short-handed. This was his chance.

“Shoo, shoo! Where did this little beggar come from? We’re not hiring.” The shopkeeper chased the boy away. After all, this place was a barbeque shop on the surface but a Nine-Netherworlds Creed base in secret; they couldn’t hire outsiders.

“I’m not a beggar!” the youth retorted angrily.

Do you know what status I have? If not for being down on my luck and getting robbed by scoundrels, how could I have been reduced to this plight, to the point of being mistaken for a beggar?

This is absolutely humiliating!

The shopkeeper had no intention of listening further. He directly grabbed the boy by the collar and dragged him out.

“Out you go.”

The filthy youth reached into his pocket. He only had sufficient money for lodging now, insufficient to take a flying vessel or carriage to his destination.

He sighed. The most urgent matter now is to find a job quickly.

Tao Tingfeng didn’t pay much attention to the youth and continued focusing on eating his barbeque skewers.

Time flew by, and another half a month passed. Tao Tingfeng’s performance in the clan academy became increasingly outstanding. He could answer all his clan uncle’s questions in class and even scored full marks in the semi-annual examinations, earning everyone's admiration.

Previously, Tao Tingfeng’s academic performance was at best above average. But with the Chess-Observing True Lord’s assistance, his perspective and knowledge had improved tremendously. The content his clan uncle taught in class was now mere beginner's knowledge to him.

“Elder cousin brother,[1] you’re so amazing!”

After class, the Tao Family descendants often gathered around Tao Tingfeng, casting envious looks his way. Tao Tingfeng would curve his lips into a humble smile, saying it was all luck and he wouldn’t perform as well next time.

The Tao Family disciples who had previously outperformed him looked at him with jealousy. So what if you have good grades? The most important thing in cultivation isn’t knowledge but bone foundation!

The Chess-Observing True Lord also slowly recovered from his soul injuries during this time. However, his recovery was extremely slow. From meeting Tao Tingfeng until now, over a month had passed, yet he had only progressed from gasping out words to being able to speak properly.

In truth, this was the normal recovery speed for cultivators.

Someone like the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was one of a kind in the cultivation world.

Even the Four Ancient Immortals couldn’t achieve her level of liveliness.

“True Lord, can my bone foundation really be changed by the Golden Cicada Shell?” Tao Tingfeng was the most concerned about this issue now.

The day for the clan’s bone foundation test was approaching. He had already found out his spirit root from the Chess-Observing True Lord in advance.

Wood, Fire, Earth Spirit Roots—Triple Spirit Root.

The past him would have him overjoyed; it was undoubtedly the best bone foundation in the clan.

But it was different now. After getting to know the Chess-Observing True Lord, his horizons had broadened. He didn’t want to be confined to the small Tao Family anymore.

A Triple Spirit Root was far from enough.

“Of course, it can.” In the mental space, next to the Chess-Observing True Lord was the Golden Cicada Shell, already merged with Tao Tingfeng.

The Chess-Observing True Lord said proudly, “This Golden Cicada Shell is a relic left by an ancient gold cicada that cultivated to the Apex Transcendent Tribulation Stage. If not for misfortune befalling that Golden Cicada old ancestor, he might have been able to advance a step further, becoming a legendary half-immortal!

“The Golden Cicada Shell is enough to transform your Triple Spirit Root into a Single Spirit Root! Even granting you an immortal physique is possible.”

Tao Tingfeng’s eyes shone with excitement at the thought of joining one of the Five Great Immortal Sects with a Single Spirit Root. My future is destined to be boundless!

“However, if you join an immortal sect, remember to conceal your spirit root,” the Chess-Observing True Lord warned.

“Why is that?” Tao Tingfeng was puzzled.

The Chess-Observing True Lord was disappointed in him. “This is called ‘concealing one’s abilities.’ As the saying goes, ‘the wind will destroy the tallest tree in the forest.’ As someone with a Single Spirit Root joining the sect, you will inevitably attract jealousy from your fellow disciples.

“You must understand, the larger the sect, the more severe the factionalism. Take the Dao-Seeking Sect, for example. With your Single Spirit Root, you will not only face suppression from senior and junior brothers, but even the elders may make a move on you!”

“Th-then what should I do?”

The Chess-Observing True Lord said confidently, “Easy. The Golden Cicada Shell can mask your spirit root. Unless a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator personally investigates, no one can see through your true bone foundation.”

Only then did Tao Tingfeng exhale a sigh of relief.

He then remembered another question. “By the way, True Lord, you previously mentioned that you were hunted down and ended up like this. Who was pursuing you?”

“You don’t even have cultivation yet. Don’t worry about these matters; they’re too distant for you. Just remember to hide my existence and don’t let outsiders know.”

“Alright.” Tao Tingfeng would have done so even without the reminder.

Lu Yang heard the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s warning while watching from the shadows.

“Three Fusion cultivators are rapidly approaching this area, and their foundations are solid.”

“What?!” Lu Yang jumped in fright. Could it be that the Chess-Observing True Lord’s enemies have caught up?

The Chess-Observing True Lord had stolen the Golden Cicada Shell from a Great Yu cultivator and killed two companions who succumbed to their avarice. Be it for wealth or revenge, they would come for him.

“Should we summon Big Senior Sister?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy waved her hand. “Nothing will happen. Just watch.”

The three Fusion cultivators flew at incredible speed. Everyone in Yanshan City saw them.

The three landed on Mount Yan, finding the spot where the Chess-Observing True Lord had fallen back then.

The leader picked up an exquisitely crafted wooden box from the ground, the very one that had contained the Golden Cicada Shell. He calculated with his fingers, then sharply turned his head toward Yanshan City at the foot of the mountain.

“Found you!”

Color drained from the Chess-Observing True Lord when he saw the three Fusion cultivators flying again. “Kid, run! My pursuers are here!”

“Run...run where?”

“Don’t worry about where, just run first!”

Following the Chess-Observing True Lord’s instruction, Tao Tingfeng couldn’t care about packing his things, getting up to run out the door.

A terrifying aura enveloped him, making him feel like he was plunged into endless darkness. Even the Chess-Observing True Lord in his mental space was too frightened to move.

“Kid, let me ask you—is there another soul entity inside your body, or have you seen anything resembling a golden cicada?”

“No...not at all.” Tao Tingfeng forced himself to maintain composure and managed a weak smile.

The leader knitted his brows, not exactly satisfied with the answer, but stopped deliberately releasing the terrifying aura waves. “KId, are you telling the truth?”

“It’s the truth.” Freed from the terrifying aura, Tao Tingfeng gasped for air.

He finally dared to look at their visitors—three unfamiliar cultivators who were undoubtedly powerful.

The leader looked at Tao Tingfeng and sighed before saying solemnly, “We three are members of the Luoshui Guard. Chess-Observing True Lord, we are now officially notifying you that you are under arrest for the robbery of a Golden Cicada Shell from a Great Yu cultivator.”

The leader turned his gaze to Tao Tingfeng. “As for you, you are also under arrest for concealing proceeds of crime and harboring a criminal suspect.”

The Luoshui Guard was Great Xia’s special force responsible for dealing with diabolic creeds, evil cultivators who bullied others, and archaic cultivators who broke the law.

Both Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou recognized the leader. It was Yu Qian, a friend of the Fifth Elder and one of the Luoshui Guard Nine Palaces, who had taken part in multiple arrests of Fifth Elder for speeding.

1. To be more specific, this is an older cousin from the father’s side. ☜

Chapter 710: Surging Waters Flooded the Dragon King Temple—Mistaking Allies for Foes

“Luoshui Guard?” Tao Tingfeng was dumbfounded. He had heard his clan uncle mention this organization. It was established by the imperial court specifically to deal with high-level cultivators.

He had listened to it as an amusing story, never expecting the real deal to come knocking on his door.

Yu Qian and the other two simultaneously produced command tokens engraved with the characters for “Luoshui.”

“Concealing proceeds of crime? Me?” Tao Tingfeng usually didn’t pay much attention to criminal law, forgetting whatever he heard. How could I have imagined I’d break the law when I’ve just been going about my life?

Yu Qian’s eyes narrowed slightly as they bore into Tao Tingfeng. “Tell me, how did you meet the Chess-Observing True Lord back then, and how did you make the Golden Cicada Shell recognize you as its master?”

This was a secret spell of the Luoshui Guard. If the gap in cultivation realm was large enough, they could determine if the other party was lying.

Shi Huagu also had a similar secret spell, which he had used when testing if Lu Yang was from the Heavenly Court Creed. However, the effectiveness of Shi Huagu’s version was inferior to the Luoshui Guard’s.

Bracing himself, Tao Tingfeng truthfully recounted the situation back then. “At the time, the Chess-Observing True Lord told me that this item is called the Golden Cicada Shell and that he had seized it from a formidable opponent, asking me to safeguard it...

“I thought the True Lord was dead, so I tried to make the Golden Cicada Shell recognize me as its master by dripping my blood...

“Later, it turned out the True Lord was alive...”

After listening, Yu Qian’s brows were slightly scrunched up as he asked sternly, “In other words, you knew he had stolen the Golden Cicada Shell but still chose to safeguard it?

“And after the Chess-Observing True Lord entered your mental space, you provided him a place to recover?

“This is utterly reckless! Do you have any idea how dangerous your actions were?

“Do you know what the Golden Cicada Shell is? It’s something that tempts even Transcendent Tribulation cultivators. The Chess-Observing True Lord risked his life to steal it. Yet after making the Golden Cicada Shell recognize you as its master, you dared to harbor him?

“If he had recovered his body, the first thing he would have done was take over your body! Did you think he was teaching you cultivation out of the kindness of his heart?”

Yu Qian took out a book documenting the deeds of Great Qian’s Fusion cultivators and read aloud.

“Chess-Observing True Lord, real name Du Guan, born in the 82,281st year of the Great Qian calendar. To advance to the Nascent Soul Stage, he sacrificed the village that raised him. At the Divine Transfiguration Stage, he became Dao partners with a cultivator at the same realm, then killed that Dao partner to prove his Emotionless Dao. At the Basic Fusion Stage, he committed three recorded cases of murder for money. At the Intermediate Fusion Stage... Later, having no hope of breaking through to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage, he focused on studying the hundred cultivation arts.

Yu Qian closed the book and questioned seriously, “And you were helping this kind of person and cultivating under his guidance?”

“I...I...I felt that he was quite affable, so I thought he was a good person...”

Yu Qian interrupted Tao Tingfeng’s defense. “By ‘good person,’ are you referring to him robbing the Golden Cicada Shell?”

“Hehe, Great Xia cultivators, I never imagined you would have investigated me so thoroughly.” The Chess-Observing True Lord chuckled sinisterly.

“Du Guan, the crimes you committed during the Great Qian era are historical issues; they don’t fall under Great Xia’s jurisdiction. But robbing a Great Yu cultivator within Great Xia territory constitutes the crime of robbery.”

“Not the crime of murder?” The Chess-Observing True Lord knew that falling into Great Xia’s hands meant certain death. After all, my crimes went beyond just robbery.

“Murder? You mean killing the Great Yu cultivator? Unfortunately, he didn’t die. We just haven’t located him yet. As for the two companions you killed, that was considered self-defense and does not constitute a crime.”

The commotion from the Chess-Observing True Lord’s internal conflict with his two companions was too huge, attracting the imperial court’s attention. When they arrived, the Chess-Observing True Lord had just fled, leaving one companion dead and the other severely injured.

The severely injured one was beyond saving. The Luoshui Guard performed an emergency soul search on him, learning the entire sequence of events.

The identity of the robbed Great Yu cultivator was unknown. They only knew he had recently awakened and was still recovering. The Chess-Observing True Lord had learned of the news somewhere and teamed up with two companions to rob him.

After the Chess-Observing True Lord escaped, the severely injured companion saw that the Great Yu cultivator was also gravely wounded but still had some strength left. The latter dispersed his cultivation to cultivate anew and fled, leading to the subsequent sequence of events.

They were also searching for that Great Yu cultivator since they needed to find the victim. That Great Yu cultivator had fled north, while the Chess-Observing True Lord fled south, so the Luoshui Guard split into two teams.

Yu Qian hadn’t expected himself to find the Chess-Observing True Lord before locating the victim.

He said sternly to Tao Tingfeng, “Whether you are guilty of harboring a criminal requires further investigation. But you are suspected of concealing the proceeds of crime and need to make a trip with us.”

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou sighed inwardly. When they saw Tao Tingfeng drip blood on the Golden Cicada Shell to make it recognize him as its master, they knew he was in trouble. They had continued observing to see if he would realize the problem.

Now that things had reached this point, further observation was unnecessary.

“Let’s go. This isn’t over yet.”

~~~

Huff, huff...

The grimy youth who had previously appeared at the barbeque shop was desperately running toward the city outskirts.

For the past half a month, he had been working odd jobs in the city, saving up to buy a set of clean clothes for himself. In another half a month, he would have enough to board a flying vessel to his destination.

“I wonder if those three Great Xia cultivators are here to catch me. To be safe, I’ll run first.”

The youth felt incredibly unlucky. I hadn’t provoked anyone. It wasn’t long after I awakened from my slumber since the Great Yu era that three Great Qian cultivators showed up to rob me of the Golden Cicada Shell.

This is my trump card for the upcoming Battle of the Great Era! How could I just hand it over to others?

After the battle, he didn’t only lose the Golden Cicada Shell but was also forced to disperse his cultivation to cultivate anew so as to save his life.

“Unlucky!”

Suddenly, he stopped in his tracks.

“Kid, you run pretty fast.”

Two figures blocked his way like a wall.

It was Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou.

Back at the barbeque shop, they had noticed something amiss with the youth—his gait and breathing pattern were unlike those of an ordinary person; he definitely had a foundation in cultivation.

At that time, they suspected the youth had dispersed his cultivation to cultivate anew but lacked evidence.

This kid had run the moment the Luoshui Guard arrived. He must be a reforged cultivator!

Meritorious achievements delivered to our doorstep! Let’s see if Senior Brother Dai will still say we only cause trouble when we go out!

“What do you want?!” The youth could tell at a glance that the two were cultivators. I’m a mortal now; there’s no way I could win.

“What do we want?” Meng Jingzhou sneered, flexing his muscles as he dragged the youth into a deserted courtyard. “Talk! Are you an archaic cultivator who dispersed his cultivation to cultivate anew!”

“N-no, I’m not!” the boy yelled, bracing himself.

“Oho, still denying it? String him up!” Lu Yang pulled out a whip from his identity jade tablet and gave it a couple of firm tugs to check its sturdiness. This was an interrogation method he had learned from Yun Zhi.

Meng Jingzhou tactfully found some rope and tied the youth up, hanging him from a tree.

The air crackled with resounding pops, making the youth’s scalp tingle. Seeing their fiendish expressions, he feared for his life if he didn’t confess.

“Don’t hit me, don’t hit me! I’ll confess.”

“Speak! Which era are you from?! What’s your name?!”

“I am a cultivator from the Great Yu era. My Daoist title is ‘Innate Daoist Priest.’”

Chapter 711: Truly Two Good Kids

Hearing the youth announce his identity, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou were both stunned, involuntarily taking two steps back with a dreadful sense of impending doom.

Innate Daoist Priest?

The Founding Ancestor?

Lu Yang was the first to regain his composure. He cracked the whip in his hand loudly. Sparks flew from its tip, frightening the youth until he trembled. Lu Yang smirked menacingly. “Audacious! How dare you impersonate the senior I admire most! Let me ask you, what is the Innate Daoist Priest’s real name?”

“Qi Tongtian.”

“How did the Dao-Seeking Sect get its name?”

“I spent a hundred thousand spirit stones to ask someone from the Heaven Strategy Sect to calculate the location with the best feng shui to build the sect. After learning the results, I set off but got lost halfway. I had no choice but to ask an old farmer by the roadside for directions. To commemorate this experience and thank the old farmer, I named the sect the ‘Dao-Seeking Sect.’”

“How many wives did the Innate Daoist Priest have?”

“When did I ever take a wife?”

“Why didn’t you take a wife?”

“Poor. No spirit stones. All the spirit stones were used to build the sect.”

The youth’s feet were tied as he hung from the tree. A slight breeze was enough to make him spin.

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou exchanged a glance. Oh no. He answered everything correctly. It seems he really is the Innate Daoist Priest.

Lu Yang cleared his throat and plastered on a smile as he hastily lowered the upside-down Innate Daoist Priest. “The Innate Daoist Priest is the person I respect most. When I encounter difficulties in cultivation, I often recall how you established the Dao-Seeking Sect under such arduous circumstances. It truly inspires me. I thought you were an imposter just now. Please forgive me, Founding Ancestor.”

The Innate Daoist Priest was merely a mortal now. Having been hung upside down for a while, he felt dizzy once his feet touched the ground and didn’t immediately process Lu Yang’s words.

Meng Jingzhou tactfully found a chair from somewhere and invited the founding ancestor to sit.

The Innate Daoist Priest thanked them and sat on the chair for a while to recover, then suddenly realized they had addressed him as “Founding Ancestor.”

“Wait, you two are from the Dao-Seeking Sect?”

The two bowed and nodded, behaving as deferentially as they could. “My name is Lu Yang. You can just call me Little Lu.”

“My name is Meng Jingzhou. You can just call me Little Meng.”

The Innate Daoist Priest looked at the two with a peculiar expression, recalling the stories he had heard by the roadside.

“So you’re the Lu Yang who challenged higher levels at the Foundation Establishment Stage, defeating Golden Core, Nascent Soul, and Divine Transfiguration cultivators?

“And you’re the Meng Jingzhou who has a steadfast Dao heart and remains unflustered despite beauties in his embrace, wholly devoted to the Dao?”

“Founding Ancestor, you must be tired after being hung from the tree. Let me massage your shoulders.”

“Let me massage your legs.”

As they massaged the Founding Ancestor, they chatted casually. “Founding Ancestor, weren’t you the one who found the Dao-Seeking Sect? Why didn’t you slumber within the sect?”

The sect had a tomb for the Innate Daoist Priest. No one knew he had faked his death and that his true body was elsewhere.

The Innate Daoist Priest felt like crying but had no tears. “I also never expected the sect I founded back then to last until now.”

When he established the Dao-Seeking Sect, he was only at the Void Refinement Stage. He advanced to the Fusion Stage after the sect was built. It was just an ordinary first-class sect. Who could have imagined a first-class sect would survive for 120,000 years and even thrive as time passed?

The ethos of the Great Yu era was terrible. If a sect fell, enemies would dig three feet underground, not just to search for treasures but to eradicate them by the root. If he had chosen to slumber in the Dao-Seeking Sect, and the sect was destroyed one day, he would be killed by enemies in his sleep.

Had I known the Dao-Seeking Sect would do so well, why would I have wasted so much energy to find a secret place to slumber back then?

“Then why did you disperse your cultivation to cultivate anew?”

The Innate Daoist Priest felt even more wronged. “Do you think I wanted to? I had just woken up and wasn’t fully recovered when three Great Qian cultivators burst in to rob my Golden Cicada Shell. The leader was called ‘Chess-Observing True Lord’ or something. Oh boy, those three were ruthless. If I hadn’t gambled by dispersing my cultivation to cultivate anew and escaping, my life would have ended there.”

Lu Yang’s mouth twitched. So you were the victim of the Chess-Observing True Lord’s robbery.

Meng Jingzhou said indignantly, “They’re too much! That Chess-Observing True Lord is really lawless, utterly disregarding our Dao-Seeking Sect!”

Lu Yang was even more furious. “How dare he treat our Founding Ancestor like this! If I run into him, I’d rather throw away this worthless life of mine than let him get away with it!”

The Innate Daoist Priest was deeply moved. Truly two good kids.

He continued, “After escaping, I heard the Dao-Seeking Sect still existed and had become one of the Five Great Immortals. I wanted to head there, but it’s too far from here. I needed to earn enough travel expenses first.

“Well, before I could earn enough, Great Xia’s official cultivators came pursuing me. I was about to run when you two blocked me and strung me up here.”

“What did you do? Why did you have to run at the first sight of Great Xia cultivators?” Lu Yang massaged the Innate Daoist Priest’s shoulders even more attentively.

The Innate Daoist Priest’s visage was plagued with worry. “I had to run even if I didn’t do anything. I’m not a cultivator from this era. The Great Xia official cultivators would definitely arrest me if they saw me. I figured the Dao-Seeking Sect would be safer.”

Lu Yang finally understood. The Founding Ancestor has just awakened and doesn’t know about Great Xia, judging Great Xia by the standards of the Great Yu authorities.

Great Xia didn’t arrest all archaic cultivators. For those willing to follow Great Xia’s rules, Great Xia would at most register them and wouldn’t do anything to them.

As for victims like the Founding Ancestor, they will be protected.

The Innate Daoist Priest sighed. “What a pity about my Golden Cicada Shell.”

“How did the Chess-Observing True Lord and the other two cultivators find out that you had the Golden Cicada Shell?” Meng Jingzhou asked curiously.

The Innate Daoist Priest seemed to remember something. He hammered his thigh and said furiously, “It must have been that Great Yu Alliance bunch.”

“Great Yu Alliance?” Lu Yang had a recollection of Wu Youdao mentioning this organization.

“An alliance formed by a group of Great Yu cultivators. After I awoke, they located me right away and hoped I’d join them. I thought they seemed unreliable and rejected them.

“They must have discovered I possessed the Golden Cicada Shell, but it was inconvenient for them to act directly without breaking their rules. Thus, they secretly informed the Great Qian cultivators and had them rob me, planning to snatch it back themselves afterward. That would make it legitimate.

“I reckon they didn’t expect the Great Xia cultivators to arrive so quickly. They didn’t dare act openly and had to give up.”

Lu Yang patted his chest in assurance. “Don’t worry, Founding Ancestor. If we ever bump into that Great Yu Alliance bunch, our Dao-Seeking Sect will definitely help you seek redress and reclaim your dignity!”

The Innate Daoist Priest thought, These two are truly filial, and their talent is also high. They are indeed as described in the storytelling tales—rare, excellent seedlings.

With these two around, the future of the Dao-Seeking Sect is vast. They will surely have a place in the upcoming Battle of the Great Era.

“By the way, Founding Ancestor, our mission outside is over, and we’re returning to the sect. Would you like to come back with us?”

“Absolutely.”

Chapter 712: Senior Brother Dai, Guess Who This Is

The old horse watched with slight astonishment as the youth boarded the carriage, wondering who this person was and why Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou were bringing him back to the sect.

Is he a promising seedling they just discovered?

But even then, he’ll need to pass the entrance trials before he can join the Dao-Seeking Sect.

Forget it, what does it have to do with me? I’m just responsible for pulling the carriage.

The old horse stopped dwelling on the matter and focused on his duty of pulling the carriage.

“Founding Ancestor, rest assured, we will definitely retrieve the Golden Cicada Shell for you. We just received news that the Luoshui Guard, the official cultivators of Great Xia, have captured the Chess-Observing True Lord.

“So fast?” The Innate Daoist Priest was greatly surprised. How did you two find out?

“However, matters like handling stolen goods are best handled by senior sect members. We juniors carry little weight, and it wouldn’t be appropriate for us to intervene.”

The Innate Daoist Priest nodded. That is true.

“Founding Ancestor, you might not be fully aware, but the sect’s ethos is quite different from your time. It’s now more open. Currently, the sect is managed not only by the elders but also by several disciples.”

~~~

The old horse transported the three back to the Dao-Seeking Sect in just a single day, a feat that astounded the Innate Daoist Priest. Even if I were traveling at his maximum speed, it would have been around the same pace.

Oh wait, no... Given my tendency to get lost, even ten days might not be enough for me to reach the Dao-Seeking Sect. This is why I was working hard to save money to board a flying vessel.

However, he hadn’t considered that he was now a person without a registered identity and thus ineligible to board a flying vessel.

With the return of some fellow disciples from their missions, the Dao-Seeking Sect was livelier than when the two had left, though it had not yet returned to its usual bustling state, for some people were still carrying out their character observation missions.

“Whoa, the Dao-Seeking Sect is this big now?” the Innate Daoist Priest exclaimed in awe. Leaving aside how much the sect has expanded since its founding, even this mountain gate is far more imposing than before.

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou led the Innate Daoist Priest to the entrance of the Great Mission Hall. “Founding Ancestor, please wait here for a moment.
