I believe you understand that your identity is special. We’re afraid the higher-ups of the sect won’t be able to accept your sudden appearance if we bring you directly to them.

“How about this? We two will go in first to explain the entire situation, and then you can enter.”

“Alright, I'll follow your arrangement,” the Innate Daoist Priest replied with a cheerful laugh. This matter indeed requires a process of acceptance.

~~~

Dai Bufan had a thick stack of mission reports placed before him, each detailing the character assessments of their targets.

The mortals requiring observation had all been screened by him prior, and the results proved his judgment was sound—the majority met the Dao-Seeking Sect’s standards.

“This boy who visited his family in prison is not bad—quite filial. I wonder if he’ll come to the Dao-Seeking Sect.

“This girl isn’t bad either. She happened to find a storage ring and used it for farming—quite clever. It’s just that her family environment isn’t ideal.

“I wonder how those two rascals, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou, are doing,” Dai Bufan mumbled to himself. He felt a sense of trepidation, worried that this duo might have cooked up some new trouble.

“It should be fine. I haven’t received any intelligence about Transcendent Tribulation battles breaking out anywhere.”

A faint smile tugged at the corner of Dai Bufan’s lips. After all these recent experiences, he had mentally prepared himself. Even if those two cause trouble that leads to battles involving Transcendent Tribulation cultivators or half-immortals, or bring back an ancient half-immortal or two, I won’t be overly shocked.

Just as Dai Bufan was ruminating, he heard a polite knock on the door. “Senior Brother Dai, we’re back.”

“Come in.”

The wooden door opened. Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou were in high spirits as they strode in.

“Have you finished your observations?”

“Yes, they’re done.”

“Tell me, what were the three people I assigned you to observe like? Did their characters pass muster?”

The two shook their heads regretfully. “Only one of the three had passed.”

“Only one?” Dai Bufan furrowed his brow slightly, somewhat puzzled. Was my judgment that poor?

“For example, that mortal named Xie An was actually the Wuji Supreme Lord Xie Jiu in disguise! Despite being a mighty expert, he pretended to be a mortal—truly shameless!”

“Oh, there was such a thing?” Dai Bufan was slightly taken aback. I didn’t expect these two to be so unlucky as to run into a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator disguised as a mortal.

Could it be that his Dao heart hasn’t recovered after he was dealt with by Senior Sister Yun last time?

“What about the one named Tao Tingfeng?”

Meng Jingzhou shook his head, answering regretfully, “Tao Tingfeng won’t do either. This brat has no respect for the law, openly violating the penal code, harboring a robber, and helping to safeguard stolen goods. When we left, he was taken away by the Luoshui Guard.”

“So the only one whose character passed is Gu Junye?”

“That’s right. This Gu Junye is an exceptionally rare, great seedling! Not only does he strictly abide by the law, but he also knows how to use the law as a weapon to protect himself. He studies diligently in class and uses every possible moment outside class to train his body. He is also very filial, obeying his mother.

“Senior Brother Dai, he best fits the criteria you mentioned—being honest and doing one’s part and cultivating steadily and diligently.”

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou lavished praise upon Gu Junye.

“His mentality is also excellent; he remains unruffled in the face of problems. Even when we told him he could participate in the Dao-Seeking Sect’s entrance trials, he didn’t appear overly excited, keeping his composure.

“We also discovered that Gu Junye holds himself to the standard of a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator, bearing the interests of the world at heart. He shared with us multiple times about his aspiration to save all living beings.

“Furthermore, he doesn’t conceal his intentions. He openly declared his ideals to us right in front of his classmates and teacher.”

Dai Bufan nodded. “With such character, he truly is a rare, great seedling.”

“By the way, Senior Brother Dai, didn’t you say that if we find someone not on the list who also meets the sect’s recruitment criteria, we could recommend them to you?”

“I did say that? Did you find someone?”

“This person could be called an unexpected gain from this trip. It’s just that his background is a bit complicated. He’s a Great Yu cultivator, but for certain reasons, he dispersed his cultivation to cultivate anew.”

Lu Yang vouched with confidence. “But rest assured, Senior Brother Dai, his character is guaranteed. He absolutely meets our Dao-Seeking Sect’s recruitment standards! And he’s renowned—you’re sure to recognize him, Senior Brother Dai.”

“A Great Yu reforged cultivator?” Dai Bufan hesitated slightly, finding the decision tricky. You two really know how to pick a person. If one isn’t careful, someone like this may likely be a traitor.

“We were afraid you would be concerned, Senior Brother Dai, so we specifically brought him back to the sect.”

“Then bring him in for me to see.”

“Roger.”

Soon, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou brought a youth with delicate and handsome features. The youth stood before Dai Bufan, smiling somewhat abashedly.

“Senior Brother Dai, guess who this is?”

“Who?”

Lu Yang introduced the youth jubilantly, “This is the Founding Ancestor of our Dao-Seeking Sect—the Innate Daoist Priest, Qi Tongtian!”

Dai Bufan’s eyes rolled back into his head. With a loud thud, he collapsed to the floor and fell unconscious.

“Wh-what’s wrong with him?” The Innate Daoist Priest panicked a little.

Meng Jingzhou replied seriously, “His psychological fortitude is probably not up to par. He’s never met you before, Founding Ancestor, so he got too excited.”

Chapter 713: Meeting the Higher-Ups

When Dai Bufan woke up, he saw Lu Yang, Meng Jingzhou, and the Innate Daoist Priest squatting on the floor, their heads nearly touching as they peered down at him. He confirmed that everything that had transpired wasn’t a dream.

“Senior Brother Dai, you’re finally awake.”

“Don’t call me senior brother. I don’t dare to have a junior brother like you.” Dai Bufan got up, fixing the two rascals, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou, with an unamused stare.

I sent you out to select a few disciples, and what did you do? You brought back the Founding Ancestor himself.

Dai Bufan was renowned for his cool-headedness; otherwise, he couldn’t have managed the Great Mission Hall and the vast intelligence network.

But he felt that ever since meeting Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou, his emotions had fluctuated significantly more than before.

Even now, his head was still spinning.

“Here, Senior Brother Dai, let me help you up.” Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou flanked Dai Bufan and hoisted him up by his arms, settling him back into his chair.

“Are you really the legendary Founding Ancestor, the Innate Daoist Priest who got lost?” Dai Bufan still didn’t dare to believe it.

Although Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou had never lied to him before, this matter involved the Founding Ancestor; he couldn’t afford to be mistaken.

After the Innate Daoist Priest dispersed his cultivation to cultivate anew, his appearance changed drastically and no longer matched the statues of the Founding Ancestor preserved within the Dao-Seeking Sect.

The Innate Daoist Priest waved his hand sheepishly. “Calling me ‘legendary’ is an exaggeration. My Daoist title is indeed the ‘Innate Daoist Priest,’ but unfortunately, my proof of identity was destroyed in a recent battle.”

“A recent battle? Then your current cultivation...”

“I lost the fight. My injuries were too severe, so I could only disperse my cultivation to cultivate anew, grasping at a sliver of a chance of survival. My luck wasn’t bad, and I managed to live.”

Dispersing one’s cultivation to start over was never a guaranteed success. To ensure a higher success rate, it was best to do it during one’s peak. For someone like the Innate Daoist Priest who did it while gravely injured, the probability of failure would increase significantly.

“Founding Ancestor, I believe you understand that your identity is special. I cannot make this decision alone.” Dai Bufan was in a tough position. “How about this? I’ll take you to find Senior Sister Yun and let her decide?”

“Alright.” The Innate Daoist Priest was an amenable person.

Dai Bufan deferentially invited the Innate Daoist Priest to Heaven’s Gate Peak to find Yun Zhi. Before leaving, he shot a glare at Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou. “You two, follow us!”

Lu Yang shook his head discreetly. Senior Dai Bufan is really irascible and has a poor temperament. I wonder how he had even managed to cultivate to the Fusion Stage.

In contrast, despite suffering the daily harassment of the Everlasting Immortal Fairy in my mental space, I can still focus on my cultivation. It’s clear who is superior.

~~~

Heaven’s Gate Peak.

Having finished consolidating her cultivation realm, True Lord Gan Tian had also been requested by Dai Bufan to go out on a mission. That left only Yun Zhi at Heaven’s Gate Peak for now.

It was rare for Yun Zhi not to be cultivating. Instead, she sat on a throne, taking small sips of tea.

Four monarch chairs were arranged around a circular stone table, making the table seem out of place.

As she sipped her tea, Yun Zhi contemplated whether she should acquire a matching stone table from somewhere.

“Senior Sister Yun,” Dai Bufan greeted with his hands clasped together.

“Hmm?” Yun Zhi set down her teacup and looked at the four with slight bewilderment.

Junior Brother Dai, Junior Brother Meng, Little Junior Brother, and an unfamiliar youth.

“There is a matter requiring your decision, Senior Sister Yun.” Dai Bufan strained the corners of his mouth, striving to maintain a solemn expression as he explained the youth’s origins.

“In other words, you’re saying that this person is our Founding Ancestor, the Innate Daoist Priest Qi Tongtian?” Yun Zhi was also stunned, not expecting the Founding Ancestor to still be alive.

After a moment of rumination, she asked seriously, “Founding Ancestor, would you like to become the sect leader then?”

“Ah? Me? Become the sect leader?” This time, it was the Innate Daoist Priest’s turn to be stunned.

He had assumed the sects now to be similar to those from the Great Yu era, where individuals would employ unscrupulous methods and stop at nothing to compete for the position of sect leader. He was even worried that upon his return to the Dao-Seeking Sect, the members would be unwilling to have a higher “Grand Emperor”[1] above them , making things difficult for him or even eliminating him.

I never imagined this junior to directly suggest I become the sect leader.

“No no no, this won’t do.” The Innate Daoist Priest waved his hands repeatedly. “Putting aside that I am currently just a mortal, even if I recovered my Fusion Stage cultivation, I wouldn’t have the capability to manage such a massive sect.”

The current scale of the Dao-Seeking Sect is worlds apart from its founding days. How could I possibly manage it?

“It’s fine. Little Junior Brother also served as sect leader for three months. Managing the Dao-Seeking Sect is very easy.”

The Innate Daoist Priest was astonished. Are the standards for becoming sect leader so low now that even a Nascent Soul cultivator can become one?

No, I can’t think of it like that. This junior was able to defeat even Divine Transfiguration cultivators at the Foundation Establishment Stage. Now that he has reached the Nascent Soul Stage, his actual combat prowess may be comparable to that of a Fusion cultivator.

“I really can’t become the sect leader. You don’t need to treat me like this; just consider me an ordinary disciple of the sect,” the Innate Daoist Priest insisted. He only wished to focus on his cultivation, leave his past behind, and return to the Fusion Stage.

“By the way, Big Senior Sister, the Founding Ancestor’s Golden Cicada Shell is currently in the hands of the imperial court. Do you think you could help ask for it back?” Lu Yang seized the opportunity to add.

“What’s the situation with the Golden Cicada Shell?”

Lu Yang recounted the Innate Daoist Priest’s experiences after waking up, naturally omitting the part where he and Meng Jingzhou had strung the Founding Ancestor up.

I presume this memory isn’t particularly pleasant for the Founding Ancestor, so I shall refrain from mentioning it here.

Yun Zhi nodded. “So that’s how it is. This matter isn’t difficult.” She turned to the Innate Daoist Priest. “Founding Ancestor, would you like to meet our sect’s higher-ups?”

The Founding Ancestor being alive is a major matter; it’s only right to inform the sect’s higher-ups.

The Innate Daoist Priest agreed readily. It’s good to meet the sect’s outstanding younger generation.

~~~

Soon, the eight elders of the Dao-Seeking Sect gathered in the Discussion Hall, with the exception of the indescribably beautiful Sixth Elder. If her true form attended, its aura might suffocate the Innate Daoist Priest to death, so only her projection was present.

The eight elders were truly figures who had weathered all kinds of situations. Not only were their cultivation levels higher than Dai Bufan’s, but even their ability to accept the unexpected outstripped his.

“So this is our Founding Ancestor?”

“So young.”

“He doesn’t look like the statues.”

“Nonsense. After dispersing his cultivation to cultivate anew, how could he look the same?”

“Should we replace the set of Founding Ancestor statues? They look quite old.”

“Big Brother, look at you, digging graves all day and never digging up the Founding Ancestor. Now look at Little Lu and Little Meng—they found him just by going out.”

“Who’s digging graves? That’s called observational studies. Even the tomb owners tacitly permit it.”

“If the tomb owners could speak, it would be you, Big Brother, lying in the coffin.”

Suddenly, Eighth Elder seemed to recall something and quietly sidled up to the Innate Daoist Priest, asking softly, “By the way, Founding Ancestor, do you still accept disciples?”

“Ah?” Before the Innate Daoist Priest could react, Eighth Elder began promoting himself zealously.

“Founding Ancestor, don’t just look at my low ranking among the elders—that’s simply because I joined the sect late. In any case, I am a Fusion expert now, and I’m proficient in the Dao of Talismans. All you need to do is nod, and you can immediately gain a disciple already at the Advanced Fusion Stage while skipping the teaching process.

“What do you think of me?”

1. The “Grand Emperor” is an emperor that has abdicated in favor or a successor. Usually, there is a change in the emperor when the reigning emperor dies, but there are cases where the emperor retires early and appoints the next emperor. The few times it happened, most weren't out of their own volition. ☜

Chapter 714: After Slumbering for 120,000 Years, My Sect Has Become the Number One Major Sect

The Innate Daoist Priest hesitantly pointed behind Eighth Elder as a kind reminder. “Let’s put aside whatever thoughts I may have now; it seems this junior named Yun Zhi doesn’t quite approve of your thoughts.”

Eighth Elder turned his head and saw Yun Zhi, whose countenance was as cold as frost.

Yun Zhi stated icily, “Eighth Elder, wanting to improve is a good thing. I will faithfully relay your thoughts to Grand-Shifu.”

Eighth Elder broke out in a cold sweat. If Shifu learns of this, won’t he lock me up in Incarceration Peak? It’s not like Incarceration Peak has no more space for one more inmate.

“No no no, let’s discuss this properly.“ Eighth Elder switched to an integrating smile.

“Sit back down.”

Eighth Elder hurriedly returned to his seat, sitting upright in an impeccable posture with his chest out and head held high.

The Innate Daoist Priest leaned slightly toward Lu Yang and whispered, “I’ve been wanting to ask, is this junior named Yun Zhi the current sect leader?”

Lu Yang shook his head. “No, but whatever she says, the sect leader generally listens.”

“The sect leader is that obedient?”

“Founding Ancestor, do you know about the current Five Great Immortal Sects in Great Xia?”

“I’ve heard about them from the pingshu storytelling.” He had learned that his own sect had become a top-tier faction from storytellers on the streets.

“Even the sect leaders of the Five Great Immortal Sects combined wouldn’t warrant Big Senior Sister to strike with one hand.”

The Innate Daoist Priest’s pupils widened. Is this junior named Yun Zhi really that powerful?

I’ve heard that the Abbot of the Hanging Monastery is a Transcendent Tribulation expert. Just how formidable is this Yun Zhi’s strength? I’m afraid she’s the most outstanding combatant even among Transcendent Tribulation cultivators.

At the moment, Yun Zhi was recounting the Innate Daoist Priest’s experiences after waking up. When she reached the part where the Chess-Observing True Lord and his two companions tried to seize the Golden Cicada Shell, the elders were filled with righteous indignation, slamming the table in anger.

“How dare they bully our Founding Ancestor? Those Great Qian cultivators are tired of living!”

“Where are they? Let’s go teach them a lesson.”

“They’ve already been captured by the imperial court.”

“Let's break into jail!”

“Yes, yes, let’s break into jail!”

They dare to bully the Founding Ancestor? We must absolutely show those Great Qian cultivators the methods of the Dao-Seeking Sect.

“Stop messing around!” First Elder berated. He was their big brother after all, and the other seven elders quieted down. “We are the brightest and the best from the righteous path! What’s with breaking into jail? Don’t you know how to use your brains and solve this through proper methods?”

“Big Brother, what do you propose?”

“Can’t we just commit a crime ourselves and get locked up with the Chess-Observing True Lord?”

“Right, right! Big Brother’s mind is still the sharpest.”

“It’s a good method.”

The elders jubilantly discussed how to commit crimes. Watching these juniors share criminal techniques so skillfully, the Innate Daoist Priest couldn’t help but feel that this scene didn’t match his impression of a righteous sect.

“Little Meng, our Dao-Seeking Sect is really a righteous sect now, right?”

Meng Jingzhou shook his head steadily. “It depends. We sometimes impersonate a diabolic creed.”

“Ah?”

Noting the elders’ intense discussion, Yun Zhi walked over to the Innate Daoist Priest. “Founding Ancestor, would you still like to meet the other higher-ups?”

“Yes.”

“Very well. Little Junior Brother, Junior Brother Meng, you two follow us. We are going to Incarceration Peak.”

~~~

Incarceration Peak was quite a distance away from the core area of the Dao-Seeking Sect. Since the Innate Daoist Priest was still a mortal, several days wouldn’t be enough if they walked.

Yun Zhi plucked a cloud from the sky and had the three sit upon it, bringing them to Incarceration Peak.

“Where is this place?” The Innate Daoist Priest sensed the Incarceration Peak’s gloomy and frigid atmosphere.

“Incarceration Peak. Our sect wields enforcement authority. Those imprisoned here are usually criminals we encounter who have violated Great Xia’s laws.”

Upon spotting Lu Yang, the criminals confined here had a trace of fear flash past their eyes.

Although this kid’s cultivation is low, isn’t every heavyweight figure imprisoned here connected to him in some way?

Who has he captured this time?

“Ah, Little Yun is here. Little Lu and the Meng boy are here too.” The childlike Grand-Shifu emerged from a room and greeted them with a smile, though he seemed somewhat nervous.

Then, he turned his gaze to the sole stranger in the group and exhaled a sigh of relief. “I thought you had captured another half-immortal. Turns out it’s just a mortal.”

The grand-shifu resumed his normal demeanor, seeming even more relaxed than usual. He opened an empty prison cage and casually said to the Innate Daoist Priest, “Go in yourself.”

Lu Yang coughed. “Ahem, Grand-Shifu, you’ve misunderstood. He isn’t a prisoner.”

“Not a prisoner?” The grand-shifu was bewildered. “Then who is he?”

“The Innate Daoist Priest, Qi Tongtian.”

“...Who?”

“Our Founding Ancestor, the Innate Daoist Priest.”

The grand-shifu’s eyes widened, his pupils reflecting the Innate Daoist Priest’s figure. With his face wreathed in disbelief, he turned his head to look at Yun Zhi for confirmation.

Yun Zhi nodded, indicating that Lu Yang was telling the truth.

The grand-shifu stared at Lu Yang like he had seen a ghost, his astonishment plain on his visage. You kid cause more trouble than Taciturn and the other eight combined! At the same time, he quietly closed the prison cell door, pretending nothing had happened.

Back then, the nine of them had simply messed with their peers; with some effort, I could handle it. But you? Going out and encountering Fusion, Transcendent Tribulation, and half-immortal cultivators is one thing, but now you’ve even unearthed the Founding Ancestor?

“Coincidence, it was all a coincidence.” Lu Yang tried his best to prove his innocence. It wasn’t that I caused trouble but that trouble found me.

“And this is?” The Innate Daoist Priest took the initiative to break the awkward situation.

“The previous sect leader of the Dao-Seeking Sect, Tang Shengyi. His cultivation is at the Transcendent Tribulation Stage.”

“This junior, Tang Shengyi, pays his respects to the Founding Ancestor.” The grand-shifu performed a deep bow.

The Innate Daoist Priest was not accustomed to it and wanted to dodge. It’s my first time having a Transcendent Tribulation expert bow to me.

He felt a bit embarrassed and tried to change the subject. Surveying his surroundings, he asked, “Speaking of which, who are all the people imprisoned here? Would it be convenient to introduce them?”

“Allow this junior to introduce them to you, Founding Ancestor. Most of the criminals locked up in Incarceration Peak are Great Yu cultivators, with a minority being Great Qian cultivators. I captured them all.” The grand-shifu pointed to one of the prison cages. “This one confines the Azure Lightning Venerable Lord.”

The first introduction already shocked the Innate Daoist Priest, who could barely control his voice. “The Azure Lightning Venerable Lord? The Transcendent Tribulation cultivator who commands lightning?”

Legends said the Azure Lightning Venerable Lord was the pinnacle of lightning-spell cultivators in his era, revered by cultivators practicing lightning spells. Even in the Innate Daoist Priest’s era, there were lightning-spell sects that claimed their ancestors had received the true legacy of the Azure Lightning Venerable Lord, a testament to his extensive influence.

“This one confines the Black-White Venerable Lord.”

“The Black-White Venerable Lord? The legends say he was the right-hand man of the second Imperial Preceptor!”

The grand-shifu scratched his head. “Originally, we had captured the second Imperial Preceptor, but there was a bit of an accident in the middle, and he died from a curse backlash.” He hurriedly added, “Although we didn’t capture the second Imperial Preceptor, our sect did capture Wu Youdao.”

“The sixth Yu Emperor, Wu Youdao?!” The Innate Daoist Priest stared at the young man with a monarch’s bearing in the prison cage, feeling an inexplicable astonishment.

This is Wu Youdao, the one with the second highest talent among all Yu emperors! Fortunately, the dynasty has changed. If this were in my era, it would be outright treason.

“These two are the Nightmare Supreme Lord and the Void Emptiness Supreme Lord.” The grand-shifu pointed at two soul entities. “Their physical bodies have already been used as artifact refinement materials.”

Seeing the lack of reaction from the Innate Daoist Priest, the grand-shifu smacked his head. “Oh right, you may not know the Void Emptiness Supreme Lord. He is a half-immortal who vied for supremacy with the Xia Emperor during the late Great Yu era.”

The Innate Daoist Priest had already been rendered speechless and lost the ability to react after the shocking revelations, his eyes turning dull and vacant.

I’ve never heard of the Void Emptiness Supreme Lord, but I know of the Nightmare Supreme Lord, a famous half-immortal. He was once an overlord of the world and the most powerful contender for supremacy at the end of the Great Qian Era. If not for the first Yu Emperor, the Nightmare Supreme Lord would have established a dynasty.

One question after another arose in his mind.

How were these legendary supreme powerhouses captured?

Why does it feel like the Dao-Seeking Sect’s strength is even more exaggerated than the storytellers described?

Just how powerful is this sect I founded?

Chapter 715: The Number One Diabolic Creed Is Also Our Sect

After the Innate Daoist Priest dispersed his cultivation to cultivate anew, he fled to the outside world, where he first encountered the concept of the “Five Great Immortal Sects” and learned that one of them was the sect he himself had founded. This caused him to be dumbstruck for a long while, and he even briefly suspected it was merely a case of identical names.

Only after confirming the location was he convinced that it wasn’t a namesake, but truly the very sect he had established back then.

The outside world spread rumors that each of the Five Great Immortal Sects either had a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator or possessed methods comparable to one. This claim alone had already astonished it.

After all, that is the exalted Transcendent Tribulation Stage.

Now, arriving at Incarceration Peak and seeing the major figures imprisoned here—never mind Transcendent Tribulation cultivators; there are even two half-immortals!

These are legendary half-immortals, cultivators that didn’t even exist in my era.

No matter how I look at it, this Dao-Seeking Sect doesn’t seem like it only has Transcendent Tribulation cultivators!

“Hehe, Qi Tongtian, you founded a great sect.” A sinister chuckle rang out.

The Innate Daoist Priest found it somewhat familiar. He followed the voice and found its owner.

It was a wizened old man. He was hunched over, and his face was wreathed in wrinkles.

“Karmic Fire True Lord?!” The Innate Daoist Priest recognized the wizened old man.

This is a Fusion Stage true lord from my era. Despite committing countless evils, he withstood the scorching of the Red Lotus Karmic Fire for three days, ultimately subduing it and founding the renowned Supreme Karmic Fire Sect.

Although they were both at the Fusion Stage, the Innate Daoist Priest could hardly compare to the Karmic Fire True Lord. The Supreme Karmic Fire Sect was also a key member of the “Diabolic Alliance,” the largest cultivator organization of that time.

Back then, even if I had taken the initiative to greet the Karmic Fire True Lord, he probably wouldn’t have given me a glance.

I didn’t expect that he would have been reduced to a prisoner when we meet again.

“This one was captured by Old Seven when he went out searching for pill-concocting materials,” the Grand-Shifu mentioned, having to think for a moment to recall who the Karmic Fire True Lord was.

“Innate Daoist Priest, I never imagined we’d meet here.” A cold voice sounded from the next cell, belonging to a middle-aged man with a deflated expression.

The Innate Daoist Priest scrutinized him for a while before matching the middle-aged man to the person in his memory. “Are you the Ten Thousand Swords True Lord?”

In his memory, the Ten Thousand Swords True Lord was ostentatiously brilliant with a youthful and spirited demeanor. He was a lone swordsman who acted solely on his whims. If someone provoked him, he would kill them regardless of whether they were righteous or diabolic.

Once, he was dead drunk and accidentally killed the only daughter of a Fusion cultivator. That cultivator was a renowned veteran and an important member of the Diabolic Alliance. Upon learning the news, he flew into a rage and sought to kill the Ten Thousand Swords True Lord for revenge.

To his surprise, the Ten Thousand Swords True Lord pierced his heart with a single sword strike, killing him on the spot.

It was only then that people realized the Ten Thousand Swords True Lord had already cultivated to the Apex Fusion Stage.

He’s been captured too? The Innate Daoist Priest did a double-take.

“Old Nine captured him.” The grand-shifu pouted. He reckoned that the Ten Thousand True Lord’s Dao heart had been shattered after witnessing the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s swordmanship, preventing him from recovering from this setback.

The Innate Daoist Priest was about to say something when he caught sight of a prominent figure who had commanded the wind and rain in his era.

“Blood Devil Venerable Lord?”

This was the Imperial Preceptor in my era. The Yu Emperor was merely a puppet, while he was the true emperor who monopolized power.

He was the one who founded the once-famous Diabolic Alliance!

Lu Yang couldn’t be any more familiar with the Blood Devil Venerable Lord. He and Meng Jingzhou had encountered a group of Great Yu Fusion cultivators in Buyi Town. After capturing them, those Fusion cultivators disclosed the locations of their hidden treasure grottoes. Yun Zhi took Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou there and inadvertently awakened the Blood Devil Venerable Lord, who was slumbering within.

Then, Yun Zhi casually captured him and brought him back.

The Blood Devil Venerable Lord’s eye twitched. He silently turned away, pretending not to know the Innate Daoist Priest.

The Innate Daoist Priest had never imagined that those imprisoned here were either legendary figures or renowned great cultivators from his era.

Is the Dao-Seeking Sect’s feng shui really this good?

Isn’t the one hundred thousand spirit stones I spent back then to have the Heaven Strategy Sect calculate the feng shui too worthwhile?

“Founding Ancestor, this way please. There is another Transcendent Tribulation cultivator in the sect.” Yun Zhi gestured for the Innate Daoist Priest to move along.

As soon as the Innate Daoist Priest arrived at the scripture library, his eyes were dazzled by the overwhelming array of cultivation manuals.

“S-so many cultivation manuals?”

When I established the Dao-Seeking Sect, the cultivation manuals we had could only barely fill half a bookshelf at most, and many were just fillers. It’s completely incomparable to the current scripture library.

“Little Yun, what brings you here? Did you write another cultivation technique?”

A lean old man appeared. It was Elder Tao, the guardian of the scripture library. When he saw Lu Yang next to Yun Zhi, it evoked some unpleasant memories.

Last time, this kid Yun Zhi brought the Phoenix Ancient Ancestor here and nearly caused me to lose face. Fortunately, I’d backed off in time and yielded.

Yun Zhi shook her head. “I haven’t written any cultivation techniques recently. Little Junior Brother and Junior Brother Meng brought someone back who wishes to meet you.”

Elder Tao laughed heartily, completely unconcerned. “As long as it’s not the Phoenix Ancient Ancestor paying a visit, anyone who wants to meet me is welcome.”

He turned his gaze to the Innate Daoist Priest. “Is he the one who wants to see me? Who is he?”

Out of respect for a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator, the Innate Daoist Priest introduced himself first. “I’m Qi Tongtian.”

“So it’s Little Qi. Just call me Elder Tao. Is he a disciple preparing to enter this intake...” Elder Tao stopped mid-sentence, feeling something was amiss. “Wait, what did you say his name was?” Why does this name sound so familiar?

He cautiously asked, “Innate Daoist Priest Qi Tongtian?”

“Yes.”

Elder Tao looked as if he had seen a ghost. He instinctively took two steps back, somewhat horrified. Isn’t it said that the Founding Ancestor had died? Why is his corpse suddenly moving again?

Is the Dao-Seeking Sect’s ethos so poor that it finally angered the Founding Ancestor back to life?

Yun Zhi introduced him to the Innate Daoist Priest. “This is Tao Xian, the guardian of the scripture library. His cultivation is at the Transcendent Tribulation Stage.”

“Hello,” the Innate Daoist Priest greeted politely.

“Just call me Little Tao.” Elder Tao bowed and scraped, not daring to put on airs.

Lu Yang proceeded to explain the entire story behind the Innate Daoist Priest’s awakening. Only then was Elder Tao convinced it wasn’t an issue of the Dao-Seeking Sect’s ethos.

“Founding Ancestor, please feel free to take any cultivation manual that catches your eye.”

The Innate Daoist Priest smiled sheepishly. He was currently a mortal and hadn’t started cultivating yet, so cultivation manuals were useless to him.

After leaving the scripture library, the Innate Daoist Priest suddenly remembered what Elder Tao had said. “What was that about the Phoenix Ancient Ancestor that Little Tao mentioned earlier? Has that major figure also visited our Dao-Seeking Sect?”

The Innate Daoist Priest had heard that the Phoenix Ancient Ancestor was one of the Four Regents of the ancient Heavenly Court. Such an ancient big shot shouldn’t have any connection to our Dao-Seeking Sect.

Meng Jingzhou replied, “She has visited us. After all, the Phoenix Ancient Ancestor is a guest elder of our Dao-Seeking Sect.”

“Guest elder?” The Innate Daoist Priest grew increasingly bewildered. “That can’t be right. Isn’t this Phoenix Ancient Ancestor a member of the Heavenly Court Creed, the head of the Four Great Diabolic Creeds?”

Lu Yang explained casually, “Oh, that’s nothing. The ancient Heavenly Court is our Dao-Seeking Sect.”

“Ah?” The Innate Daoist Priest stood frozen in place.

Chapter 716: Once the Strongest Trump Card of the Dao-Seeking Sect

“The ancient Heavenly Court is our Dao-Seeking Sect?”

But I’ve heard the ancient Heavenly Court has formidable experts as numerous as clouds—the Heavenly Sovereign, the Creed Leader, the Four Regents, the Heavenly King Protectors, and all sorts of geniuses.

Most of all, there are things like the Phoenix Ancient Ancestor overpowering Supreme Lord Zhu Tian in a tough battle and Creed Leader Chu capturing two half-immortals.

Wait, two half-immortals?

The Innate Daoist Priest suddenly remembered the Nightmare Supreme Lord and the Void Emptiness Supreme Lord imprisoned at Incarceration Peak.

Aren’t they precisely the two half-immortals mentioned in the rumors on the streets?

I’ve been bombarded by successive shocking news at Incarceration Peak that I’ve lost my ability to think. But I’ve returned to my senses now. Creed Leader Yun couldn’t possibly have voluntarily handed over the two half-immortals to the Dao-Seeking Sect.

Unless Creed Leader Yun is one of the Dao-Seeking Sect members!

This explains everything!

But that still doesn’t make sense. The Heavenly Court Creed originated from ancient times; could it be that our Dao-Seeking Sect is actually an ancient major sect?

How did I not know about this?

“To be accurate, some members of our sect are the Heavenly Court Creed,” Lu Yang corrected. “Our ancient Heavenly Court Creed endured humiliation and pretended to be a diabolic creed as part of our mission to wipe out all the diabolic creeds in one fell swoop.”

The Innate Daoist Priest looked at Lu Yang with a strange expression.

You pretend to be a diabolic creed, and you ended up pretending to be the head of the diabolic creeds?

Given the strength the ancient Heavenly Court Creed has displayed, it would have been sufficient to sweep across the world several times over in my era.

As they spoke, the four arrived at the bamboo forest on the sect’s periphery. Deep within the forest, a stream babbled.

“Senior River Spirit, please come out and meet us,” Yun Zhi called out in a resounding voice.

The calm stream became turbulent. A fountain formed on the water’s surface, and upon the foundation appeared a weathered figure.

“What is it?” The River Spirit asked impassively.

“Little Green!” The Innate Daoist Priest blurted out the River Spirit’s nickname, his eyes lighting up upon seeing the River Spirit.

The River Spirit couldn’t keep up his aloof expression. Why does someone still know my name now?

No, I refuse to acknowledge this as my name.

“Who are you?” The River Spirit’s gaze landed on the Innate Daoist Priest, not recognizing the youth.

“It’s me! Qi Tongtian!” The Innate Daoist Priest introduced himself excitedly. I didn’t expect River Spirit Little Green to still be around.

The stream’s history predated even the Dao-Seeking Sect.

Before the Dao-Seeking Sect existed, the stream had produced a spark of spirit light, which at that time had not yet developed spirit intelligence. When the Innate Daoist Priest was traveling around, he discovered the stream’s anomaly by chance. He locked that spark of spirit light within the stream to prevent its dissipation and brought the stream back to the Dao-Seeking Sect. This eventually gave rise to the River Spirit.

If one were to get into the specifics, it wouldn’t be an exaggeration to say the Innate Daoist Priest had saved his life. It was due to this life-saving grace that the River Spirit kept protecting the Dao-Seeking Sect.

“Holy crap, you’re Qi Tongtian? You’re still alive?” The River Spirit showed a rare delighted expression upon seeing the Innate Daoist Priest.

“I’m still alive; it’s just that I had a bit of an accident.” The Innate Daoist Priest scratched his head, chuckling sheepishly.

“Seems like it was quite the accident; you’ve even turned into a mortal.”

“Just being alive is fine. I’m content.”

“True, you’ve always had that mindset.”

“The current Dao-Seeking Sect is incredible, completely different from when you first established it.” The River Spirit had witnessed firsthand how the Dao-Seeking Sect had grown stronger step by step.

The Innate Daoist Priest nodded. “I can see that. The younger generations are all very diligent, far better than I was.”

The two chatted back and forth about matters only they knew, their expressions animated. Having met again after 120,000 years, it felt as if they had returned to the Great Yu era. They had endless things to say and talked for a good half-day before finally pausing for a moment, looking like they still had much more to share.

Yun Zhi reminded them, “Seniors, you can chat anytime you wish in the future. Founding Ancestor, there is still one more person you haven’t met.”

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou were befuddled. By their count, they should have met all the senior members of the Dao-Seeking Sect. Who else have we not met?

“Right, we haven’t finished meeting everyone. Let’s go.” The Innate Daoist Priest smacked his forehead, realizing he couldn’t spend all his time here. “Little Green, see you next time.”

The River Spirit chuckled and scolded, “I told you I don’t want that rotten name! Think of a new one for me next time!”

“Big Senior Sister, who else haven’t we met?” Lu Yang whispered.

“There’s one left. You’ll know when we get there.”

The last higher-up was a significant distance away. Yun Zhi once again plucked a cloud and used it to carry the three of them.

The great grassland, Incarceration Peak, the former site of the Sword-Cleansing Pond... the cloud flew past these places without the slightest intention of slowing down.

Finally, it stopped at a desolate mountain upon reaching a deep part of the Dao-Seeking Sect, which Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou had never visited before.

“This is Boundless Mountain, where a senior of the sect is in seclusion. You haven’t met him because he has been in seclusion all this time. Moreover, his identity is rather special, and very few people know about him.”

As Yun Zhi spoke, she pushed aside the withered vines, revealing a cave behind them. “Senior, are you there? If you’re not in seclusion, please come out for a moment.”

Before long, a youthful voice came from within the cave, sounding like a youth roughly the same age as the Innate Daoist Priest. “Why are you shouting so loudly? Don’t you know how to respect your elders?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy let out a soft sound of surprise in the mental space.

Before Lu Yang could ask what was wrong, a youth emerged from the cave, his face full of impatience.

“Let me introduce—this is the Resurgence Ancestor of our sect, the Vast Sea Daoist Lord, Fang Wuya.”

“!!!”

This time, it was Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou’s turn to be astonished.

The Resurgence Ancestor from fifty thousand years ago—the Vast Sea Daoist Lord!

He’s still alive? Isn’t it said he was only at the Transcendent Tribulation Stage?

“No, he’s a half-immortal.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy saw through the Vast Sea Daoist Lord’s cultivation realm.

“I’m busy with seclusion. Why are you looking for me?”

The Vast Sea Daoist Lord’s existence was the Dao-Seeking Sect’s strongest trump card. He would not take action unless the sect faced a life-or-death crisis.

At least, that was the case before Yun Zhi joined the Dao-Seeking Sect.

After Yun Zhi joined the Dao-Seeking Sect, her cultivation advanced by leaps and bounds. The Vast Sea Daoist Lord felt this junior was a talent worth grooming and offered to give her some guidance.

Then, he was utterly defeated by Yun Zhi and reduced to a sorry plight, foaming at the mouth and collapsing to the ground.

From then on, he vowed to cultivate diligently, attain the Dao and become an immortal, and restore his dignity as the Resurgence Ancestor. Hence, he went into seclusion deep within the Dao-Seeking Sect.

Since then, he had vanished without a trace from the Dao-Seeking Sect.

“We found a senior whom you might need to meet.”

“Oh, which junior is it?” Fang Wuya asked casually. As the exalted Resurgence Ancestor, he was a senior to Yun Zhi, so anyone she brought would be a junior to him.

“This one.” Yun Zhi stepped aside, revealing the Innate Daoist Priest. “The person we found is the Founding Ancestor of our sect, the Innate Daoist Priest Qi Tongtian.”

“Hello, I am Qi Tongtian.” The Innate Daoist Priest was as polite as ever.

“Found-Founding Ancestor?” Fang Wuya was dumbstruck.

Originally, my status in the Dao-Seeking Sect was the highest—I was number one in both cultivation and seniority.

Later, Yun Zhi appeared, causing my cultivation to fall to second place in the Dao-Seeking Sect.

Now, just great, even my seniority is no longer number one.

Chapter 717: I Will Protect the Two of You Once

“This junior, Fang Wuya, pays his respects to the Founding Ancestor.” Fang Wuya performed a grand bow.

“I dare not accept such honor, I dare not.” The Innate Daoist Priest hurriedly waved his hands. For the Dao-Seeking Sect to survive until now, Fang Wuya’s contributions are no less than mine.

“The Founding Ancestor established the Dao-Seeking Sect. You deserve this bow,” the Innate Daoist Priest stated earnestly.

“Big Senior Sister, who in our sect knows of Senior Vast Sea’s existence?” Lu Yang whispered.

“The Vast Daoist Sea Lord is our sect’s strongest trump card and is not to be accessed lightly. According to the rules, only the sect leader is qualified to know of him. However, by Grand-Shifu’s generation, Grand-Shifu did not inform Shifu about Senior Vast Sea. Hence, Grand-Shifu was the only person who knew of Senior Vast Sea’s existence.”

Lu Yang remarked, Could it be that Grand-Shifu was afraid that if Shifu learned of Senior Vast Sea’s existence, he would rely on having a half-immortal backer and act even more recklessly to cause trouble outside? Maybe that’s why he didn’t tell Shifu.

It seems Shifu’s actions of scamming and swindling everywhere had cost him Grand-Shifu’s trust.

In contrast, although I resurrected an ancient immortal and drew out archaic Fusion, Transcendent Tribulation, and half-immortal cultivators, those events had ultimately occurred through various coincidences and weren’t intentional.

That must be why Big Senior Sister doesn’t consider me a troublemaker and is willing to tell me about Senior Vast Sea.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy looked at Lu Yang in surprise. Isn’t Yun Zhi telling you because the trouble you stir up exceeds the Vast Sea Daoist Lord’s ability, such that telling or not telling you about his existence makes no difference?

“Later, Grand-Shifu noted my remarkable talent in cultivation and hoped the Vast Sea Daoist Lord could guide me through my perplexity in cultivation. That’s why he broke the precedent and introduced me to Senior Vast Sea.”

“What happened after that?”

“After that, I guided Senior Vast Sea through his perplexity in cultivation. He had an epiphany and has been in seclusion ever since.”

Lu Yang, “...”

Meng Jingzhou, “...”

Did Senior Vast Sea really go into seclusion because of an epiphany?

“By the way, Big Senior Sister, could it be that the Primordial Heavenly Sovereign is also still alive?”

Yun Zhi shook her head gently. “The Primordial Heavenly Sovereign disappeared a long time ago. If the Primordial Heavenly Sovereign were still around, the Dao-Seeking Sect wouldn’t have experienced decline and then resurgence.”

The Primordial Heavenly Sovereign was a figure from the same era as the Xia and Meng families’ old ancestors. He established the concept of the Five Great Immortal Sects, and his strength was unquestionable. If someone like him had remained with the Dao-Seeking Sect, how could it have declined? And how could there have been the mention of “resurgence?”

Lu Yang contemplated it and felt it did make sense. “How did the Primordial Heavenly Sovereign disappear?” he asked.

“According to the sect’s daily records, eighty thousand years ago, the Primordial Heavenly Sovereign declared he wanted to travel the world. After that, no one knew where he went, and he was never heard of again. My guess is that he became trapped somewhere and couldn’t leave.” Yun Zhi sighed.

The Primordial Heavenly Sovereign was a half-immortal, and half-immortals have limited lifespans. After eighty thousand years, it’s unknown whether he is still trapped somewhere or has perished after his lifespan was depleted.

Of course, it’s also possible that he had the misfortune of encountering a certain immortal and was directly eliminated.

“Speaking of which, Founding Ancestor, why have you become a mortal? Did you disperse your cultivation to cultivate anew?” The Vast Sea Daoist Lord inquired.

The Innate Daoist Priest nodded. “Yes.”

“Then do you plan on cultivating again? How about I teach you?” A trace of excitement crept onto the Vast Sea Daoist Lord’s visage.

The Innate Daoist Priest couldn’t help but feel that something was odd about the Vast Sea Daoist Lord’s words. Although I was previously at the Fusion Stage and returning to it won’t be difficult, having a half-immortal teach me will indeed be more effective than cultivating alone.

“Alright.”

Seeing the Innate Daoist Priest agree, the Vast Sea Daoist Lord grew even more excited. “Then let’s start cultivating now—”

“Ah, no, there’s no hurry right now.” The Innate Daoist Priest cut off the latter part of the Vast Sea Daoist Lord’s sentence. “You see, I will definitely be cultivating in the sect in the future, which means I’ll inevitably interact with the sect’s disciples. I can’t possibly tell them I’m the Founding Ancestor; that would make them very reserved.”

The Innate Daoist Priest smiled sheepishly. “And I can’t just directly join the Dao-Seeking Sect; that would seem like I got in through backdoor connections, making our sect look corrupt.”

“Then what do you suggest?”

“Isn’t the entrance trial about to start? I’m wondering if I could pass it and join our sect as an ordinary disciple, starting everything afresh.”

The Vast Sea Daoist Lord’s eye twitched. Unsure how to respond, he remained silent for a long while before finally saying respectfully, “As the Founding Ancestor commands.” He proposed with a smile, “In that case, since my seclusion isn’t showing much results anyway, how about I give you a tour of the current Dao-Seeking Sect?”

I’ve been in seclusion for so long, but every time I close my eyes, I see Yun Zhi’s punches and kicks, each move threatening my life. In the end, my cultivation hasn’t progressed at all.

Besides, advancing from a half-immortal to an immortal can’t rely solely on seclusion. Throughout history, no immortal had achieved immortality through pure seclusion.

“This line of thinking is correct.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy saw through the Vast Sea Daoist Lord’s thoughts at a glance with her immense wisdom.

She selflessly analyzed the experience of becoming an immortal for Lu Yang. “To cultivate to an immortal, the most important factors are comprehension and mindset. There are many Dao Fruits similar to the Everlasting Dao Fruit, such as the Undying Dao Fruit and the Imperishable Dao Fruit. But why did none of them succeed, while only this immortal did?

Lu Yang couldn’t help but say, “Isn’t it because you are exceptionally talented, Immortal Fairy?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was about to say “It’s because this immortal has a good mindset,” but hearing Lu Yang’s words, she immediately grinned happily. “Yes, it’s because I’m a genius.”

The Vast Sea Daoist Lord continued, “Founding Ancestor, I presume that Yun Zhi brought you directly to this junior after meeting you. You haven’t had the chance to tour the current Dao-Seeking Sect. It’s very different from your time. Putting aside the faraway areas, just take the Incarceration Peak for example—it confines serious criminals with profound cultivation.”

The Innate Daoist Priest nodded. “Yes, I’ve gone to Incarceration Peak. It indeed confines many legendary great cultivators, including the Nightmare Supreme Lord and the Void Emptiness Supreme Lord.”

“Yes, it also confines the Nightmare Supreme Lord and the Void Emptiness... Wait, who did you say is in Incarceration Peak?” The Vast Sea Daoist Lord stopped mid-sentence, realizing something was amiss.

How long have I been in seclusion? Since when are half-immortals imprisoned in Incarceration Peak? Why do I not know about this?

The Innate Daoist Priest looked at the Vast Sea Daoist Lord with a peculiar expression and pointed at Yun Zhi. “I heard it was Yun Zhi who captured them.”

Standing beside Yun Zhi were Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou.

Previously, the Vast Sea Daoist Lord’s attention had been entirely focused on the Innate Daoist Priest, and he hadn’t noticed the presence of the two mighty Double Infants experts.

“Who are you two?”

“Greetings, Ancestor Vast Sea, I am Lu Yang, and my shifu is the Taciturn Daoist Priest.”

“Greetings, Ancestor Vast Sea. I am Meng Jingzhou of the Meng Family and a disciple of the sect.”

The Vast Sea Daoist Lord’s knowledge of the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s disciples stopped at the third disciple, Gan Tian. He wasn’t aware there was now a fourth disciple.

“Two decent juniors. Since Yun Zhi brought you to see me, I believe she holds you in high regard and considers you two exceptionally talented with promising prospects. Yun Zhi’s judgment has always been good.

“As your ancestor, I can’t meet you empty-handed, but I don’t have any suitable gifts on me at the moment.” He thought for a moment. “How about this? If the two of you ever cause trouble in the future, I will protect you once.”

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou quickly expressed their gratitude. “Thank you, Ancestor Vast Sea!”

Chapter 718: Intermediate Nascent Soul Stage

Although it was their first meeting, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou had already developed a considerable fondness for the Vast Sea Daoist Lord.

So this is the magnanimity of a senior.

When the Vast Sea Daoist Lord declared he would protect Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou once, Yun Zhi had originally wanted to advise him against it. However, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou were too polite and thanked him too quickly, so it was no longer convenient for her to interject.

The Innate Daoist Priest temporarily remained with the Vast Sea Daoist Lord, while Yun Zhi bid farewell to the two ancestors and took Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou back to their respective peaks.

“You two, focus on your cultivation.”

“As you command.”

~~~

Four months passed. Less than a month remained until the second day of the second month.

Disciples who had been out on missions returned one after another. Dai Bufan looked at the stacks of mission reports, nodding frequently with immense satisfaction. This proves that the characters of most mortals I had selected are acceptable.

Upon the sword stone, Lu Yang sat in the lotus position, gathering sword qi within. The Qingfeng and Mingfeng swords, the Seven Star Sword Set, and the extremely conspicuous Sword-Cleansing Pond hovered around Lu Yang, guarding his cultivation.

With each breath, a fresh energy circulated within him, breaking through acupoints and the shackles of his body, making Lu Yang resemble a slumbering jiao-dragon in the abyss that soared upward to roam the heavens!

Huff... Lu Yang exhaled a turbid breath containing the impurities within his body. The turbid breath transformed into a streak of sword qi that shot out with a whoosh. Following that, countless gigantic trees were severed at the waist and toppled over one after another.

Inhaling qi, he could swallow mountains and rivers; exhaling qi, he breathed out sword qi.

Lu Yang’s comprehension of the Sword Dao had climbed to a new level!

In the current cultivation world, no one had heard of anyone aside from the Taciturn Daoist Priest achieving this at the Nascent Soul Stage!

“Intermediate Nascent Soul Stage now.”

Lu Yang carefully sensed the changes after his advancement. Although it wasn’t as heaven-shocking and earth-shaking as shattering the golden core to form the nascent soul, there were indeed changes, and the improvement was substantial.

Now, I can defeat the Unbeatable Nascent Soul that is at the Basic Nascent Soul Stage!

“Unbeatable Nascent Soul, come forth for battle!”

Having obtained incredible power, Lu Yang attempted to challenge the Unbeatable Nascent Soul.

Soon, the Unbeatable Nascent Soul made him recognize reality.

“W-wait, hit softer.”

After all, the Unbeatable Nascent Soul was also at the Intermediate Nascent Soul Stage.

Wincing from the pain, Lu Yang reconnected his link with the Unbeatable Nascent Soul. Only then did it quieten down and return to his dantian.

After the brief exchange with the Unbeatable Nascent Soul, he had indeed identified his own shortcomings.

“Although my strength and speed are the same as the Unbeatable Nascent Soul’s, its techniques and methods are clearly more sophisticated and brilliant. Theoretically, I should be capable of this too.”

Lu Yang calmed down and repeatedly recalled his earlier beating, gaining significant insights.

“Perhaps this is the true use of the Unbeatable Nascent Soul—to help me find my shortcomings.”

Then, he mobilized the nine swords and activated the sword array excitedly.

“Immortal-Exterminating Sword Array!”

The nine swords levitated high above his head with their tips faced downward, emitting tremendous pressure. The Sword-Cleansing Pond exerted the greatest pressure.

Thud. Lu Yang knelt on the ground, unable to rise.

“Does this damned sword array not distinguish friend from foe? Even the master is affected!” Lu Yang fumed.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy pouted. “Have you forgotten what this sword array was originally used for?”

This was a sword array used by the Qilin Immortal on himself. Since its inception, it was designed to target the sword array’s master.

~~~

At the entrance to Meng Jingzhou’s cave abode, the stone door rumbled open. Meng Jingzhou put away the Yin-Yang Taiji Diagram and stepped out of the cave, stretching comfortably under the sunlight.

“Ah, so comfortable. I’ve finally reached the Intermediate Nascent Soul Stage.

“Hmm? Old horse, what are you doing?”

Meng Jingzhou noticed the old horse guarding the cave abode’s entrance, sitting on the ground with its hind legs crossed and its front legs resting on its knees. It inhaled and exhaled white vapor through its nostrils continuously.

“Are you cultivating?” Meng Jingzhou was unsure as he had never seen the old horse cultivate.

The old horse glanced sideways at Meng Jingzhou. I used to think the Fusion Stage was pretty good. After all, as long as Transcendent Tribulation old monsters don’t show themselves, I’m an unbeatable existence.

But now, I know I was wrong. Three years have passed since I pulled Meng Jingzhou away from the Meng Family. During this time, every enemy we encountered had exceeded my ability to handle.

They were either numerous or had high cultivation.

In any case, I could deal with none of them.

Only the clay statue we ran into not long ago gave me a slight sense of reassurance and let me know that I’m actually a mighty Fusion expert capable of sweeping across the world.

If I don’t work hard at cultivation now, it’s uncertain who will be guarding whom in the future.

~~~

“What a lively street.”

The Innate Daoist Priest and the Vast Sea Daoist Lord arrived at the commercial street. Given that they wouldn’t fit in as “strangers” in the Dao-Seeking Sect, the Vast Sea Daoist Lord employed a Daoist spell to conceal their existence.

The Vast Sea Daoist Lord thought, I’ve finally found a place the Founding Ancestor hasn’t visited.

He had just visited Incarceration Peak, confirming that the Nightmare Supreme Lord and the Void Emptiness Supreme Lord had indeed been captured. He also listened to the Grand-Shifu Tang Shengyi complain incessantly for half a day about how Incarceration Peak imprisoned too many half-immortals and Transcendent Tribulation cultivators, and that he—a mere Transcendent Tribulation cultivator—could barely manage it.

Afterward, the Vast Sea Daoist Lord and the Innate Daoist Priest went through a series of twists and turns before finally arriving at the commercial street.

The two traversed the bustling street like passing travelers of the world. Neither the Dao-Seeking Sect disciples nor the mighty experts hidden within the commercial street detected their presence.

“Lamb skewers! Fresh, authentic lamb skewers!”

The Innate Daoist Priest smelled the sizzling aroma of lamb fat dripping onto true fire and sniffed the air. “It smells so good.”

If I were still at the Fusion Stage, I would have passed the phase of satisfying base appetites and wouldn’t be tempted by simple lamb skewers. But I’m now a mortal, and mortals need to eat.

“Founding Ancestor, would you like some?” the Vast Sea Daoist Lord asked attentively.

“Dear guests, would you like to come inside to eat some lamb skewers?” the person hawking outside the barbeque shop entrance asked with a smile.

“Eat... Wait, you can see us?” the Vast Sea Daoist Lord instinctively answered on the Innate Daoist Priest’s behalf before suddenly realizing something was wrong.

We’re both under the effect of a Daoist spell. No one should have noticed us.

Unless the other party is at the Transcendent Tribulation Stage!

Since when does the Dao-Seeking Sect have a third Transcendent Tribulation cultivator?!

The Vast Sea Daoist Lord jerked his head up, staring at the person calling out. A soul form with the fluctuations of an Incipient Dao Fruit. “A half-immortal? Who are you?!”

“Me? I used to be the Everlasting Immortal. Now, I’m the boss of this barbeque shop and the slaughterhouse.”

“The Everlasting Immortal? You’re from the Everlasting Creed!” The Vast Sea Daoist Lord grew even more wary. To think that the Everlasting Creed has a half-immortal figure who has even infiltrated our Dao-Seeking Sect.

Judging from this, the Everlasting Creed is the strongest among the Four Great Diabolic Creeds!

The Vast Sea Daoist Lord activated his Incipient Dao Fruit, preparing to take action.

“Wait, wait, you’ve probably misunderstood. I was captured and brought to the Dao-Seeking Sect,” the Everlasting Immortal hastily explained. He had recognized the Vast Sea Daoist Lord at a glance, for the latter looked exactly like his statue.

“What’s going on?” The Vast Sea Daoist Lord frowned, withdrawing his Incipient Dao Fruit.

I’ve been in seclusion for three hundred years, but why does it feel like it has been tens of thousands of years? It seems the Dao-Seeking Sect has undergone heaven-shocking and earth-shaking changes, yet I know nothing about them.

If he had meticulously investigated the timing of these changes, he would have discovered that they hadn’t occurred over three hundred years, but within the last three years.

The Everlasting Immortal invited the two ancestors into the barbeque shop, instructing Chefs Liu and Gao to bring out their signature skills and serve all the good stuff.

“To explain how I ended up in your Dao-Seeking Sect, we must start from the beginning. It all began when your sect disciples went out on a mission to kill a tiger demon...”

Chapter 719: Myriad Spells Daoist Lord

It was the second day of the second month of the lunar calendar—a suitable day for recruiting disciples.

A colossal flying vessel slowly descended near the Dao-Seeking Sect. Countless young talents eagerly disembarked, excitedly gazing at the continuous mountain range in the distance.

“That must be the legendary Dao-Seeking Sect’s mountain gate!”

“I wonder how many people will pass the trials this time.”

“I heard that less than one percent of the participants managed to enter the Dao-Seeking Sect in the last round.”

“That’s so little. I’ve heard the acceptance rates of the Prison Suppression Sect and the Five-Elements Sect aren’t that extreme.”

“It’s not just that. I also heard that those who were filtered out either entered S-class sects or first-class sects, with only a handful entering second-class sects.”

“You get it now? Even those who failed the selection last time were considered great seedlings by other top-tier sects.”

“Young Master, don’t forget the Family Head’s advice. The matter of joining the Dao-Seeking Sect shouldn’t be forced.”

Most young talents were accompanied by their family elders. Whether they could join the Dao-Seeking Sect would determine their future life direction. Without an elder’s guidance, it was easy to lose self-confidence through constant self-doubt even before the trials began, leading to defeat without a fight.

Of course, there were also youths who came alone, such as Lu Yang from the previous cohort, who didn’t even know what a spirit root was and came to try his luck, and Meng Jingzhou, who had run away from home.

A handsome youth with a cold countenance alighted from the flying vessel. Each of his steps was of equal length, and his breath was drawn out, clearly indicating he was equipped with martial skills.

The youth looked toward the Dao-Seeking Sect, a mysterious smile curling at the corner of his lips. “I hope the Dao-Seeking Sect can bring me some surprises.”

“Fellow Daoist, did you come alone?” someone called out to the youth.

The youth turned to see two other youths roughly his own age—one with a shy smile, and the other with a serious expression.

The one who spoke was the youth with a shy smile.

“Who are you?”

“I’m Qi Tong, and this is Fang Ya. We are also here to participate in the Dao-Seeking Sect’s trials. I noticed you seem to share a similar goal. How about we go together?”

The cold youth snorted. “Who is your ‘fellow Daoist?’ My name is Gu Junye, and I am the reincarnation of the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord.”

“Myriad Spells Daoist Lord?” The youth with the shy smile was startled. The Myriad Spells Daoist Lord is a renowned, top-notch, great cultivator.

The Myriad Spells Daoist Lord was a figure from the early Great Yu Dynasty. He had a natural affinity with spells and was able to master any spell rapidly, his talent bordering on an immortal’s.

Foundation Establishment Stage at seventeen, Golden Core Stage at eighteen, Nascent Soul Stage at nineteen—his cultivation speed surpassed all geniuses. He made history by reaching the Transcendent Tribulation Stage in the shortest time ever.

Claiming “Myriad spells reside within the heart,” he thus received the Daoist title of “Myriad Spells Daoist Lord.”

In the Innate Daoist Priest’s era, one would say “you have the talent of the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord” to praise a genius.

What is the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord doing here?

What is reincarnation? Is it a mighty divine ability the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord comprehended?

Qi Tongtian stared at Gun Junye with shock and doubt, never expecting to encounter a legendary figure outside Incarceration Peak.

The Vast Sea Daoist Lord’s brows were imperceptibly scrunched up as he eyed Gu Junye warily. This person is the reincarnation of the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord? Could it be that the Nine-Netherworlds Creed was founded by the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord?

“However, our meeting signifies the fate between the three of us. You two can accompany me to the Dao-Seeking Sect.” With that, Gu Junye walked toward the Dao-Seeking Sect, gesturing for the Innate Daoist Priest and the Vast Sea Daoist Lord to follow.

“Founding Ancestor, why can’t we wait at the mountain gate? Why must we get off the flying vessel?” The Vast Sea Daoist Lord transmitted an auditory message. This is too troublesome.

The Innate Daoist Priest didn’t know how to transmit an auditory message, so he whispered, “For the disguise, we can’t miss any small detail. What if someone notices us walking out from the Dao-Seeking Sect? Wouldn’t that blow our cover?”

The Vast Sea Daoist Lord felt that the Innate Daoist Priest was overthinking it, but since the latter was the Founding Ancestor, he felt it wasn’t his place to comment.

The crowd surged toward the Dao-Seeking Sect like a tide. Compared to the previous cohort, the number of mortals coming to participate this time had increased severalfold. This was thanks to the popular storytelling performance, Saga of the Dao-Seeking Sect, in the outside world, which had attracted many mortals who admired the Dao-Seeking Sect.

Gu Junye and the other two blended into the crowd, utterly inconspicuous.

Meanwhile, a carriage slowly passed by the trio.

Inside the carriage, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou were muttering.

“Why hasn’t anyone come to sit in our carriage?”

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou recalled this day three years ago when Yun Zhi had boarded their carriage and claimed she was also here to participate in the entrance trials. Meng Jingzhou acted recklessly and courted death by revealing he knew the exam questions. Upon reaching the mountain gate, Yun Zhi alighted and soared into the air, announcing she was the chief examiner.

So cool.

They also wanted to randomly find someone to get into their carriage, then claim they were here to participate in the entrance trials, replicating Yun Zhi’s experience.

Unfortunately, they never found the opportunity.

“Should we have the old horse make another round?” Meng Jingzhou suggested. They had already made the old horse circle the area near the Dao-Seeking Sect several times.

Lu Yang shook his head. “Forget it, let’s get out. It’s almost time. Don’t forget we also have to organize the trials.”

To train their disciples, the Dao-Seeking Sect’s higher-ups had assigned the organization of the entrance trials to the disciples these two times. The organizer-in-charge last time was Yun Zhi, and this time, it was Dai Bufan.

Dai Bufan felt that nothing major should go wrong with him presiding over the event, so he had appointed Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou as organizers.

~~~

Elsewhere, the Innate Daoist Priest was making friends all around.

“Fellow Daoist, are you also here to participate in the trials? I’m Qi Tong. What’s your name?”

The person looked displeased upon hearing the Innate Daoist Priest address him as “fellow Daoist.” He snorted coldly and said nothing more.

How can some random cat or dog be qualified to address this esteemed one as a “fellow Daoist?” If not for the Yu Emperor’s treasure, who could come to a place like this?

Even if it’s during their recruitment drive, when the Dao-Seeking Sect’s defenses are relaxed, a rash assault by our Great Yu Alliance still has a chance of being repelled, with the Dao-Seeking Sect activating the Great Sect Defense Array and holding out until aid from the imperial court arrives.

If that happens, the operation would end in failure, and the difficulty of obtaining the Yu Emperor’s treasure next time would increase dramatically.

For this reason, I had taken the lead by disguising myself as a mortal to participate in the entrance trials.

Accompanying him in the entrance trials were several of his trusted aides. Not far away, cultivators from the Great Yu Alliance lay in ambush. At his command, they would coordinate from outside and inside, going on a rampage to slaughter and crush the Dao-Seeking Sect.

His aides had initially felt that their Alliance Leader was making a mountain out of a molehill, believing that dealing with a mere Dao-Seeking Sect shouldn’t require such trouble.

But when they saw an old horse at the Fusion Stage disguised as an ordinary horse and constantly circling the area near the Dao-Seeking Sect, they realized the sect wasn’t as simple as it appeared.

This old horse is clearly a great demon king that is subordinate to the Dao-Seeking Sect! It’s patrolling covertly and searching for suspicious individuals!

The aides communicated secretly with their spiritual consciousness. As they were at the Transcendent Tribulation Stage, they didn’t fear being discovered by the Dao-Seeking Sect.

“His Excellency is truly excellent; his considerations are always thorough.”

“Well, of course! His Excellency is none other than the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord, whose reputation resounded throughout the entire era!”

Chapter 720: Bone Foundation Test

“What's with the attitude?!” The Vast Sea Daoist Lord immediately flared up upon seeing the Innate Daoist Priest’s friendly greeting met with nothing but a disdainful snort.

That person narrowed his eyes, scrutinizing the Vast Sea Daoist Lord. Aside from the Yu Emperor and the first Imperial Preceptor, I’ve never encountered anyone who dares to speak to me like this.

In his eyes, the Vast Sea Daoist Lord was already a dead man.

If not for the occasion being inappropriate, I could crush this mortal a thousand times over with a mere thought.

Noticing an argument about to break out between the two, the Innate Daoist Priest hastily stepped between them. “Fang Ya, that’s enough. This is my fault. I shouldn’t have greeted him directly. He’s probably shy around strangers; let’s be understanding.”

If this were the Great Yu era, the Innate Daoist Priest would have assumed the other party was unwilling to engage with him; he had much experience with this. Cultivators in the Great Yu era might not speak for half a day, communicating only with a snort or a glance, as if everyone was deaf and mute.

But now was the Great Xia era. Based on his observations over the past few months, people in Great Xia were relatively optimistic and cheerful, unlikely to be so impolite as to snort coldly.

This person is probably just timid and shy around strangers.

Gun Junye sighed softly but said nothing.

The person was about to speak when a commotion from the crowd interrupted him.

Mist rose and morphed into an auspicious cloud that lifted Dai Bufan. Standing with his hands clasped behind his back, Dai Bufan wore a solemn expression as he addressed the densely packed crowd of participants in a clear voice.

“I am Dai Bufan, the person in charge of the entrance trials.

“The entrance trials this time consist of three rounds. Those who pass all three may become disciples of the Dao-Seeking Sect.

“Now, we shall begin with the first round—the bone foundation test. Line up in order of arrival. I will test your bone foundation.

“The rules for the first round are simple. Anyone under sixteen years of age who either possesses a minimal aptitude of Triple Spirit Root or a special constitution will pass the first round.”

Those accompanying the participants consciously moved away from the Dao-Seeking Sect’s mountain gate to await the final results, hoping their juniors would be fortunate enough to join the Dao-Seeking Sect.

Dai Bufan sat upright behind a table, and before him was a long queue. Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou stood on his sides like two guardian deities, their hands clasped behind their backs.

Their eyes roved restlessly, searching for Gu Junye, but they couldn’t locate him after looking for a long while; there were simply too many people.

The first person sat down and extended a hand. Like a physician diagnosing one’s pulse, Dai Bufan placed two fingers on his wrist and circulated his cultivation technique, examining this individual’s condition.

“Age is suitable. Metal-Water Dual Spirit Root. Not bad. What is your name?”

The first person felt overwhelmed and flattered. “I am Pang Yu!”

“Alright, you pass. Go ahead.”

The first person had a Dual Spirit Root. Dai Bufan felt that today's luck was good. It seems this intake will recruit many disciples with decent aptitude.

He tested thirty people in a row, and all had either a Dual Spirit Root or a Triple Spirit Root.

The mortals coming to participate in the Dao-Seeking Sect’s entrance trials could be divided into two categories—those who heard about the recruitment and came at their own expense to try their luck and those whom Dai Bufan had previously identified as potentially meeting the sect’s standards.

Dai Bufan had sought out qualified mortals in advance because he was worried they might otherwise go to the Five-Elements Sect or the Prison Suppression Sect.

The Five-Elements Sect, the Prison Suppression Sect, and the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace would conduct covert preliminary screenings before recruitment. They would then show themselves to candidates who passed and inform them that they could go to their respective sects.

Since the other immortals did this, if the Dao-Seeking Sect didn’t follow suit, they would be at a disadvantage.

In fact, many disciples mentioned in their mission reports that they had run into other immortal sect disciples. There were even instances where a single mortal was secretly observed by multiple immortal sects.

When such candidates were notified by several immortal sects that they could participate in the entrance trials, they would typically choose the Dao-Seeking Sect.

By joining the Dao-Seeking Sect, perhaps they could also become protagonists in Saga of the Dao-Seeking Sect.

“Triple Spirit Root. Are you Zhuang Ping?” Dai Bufan suddenly asked.

“Yes, I am Zhuang Ping. Is there anything wrong?”

“Nothing. You may go ahead.” Dai Bufan suppressed the urge to ask further, recalling Ji Hongwen’s mission report.

Out of kindness, Ji Hongwen had reported the case to the authorities, sending both the higher-ups of the Sea-Listening Sect and Zhuang Ping’s mother to prison. He was even considerate enough to assist with arranging prison visitation procedures for Zhuang Ping.

Originally, I thought Zhuang Ping wouldn’t choose the Dao-Seeking Sect. I didn’t expect him to actually come.

About half the participants had completed the bone foundation test. Aside from a few trying to slip through the tracks, most had passed the first round.

“A Dual Spirit Root temporarily faked with pills? Did you think I wouldn’t notice? You fail.” Dai Bufan shot a glance, signaling Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou to take action. They escorted the person away to be dealt with later.

Using pills to fake one’s spirit root was undoubtedly for fraudulent purposes. A mere mortal couldn’t access such a level of pills; there must be someone behind it.

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou stepped forward and hauled the person away, handing him over to Man Gu and Li Haoran. Then, they resumed their positions like door deities flanking Dai Bufan.

Finally, someone Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou were familiar with arrived.

Gu Junye exchanged a glance with the Xuanyuan Sword Master and the Unbreakable Saint. After all, the three of them had once fought valiantly across the realms, warring the heavens above and the abyss below and quelling turmoil in the human realm. The camaraderie forged through such bloody battles can’t be erased by mere cycles of reincarnation!

He confidently extended his arm.

“Water Spirit Root? Are you Gu Junye?” Dai Bufan was surprised. From Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou’s report, it was clear they held Gu Junye in extremely high regard.

“Indeed.”

Gu Junye possessed a Water Spirit Root, the same as Dai Bufan’s.

Dai Bufan also discerned that Gu Junye had undergone long-term physical training. Such a level of tempering is impossible without tremendous perseverance. This indicates that he has a steadfast Dao heart.

He pondered. If his other qualities are truly as impressive as Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou had claimed, passing the trials shouldn’t be a problem. Should I accept him as a disciple on Shifu’s behalf, like what Senior Sister Yun did with Lu Yang?

Oh, wait, our situations are different. The sect leader was imprisoned and couldn’t take disciples, but my own shifu is still alive and kicking. There’s no need for me to be a proxy; I can just have Shifu take him as a disciple directly.

“Alright, you may go ahead.” Dai Bufan waved his hand. He found Gu Junye’s tone somewhat amiss, but didn’t think much about it.

Gu Junye moved away, revealing the next person, whose appearance wrung Dai Bufan’s heart painfully.

“Hello, my name is Qi Tong. I’m here to participate in the trials.”

Dai Bufan had long heard that their Founding Ancestor also intended to participate in the trials. Although he was mentally prepared, encountering him in person still felt very awkward.

Should I offer my seat to the Founding Ancestor and let him sit here?

Dai Bufan placed two fingers on his Founding Ancestor’s wrist and instantly determined his spirit root.

“Wood Spirit Root. You pass.”

This didn’t involve pulling strings and connections through the back door; the Innate Daoist Priest genuinely had a Wood Spirit Root.

The Innate Daoist Priest originally had a Triple Spirit Root, but after dispersing his cultivation to cultivate anew, it improved to a Dual Spirit Root. Following that, Yun Zhi personally went to the Luoshui Guard headquarters to explain the situation. She removed the Golden Cicada Shell from Tao Tingfeng and brought it back.

With the help of the Golden Cicada Shell, the Innate Daoist Priest’s aptitude reached the zenith, becoming a Single Spirit Root.

Chapter 721: Gu Junye’s Heart Devil

“Next.”

Conscious of his role as a guardian, Lu Yang called out the next candidate like a sycophantic lackey.

The person after the Innate Daoist Priest was naturally the Vast Sea Daoist Lord.

However, Dai Bufan was unaware of this. He only knew that the Innate Daoist Priest was participating in the entrance trials.

The Vast Sea Daoist Lord carried himself with the demeanor of an expert—reticent and ice-cold.

Dai Bufan gently placed two fingers on the Vast Sea Daoist Lord’s wrist and quickly ascertained the results. “Variant Spirit Root—Thunder Spirit Root? What’s your name?”

“Fang Ya.”

Dai Bufan rummaged through his memories. This person isn’t in the character observation list. Did he come because of the sect’s reputation?

“Fang Ya? I’ve remembered you. Perform well.”

Dai Bufan placed the Vast Sea Daoist Lord in high regard. If he gets meticulously nurtured by the Dao-Seeking Sect, he could reach at least the Apex Fusion Stage in the future and become a mainstay of the sect.
