As a mortal, Fang Ya did not yet realize what a great fortune it was to earn Dai Bufan’s favor. He showed not a hint of gratitude for the goodwill extended to him, simply standing up and proceeding to the second round.

Only after joining the Dao-Seeking Sect would Fang Ya find out about the tremendous fortuitous opportunity he had missed today.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy looked at Lu Yang in surprise, not understanding why he had suddenly launched into an internal monologue.

“Next.” This time, it was Meng Jingzhou’s turn to call out.

The corner of Dai Bufan’s eye twitched. He couldn’t help but feel like an emperor seated upon the throne, with two little eunuchs on either side announcing the arrival of various officials in a shrill voice.

When he instructed Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou to drag away the person with the fake spirit root earlier, he had considered the idea of replacing the two beside him. Unfortunately, his plan didn’t succeed.

The person behind the Vast Sea Daoist Lord was the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord.

Originally, the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord had planned to simply fake a Dual Spirit Root. But the three people in front of me all had a Single Spirit Root. Wouldn’t faking a Dual Spirit Root make me seem inferior?

No, that won’t do.

The Myriad Spells Daoist Lord extended his arm, allowing Dai Bufan to examine him.

Dai Bufan’s cultivation technique could probe another’s physical condition, but it was ineffective against an opponent of the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord’s caliber.

The Myriad Spells Daoist Lord was confident no one would detect anything amiss with him. This is my confidence as a half-immortal.

The look of astonishment on Dai Bufan’s visage grew more pronounced. “Longevity Immortal Physique?”

As the name suggested, this was an immortal physique with an extremely long lifespan. From antiquity to the present, it was exceedingly rare that fewer than five such cases could be found.

Dai Bufan mumbled inwardly, What’s going on? Having high-quality candidates for this cohort is one thing, but why are they appearing in succession?

Starting from Gu Junye, this is already the fourth one.

The person waiting behind grew restless, glancing at the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord with envy. This is the kind of constitution even the Five Great Immortal Sects will fight over!

“What’s your name?” Dai Bufan asked.

“Gu Xie.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy stared at Gu Xie for a moment. “Why does something feel off?”

“Is there something wrong with this person?” Lu Yang asked.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy glanced at him again and stated with certainty, “This person is a half-immortal.”

“Half-immortal?!” If not for Lu Yang being used to seeing immortals and half-immortals, this matter alone would have made him exclaim aloud.

“That’s right, he has an Incipient Dao Fruit—he’s definitely a half-immortal,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy asserted.

“It looks like we have to report this matter to Big Senior Sister.” Lu Yang contemplated. This is beyond Senior Brother Dai’s ability to handle. The other party has hidden his identity to enter the Dao-Seeking Sect, likely with ill intentions.

However, Lu Yang didn’t return directly to Heaven’s Gate Peak, for it might alert Gu Xie.

After that, Dai Bufan tested roughly two hundred more individuals.

“Water-Wood Dual Spirit Root and a natural affinity for cultivating spirit plants?” Dai Bufan found yet another promising seedling. “I believe your name is Zhou Xing’er?”

This was also one of the mortals from the character observation list.

The mission report had recorded that Zhou Xing’er was born in a mountain village where sons were commonly favored over daughters, and she was no exception. Until a year ago, she happened to obtain a storage ring that could grow grains and vegetables inside it, and the crops planted in the storage ring grew exceptionally well. With this special storage ring, Zhou Xing’er avoided the fate of being married off.

According to the Dao-Seeking Sect’s investigation, the storage ring was crafted by Fifth Elder. He accidentally lost it while being pursued by the authorities for speeding with his flying shuttle.

After Fifth Elder learned of this, he explicitly stated there was no need to retrieve the storage ring.

“Alright, you may go ahead as well.”

“Thank you, True Lord.”

Seeing the timing was about right, Lu Yang transmitted an auditory message to Dai Bufan. “Senior Brother Dai, I have something to attend to. I’ll step away for a moment.”

Dai Bufan couldn’t be any more elated to see Lu Yang leave, and it would be even better if he dragged Meng Jingzhou along. Unfortunately, Lu Yang lacked such discernment and departed alone.

Man Gu took Lu Yang’s place.

“Next!”

Man Gu’s voice was loud and full of vigor, like an imperial guard at the palace gates announcing the arrival of various officials.

~~~

The first round concluded, with eight hundred people advancing to the second round.

If these eight hundred were placed in the outside world, second-class sects would scramble for them, while first-class sects would try to appear more reserved.

“Congratulations on passing the first round. We will now begin the second round.”

Dai Bufan continued to oversee the trials, while other sect disciples surrounded the eight hundred participants to maintain order.

The location for the second round was the bamboo forest—the River Spirit’s territory.

“As the saying goes, the path of cultivation is fraught with heart devils. In truth, before you even step into the cultivation world, the heart devils have already taken root in your hearts—the earnest expectations of parents, the deep affection of elders, the fear of failing this trial... All of these give rise to inner devils!

“This second round tests whether you can face your heart devils directly and overcome them!

“Of course, considering your minds are not yet fully mature, overcoming heart devils would be extremely difficult. Therefore, in this second round, you may choose to face your heart devils alone or form teams to overcome them together. After all, the companionship and assistance of friends are indispensable on the path of cultivation.”

The Innate Daoist Priest remarked with a smile, “All of you are so impressive—a Water Spirit Root and the legendary Longevity Immortal Physique!” He admired Gu Junye and Gu Xie. “I heard the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord possessed the Longevity Immortal Physique. Perhaps you can become a powerhouse like him one day.”

Gu Xie remained unmoved by the Innate Daoist Priest’s praise.

Gu Junye patted Gu Xie’s shoulder and exhorted like an elder mentoring a junior, “While one’s physique is important, what matters more is a steadfast Dao heart!”

Gu Xie snorted coldly, subtly evading Gu Junye’s hand.

“How about this? As they say, many hands make light work. It is fate that the four of us met at the mountain gate. Why don’t we form a team to overcome our heart devils?”

Gu Xie sneered inwardly. Fine, I’ll join your team. This will be an opportunity to eliminate all three of you, leaving only me to pass.

“Alright.”

In an instant, the bamboo forest was shrouded in a mist, obscuring vision beyond a distance of one zhang.

The River Spirit stood upon the water’s surface. Bubbles gurgled up from the water and floated into the air, growing larger and larger until they were finally the size of a person.

These giant bubbles enveloped everyone. For those who had teamed up, the bubbles collided and merged into larger ones, allowing the temporary squads to enter a single bubble together and face a shared heart devil.

~~~

“Looks like this is the illusory domain.”

When the Innate Daoist Priest and the other three regained consciousness, they found themselves in a desolate place and immediately knew they were inside an illusory domain.

Gu Xie laughed inwardly. I’d like to see what heart devils these three have. They’re probably nothing more than the reproach from parents or things that frighten only wimpy kids—nothing to be concerned about.

Let’s see you three make utter fools of yourselves!

Suddenly, the wind and clouds shifted. A thunderbolt struck a distant mountain peak and shattered it directly.

Gu Xie was startled. What’s happening?

Gu Junye stood with his hands clasped behind his back. His head was tilted at a forty-five-degree angle as he gazed indifferently at the sky and murmured, “It’s coming.”

“What’s coming?” Gu Xie couldn’t help but ask.

Gu Junye covered his restless right eye, calming the unruly Heaven-Swallowing Beast within it, and pointed toward the ominously dark sky.

In the sky, thunder roiled, its sound resembling the cry of dragons and phoenixes, with the momentum to destroy heaven and earth.

“I never imagined my heart devil to be this.”

“What exactly is this?” Gu Xie’s eyelids twitched, a sense of foreboding welling within him.

Gu Junye sighed softly. “The lightning tribulation that caused me to perish in my previous life—the Ninety-Nine Immortal Ascension Tribulation.”

Chapter 722: The Real and Fake Myriad Spells Daoist Lords

“What did you just say?” Gu Xie wondered if he had misheard.

Why would a Ninety-Nine Immortal Ascension Tribulation suddenly appear?

Just who is the half-immortal here—you or me?

Besides, I haven’t heard of any lightning tribulation called the “Ninety-Nine Immortal Ascension Tribulation!”

What the hell is this Ninety-Nine Immortal Ascension Tribulation?! Did I miss it in some ancient text?

Within the Ninety-Nine Immortal Ascension Tribulation, Gu Xie saw the Jade Purity Heavenly Tribulation, the Cosmos Great Lightning Tribulation, and the Silent Annihilation Purple Lightning Tribulation... It was as if all the lightning tribulations had gathered together.

BOOM.

Before the Ninety-Nine Immortal Ascension Tribulation had even fully formed, its shockwaves already flattened one mountain peak after another. Several large rocks fell from the sky, landing near their feet.

~~~

Outside the illusory domain, Dai Bufan’s eye twitched violently.

He had originally wanted to see how the Founding Ancestor would overcome his heart devil. Before the Innate Daoist Priest’s heart devil appeared, the sudden flash of lightning nearly blinded him.

“Whose heart devil is this?!”

Which mortal’s heart devil creates such a huge commotion? The lightning tribulation I faced to reach the Fusion Stage wasn’t even this intense!

“That Gu Junye fellow.” The River Spirit conjured a chair from water and sat down beside him with his legs crossed. He controlled all the heart devils and knew who generated each one.

Dai Bufan whipped his head around and stared at Meng Jingzhou. “You need to give me an explanation.”

Meng Jingzhou wanted to drag Lu Yang down with him, but suddenly remembered that Lu Yang had disappeared before the second round started. Could it be that bastard Lu Yang knew there’d be trouble and ran off in advance?

“They’re kids, after all. It’s totally normal for them to have vivid imaginations.”

“What’s the Founding Ancestor’s heart devil?” Dai Bufan asked the River Spirit curiously.

The River Spirit waved his hand. “He might have had a heart devil before, but not anymore. If not for him having nothing better to do than to form a team, he would have passed on his own.”

~~~

The Innate Daoist Priest truly had no heart devil. He had one during the Great Yu era, but after seeing his contemporaries imprisoned at Incarceration Peak and realizing even heart devils could be captured, his own heart devil vanished.

Gu Xie’s eyelids twitched as he watched the swirling lightning tribulation overhead. If I act, I’ll definitely expose my identity. If I don’t act, I’ll be struck dead by lightning and fail.

Why was I out of my mind to form a team with you three?

The Innate Daoist Priest had never witnessed such a massive lightning tribulation and murmured in admiration, “As expected of the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord. Even his heart devil is this powerful.”

Gu Xie’s expression was even more stunned than when he encountered the lightning tribulation. “Who is the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord?”

The Innate Daoist Priest pointed at Gu Junye. “Him. He’s the reincarnation of the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord.”

Gu Xie was dumbfounded. If he is the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord, then who am I?

Soon, Gu Xie realized that Gu Junye was an imposter.[1]

He has a death wish!

Wait, that’s not right. The world only knows that I, the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord, is a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator; they don’t know I had become a half-immortal long ago. Besides, a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator can’t possibly encounter an Immortal Ascension Tribulation!

How does Gu Junye know he’s a half-immortal?

He asked Gu Junye nonchalantly, “How do you know the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord was a half-immortal? Why haven’t I heard of that?”

Gu Junye turned his head, his eyes revealing loneliness, as if he was recalling his past life. “What half-immortal? The Myriad Spells Daoist Lord was a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator, of course.”

“How could a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator survive an Immortal Ascension Tribulation?!” Gu Xie fumed, feeling he was being toyed with.

The corner of Gu Junye’s mouth curved into a mocking smile as he said meaningfully, “Becoming an immortal means becoming an immortal. If you haven’t, then you haven’t. Where does this so-called ‘half-immortal’ come from? It’s merely the idle talk of the common folk.”

Gu Xie initially wanted to refute this, but upon deeper contemplation, he found Gu Junye’s words surprisingly reasonable.

Gu Junye paid no further attention to Gu Xie. In truth, he didn’t know about the half-immortal realm; he had simply gone along with Gu Xie’s words earlier. Gazing at the fully formed Ninety-Nine Immortal Ascension Tribulation overhead, he said insipidly, “No matter. Since this matter arose because of me, it shall end with me.”

Under the astonished gazes of the other three, Gu Junye slowly flew into the air and faced the lightning tribulation head-on!

He remained unyielding despite bathing in the tribulation lightning, as if a figure from time immemorial had manifested at this moment, eternal throughout time. For a moment, Gu Xie felt that the other party was the true Myriad Spells Daoist Lord and that he himself was the imposter instead.

The next moment, Gu Xie and Vast Sea Daoist Lord realized simultaneously. Gu Junye is undoubtedly a mortal. The reason he can fly and face the lightning tribulation unscathed is that this is an illusory domain!

If heart devils can be imagined, one’s own strength can also be imagined!

Having connected the dots, the two felt greatly reassured. It’s fine as long as we can rely on our imagination for strength.

The Vast Sea Daoist Lord felt that this was a good opportunity to see what his heart devil was. If he didn’t open his heart, the River Spirit couldn’t draw out his heart devil.

Gu Xie and the Vast Sea Daoist Lord instantly erupted with a massive boost in power, envisioning themselves as mortals becoming Transcendent Tribulation cultivators. They stood shoulder-to-shoulder with Gu Junye and jointly resisted the lightning tribulation.

Due to the Innate Daoist Priest’s lack of imagination, he could only watch from below.

The three joined forces to fight the lightning tribulation.

“Why is this lightning tribulation so powerful?” Gu Xie inwardly cursed after experiencing it firsthand, realizing the lightning tribulation was even fiercer than it appeared.

~~~

Meanwhile, Zhou Xing’er was also trapped in her heart devil of being berated by her mother.

“I gave birth to you and raised you for so long. Find a good family to marry into in the future; that can earn you some spirit stones and support your elder brother’s cultivation!”

Zhou Xing’er was timid and didn’t utter a word.

~~~

The lightning strikes fell, containing boundless power, as if they intended to split heaven and earth apart again to create the universe.

“This is the Jade Purity Heavenly Tribulation,” Gu Junye explained. He had seen a description of it in an ancient text sold at a street stall.

Gu Xie was struck until smoke practically emitted from his mouth. Forget about scheming to eliminate the other three; I’ll be lucky not to be eliminated myself.

The Vast Sea Daoist Lord had a Lightning Spirit Root and had his own methods for dealing with lightning tribulations, so he fared slightly better than Gu Xie.

Gu Junye had imagined himself enduring a lightning tribulation countless times. He could survive all of them except the eighty-first.

~~~

“You have a Dual Spirit Root? Perfect! You can transplant your spirit roots to your elder brother. Let him cultivate; his talent is surely higher than yours!” Zhou Xing’er’s mother continued to point at Zhou Xing’er and chastise her. She wore a shrewish expression, and spittle flew everywhere.

Zhou Xing’er kept her head down, not daring to retort.

~~~

“This is the Silent Annihilation Purple Lightning Tribulation!”

Purple heavenly lightning descended, piercing through space and annihilating all things into utter stillness. The three were blasted until they were on the brink of death.

Gu Xie was charred all over, and the Vast Sea Daoist Lord and Gu Junye weren’t much better. After eighty tribulation lightning strikes, they didn’t have a single area of intact flesh left on them.

Gu Xie glared at Gu Junye resentfully. Once I conquer the Dao-Seeking Sect, you will be the first to die!

Crack.

The eighty-first tribulation lightning fell. The three braved it with sheer willpower and finally survived it.

Thud. They crashed into the ground simultaneously and created a crater, their lives hanging by a thread.

~~~

“You’re saying a half-immortal has infiltrated the entrance trials?” Yun Zhi repeated, her eyelids lifting slightly upon hearing Lu Yang’s report.

“Yes, that person calls himself Gu Xie, but his real name is unknown.” Lu Yang was about to say more when Yun Zhi raised a hand to interrupt him.

“Wait a moment, Little Junior Brother. I sense someone has manifested me as their heart devil. Let me go and take a look first.”

~~~

“It’s finally over.” Gu Xie heaved a sigh of relief. He was worried that if the strikes continued, he wouldn’t be able to stop himself from using his Incipient Dao Fruit.

An Incipient Dao Fruit is definitely not something a mortal can imagine. Using it would have exposed me immediately.

Gu Xie had blocked the River Spirit’s probing. From the River Spirit’s perspective, Gu Xie had no heart devil.

It should finally be over now.

Before Gu Xie could catch his breath, he felt an oppressive pressure descend from the sky, even more terrifying than the previous Ninety-Nine Immortal Ascension Tribulation.

He looked up and saw a female cultivator high up in the air. She had her back to the sun, her features indistinct, appearing divine and sacred.

The Vast Sea Daoist Lord’s heart devil—Yun Zhi.

1. Just a small note: they don’t use the same “gu” in their names. ☜

Chapter 723: Not A Bad Opponent

“Yun Zhi?” Gu Xie was flabbergasted. Whose heart devil is this?

Yun Zhi hadn’t acted in public many times, and the outside world knew little about her. But who was Gu Xie? He had been secretly gathering intelligence on the major factions of Great Xia, including Yun Zhi.

Yun Zhi, the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s first disciple, possesses astonishing cultivation talent. During an exchange event between immortal sects, she managed to defeat four sect leaders after much effort, including three at the Fusion Stage and one at the Transcendent Tribulation.

Hence, Yun Zhi’s strength is evident—she’s a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator.

She absolutely can’t be a half-immortal.

In this regard, the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord was in the best position to speak. He was the cultivator with the fastest cultivation speed in history; even the Yu Emperor Wu Youdao was slightly slower than him.

However, even he could not cultivate to a half-immortal in less than a thousand years.

Therefore, it’s also impossible for this Yun Zhi of the Dao-Seeking Sect.

So whose heart devil is this?

Gu Junye’s?

Impossible. His heart devil was that pain in the ass Ninety-Nine Immortal Ascension Tribulation, and we’re done with that.

That Qi Tong fellow’s?

It doesn’t look like it from his reaction.

Then it must be Fang Ya!

Gu Junye staggered to his feet, sensing the boundless power emanating from the graceful figure in the sky. His expression had never been this grim.

“I have passed the Ninety-Nine Immortal Ascension Tribulation and become an immortal. I am unbeatable under heaven. Yet, I never imagined denizens of the Heavenly Realm would exploit the rift torn between the immortal and mortal realms during the immortal tribulation to enter the mortal world!”

Gu Junye fell to his knees weekly. “My friends, I can only count on you two to deal with the Heavenly Realm invader now!”

Gu Xie, “...”

Yun Zhi can’t be your heart devil too, right? You brat, just how many heart devils do you have?

Gu Xie sneered coldly. It doesn’t matter whose heart devil it is. I’ve just imagined myself as a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator. At the same cultivation realm, I fear no one!

Gu Xie leaped into the air and struck Yun Zhi with a golden fist seal, and then...

Boom!

Gu Xie was slapped to the ground by Yun Zhi, landing spread-eagled in the shape of a “大” character.

“Pah!” Gu Xie sat up, spitting out mud from his mouth. What cultivation realm is this heart devil at? How is its strength so formidable?

The Vast Sea Daoist Lord thought, So my heart devil is Yun Zhi. This was actually within his expectations; he had just been unwilling to admit it. After all, he had been beaten far too tragically back then.

“This is troublesome.” The Vast Sea Daoist Lord was in a quandary. My heart devil is absolutely undefeatable.

What should I do? Should I reveal my identity and ask the River Spirit for special treatment through a back door?

But I can’t afford to disgrace myself like this.

~~~

In the real world, the River Spirit sat with his legs crossed. He pretended not to know that Fang Ya was the Vast Sea Daoist Lord, excited to watch the spectacle.

Just wait to get beaten up!

“A heart devil of Senior Sister Yun? Whose heart devil is this?” Dai Bufan was flummoxed. Have any of these four even met her?

That doesn’t make sense either. Even if they had met her once, it’s unlikely for her to have become their heart devil.

~~~

The Vast Sea Daoist Lord noticed Gu Xie, who had been slapped to the ground, and became pensive.

During the lightning tribulation earlier, I noticed that this Gu Xie kid has a vivid imagination. Coincidentally, this round tests teamwork. Perhaps the two of us can join forces to defeat Yun Zhi!

“Shall we attack together?” the Vast Sea Daoist Lord proposed.

Gu Xie was also a smart person and instantly understood the Vast Sea Daoist Lord’s meaning.

We can indeed join forces.

Gu Xie and the Vast Sea Daoist Lord soared into the sky, confronting Yun Zhi. For a moment, their auras were evenly matched.

“Mountain-Moving Seal!”

“Ten-Thousand-Zhang Divine Light!”

The two acted simultaneously as if they had a tacit understanding. Gu Xie employed the Mountain-Moving Seal, condensing a range of a hundred thousand continuous mountains into a fist within his grasp and decisively throwing a punch!

The Vast Sea Daoist Lord summoned a ten-thousand-zhang divine light, which transformed into a divine sword occupying most of the sky. The sword’s tip pointed downward, piercing the clouds as it plummeted toward Yun Zhi!

Boom! Boom!

The more the two fought, the more vigorous they became. Since the Yun Zhi in the illusory domain was the Vast Sea Daoist Lord’s heart devil, the bolder he became, the weaker the heart devil Yun Zhi became. As one waxed and the other waned, the two gradually shifted from a state of being beaten to fighting on equal footing.

~~~

“Could they actually defeat Senior Sister Yun?” Dai Bufan was stunned, having watched this side closely.

“Junior Brother Dai, who wants to defeat me?”

Dai Bufan turned around to find Yun Zhi standing behind him, unsure when she had arrived. “Senior Sister, why are you here?”

“I sensed someone manifesting me as their heart devil, so I came over to check on the situation.”

“Inside this bubble?”

“Yes.”

Yun Zhi nodded, saying nothing more. She took a step forward and vanished on the spot, entering the bubble.

~~~

“Whew—”

“Whew—”

Although Gu Xie and the Vast Sea Daoist Lord were battered and covered in bruises, their eyes were filled with hope. Together, we might actually defeat Yun Zhi!

The most obvious sign is that Yun Zhi’s aura is continuously plummeting—it has now dropped to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage!

The heart devil Yun Zhi suddenly paused for a moment, then resumed her previous demeanor. The two couldn’t help but wonder if it was a figment of their imagination when they noticed Yun Zhi’s eyes seeming more lively than before.

Gu Xie also felt the heart devil Yun Zhi glancing in his direction, though he wasn’t sure whether it was intentional. It doesn’t matter. We must finish this quickly to avoid further complications!

“Heaven-Imprisoning Finger!”

A finger thicker than a mountain descended from the sky, aiming to suppress the heart devil Yun Zhi.

“Thousand-Layer Wave Strike!”

The Vast Sea Daoist Lord unleashed a thousand palm strikes, each more powerful than the last. By the thousandth strike, the accumulated force was enough to destroy heaven and earth!

Below, Gu Junye watched the battle excitedly, eager to learn these moves.

The Heaven-Imprisoning Finger and the Thousand-Layer Wave Strike attacked simultaneously. The heart devil Yun Zhi raised her hand, the golden bell on her wrist tinkling softly.

Ding-dong.

Accompanied by the crisp bell chime, an invisible wall seemed to appear before the heart devil Yun Zhi, blocking all attacks.

The Vast Sea Daoist Lord was merely three inches away from the heart devil Yun Zhi, yet he couldn’t breach the defense no matter what.

The heart devil Yun Zhi flipped her palm and gently delivered a strike, returning all the attacks in full measure!

She launched a series of attacks, her moves no longer as rigid as before, and dished out ingenious moves continuously. Although the power of each move did not exceed the Transcendent Tribulation Stage, they forced Gu Xie and the Vast Sea Daoist Lord to retreat repeatedly, wearing them down.

Gu Xie was beaten black and blue. He had eight fractures, and he felt like his organs were intertwined. Even with his willpower, he couldn’t remain expressionless with such injuries.

All he felt now was regret and regret. Being struck by lightning and then beaten up... Had I known, I would have chosen a different method to infiltrate the Dao-Seeking Sect!

Through the exchange, Yun Zhi probed Gu Xie’s hidden strength. Having tested his power, she ended the battle, pretending her power was depleted and feigning defeat before dissipating into the air.

With a massive explosion, the bubble burst. Gu Xie finally heard the heart devil Yun Zhi say, “Not a bad opponent.”

Before leaving, Yun Zhi instructed Dai Bufan to let all four of them pass this round.

~~~

“Big Senior Sister, you’re back so soon?” Lu Yang had not even warmed the throne when he saw Yun Zhi return.

“Things went quite smoothly. Didn’t you say a half-immortal had infiltrated the sect’s entrance trials?”

“Yes.”

“You don’t have to care about him. He’s not a bad opponent—perfect for Senior Vast Sea to handle and restore his confidence.”

Chapter 724: The Third Trial

“I just surveyed the area. Apart from this half-immortal, several unfamiliar Transcendent Tribulation cultivators have also disguised themselves as mortals and infiltrated the entrance trials. They’re likely working together.”

“Several Transcendent Tribulation cultivators too?” Lu Yang was astonished. They dare to barge into the Dao-Seeking Sect when this is all they’ve got? Are they tired of living?

Yun Zhi assumed Lu Yang was worried about the sect’s safety and reassured him, “There’s no need for concern. Our sect also has Transcendent Tribulation cultivators, enough to handle them. With me around, life in the sect has been too peaceful, which can breed complacency. This is a good opportunity for them to get some exercise.

“You can return to organizing the trials. With me here, nothing will go wrong.”

“Understood.”

~~~

Following Yun Zhi’s imperial decree, Lu Yang returned to the bamboo forest to continue overseeing the trials.

“Senior River Spirit, it has been a long while,” Lu Yang greeted him politely. It had been four months since they last met.

The River Spirit snorted coldly, not wanting to acknowledge Lu Yang. He remembered clearly what Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou had done during the entrance trials three years ago.

Lu Yang saw that the River Spirit was unwilling to engage with him and sidled up to Meng Jingzhou’s side, whispering, “How is the second round progressing?”

Meng Jingzhou rolled his eyes. Gu Junye’s trial is already over, and you only show up now? Can you be any later?

Meng Jingzhou decided then and there. When I get married and send out marriage invitations, I will send one to everyone except Lu Yang. I’ll only send Lu Yang an invitation on the second day, after the wedding night!

I absolutely have to get back at him!

“Gu Junye, the two founding ancestors, and that kid with the immortal physique teamed up and passed the second round.”

Lu Yang nodded. This was within expectations.

“The others aren’t progressing as fast. I reckon it’ll take at least half a day or an entire day.”

For the vast majority of people, heart devils were an incredibly challenging hurdle to overcome. The heart devils encountered by Gu Junye and the other three only required fighting and killing. Regardless of whether they succeed, the outcome would be quickly apparent.

Others didn’t face such heart devils that could be resolved by mere force.

One example was the one Lu Yang was currently watching—Zhou Xing’er’s heart devil.

Zhou Xing’er’s mother favored sons over daughters and upheld the belief that the husband was king. She had originally hoped for two boys but didn’t expect her second child to be a girl. As such, she often verbally abused Zhou Xing’er, calling her a burden and a waste of money. Over time, Zhou Xing’er’s character became timid and submissive, afraid to resist.

Although Zhou Xing’er later earned a considerable amount of money for the family with the help of the storage ring, her status at home did not improve.

When her mother learned that Zhou Xing’er was qualified to enter the Dao-Seeking Sect, she mocked her even more, thinking Zhou Xing’er was delusional.

Zhou Xing’er’s relatives also treated her with mostly ridicule and sarcasm. After finding out about the storage ring, they used her young age and her inability to safeguard valuable items as a pretext to demand the ring.

Zhou Xing’er naturally refused. Subsequently, her relatives’ attitude toward her worsened.

She did try resisting, repeatedly proposing to sever ties with her family. However, each time, her mother would insist that they were connected by flesh and blood and remind her of the grace of upbringing, saying that blood ties couldn’t be severed so easily.

Left with no choice, Zhou Xing’er rose in rebellion and went alone to the imperial city to assassinate the Xia Emperor.

The assassination failed. Her entire clan was subjected to the nine familial exterminations.[1]

The heart devil was dispelled.

Zhou Xing’er woke up and stretched lazily. “Serves you right for not severing ties with me. Finally, you’re all dead.”

Although she could have chosen to cultivate peacefully in the Dao-Seeking Sect, she felt unsettled as long as her family was alive, which would cause her to feel uneasy when she cultivated in the future. Now that they’ve all died once in the illusion, my Dao heart is finally clear.

Lu Yang, “...”

He pretended not to have seen Zhou Xing’er and turned to look at Zhuang Ping, feeling a bit of schadenfreude.

Zhuang Ping’s mother was sent to prison by Senior Brother Ji. What is his heart devil? Revenge against Senior Brother Ji? Revenge against those from the Sea-Listening Sect?

~~~

Inside the illusory domain.

In a prison.

“Mother, I will definitely save you!” Zhuang Ping roared, veins bulging on his neck as he gazed at his mother in the prison cell, his emotions out of control.

“No, don’t save me! I’m guilty and deserve this!” Zhuang Ping’s mother had tears flowing down her face.

“Mother, I will master great skills to save you! Even if I have to chop my way through with an axe, I will save you!” Zhuang Ping gripped the axe in his hand.

It was the legendary Heaven-Splitting Axe, capable of splitting heaven and earth apart—more than enough to cleave open a prison cell.

“Son, you mustn’t do this. There’s no way you can oppose the imperial court!” Zhuang Ping’s mother shook her head, urging her son to get back on the right path, since those who resisted the imperial court faced no good end.

Zhuang Ping’s lips quivered. The axe fell to the ground with a clang. His knees collapsed to the ground weakly, and he bawled bitterly. “Mother, I will listen to you.”

***

“In summary, my mother prevented me from breaking her out of prison, which constitutes the meritorious act of stopping another from committing a major crime. Hence, she should receive a sentence reduction,” Zhuang Ping stated calmly to the official from the Ministry of Justice.

Zhuang Ping’s mother had her sentence reduced.

Zhuang Ping’s heart devil was dispelled.

Lu Yang, “...”

~~~

After half a day, fewer than fifty out of the eight hundred people had dispelled their heart devils, a testament to the difficulty of the task. Those who hadn’t overcome their heart devils were already trapped within them, unable to break free without external intervention.

Seeing that time was almost up, Dai Bufan requested the River Spirit’s help to disperse the thick mist and water spheres, releasing everyone from their heart devils.

Those who failed the second round were crestfallen. They were destined to have no affinity with the Dao-Seeking Sect, and disciples escorted them out.

Dai Bufan clapped and smiled as he announced to the remaining fifty in a sonorous voice, “Congratulations on successfully overcoming your heart devils. We will now move on to the third and final round.”

He paused, then added, “Cultivators are not devoid of emotion and virtue. Among these virtues, filial piety is of utmost importance.

“The third round tests filial piety, in other words, your attitude toward your parents and siblings.

“Unlike the second round, where you could team up, the third round is conducted individually. During this round, you will forget your original identity and act based on your inherent nature.

“Let the third round begin now.”

Dai Bufan bowed slightly to the River Spirit beside him. “Senior, if you will.”

With a thought from the River Spirit, mist rose once more. This mist contained an illusory array; anyone enveloped by it would fall into an illusion.

The corners of Gu Xie’s mouth revealed a smile. Testing filial piety? It looks like this round isn’t hard. Others may forget their original identities, but I won’t. As long as I carefully tend to my parents and get along with my brothers, passing will be a cinch.

~~~

He entered the illusory domain and found himself on top of a granary. There was a leak in the roof, and he was holding tools to repair it.

“Where is this?”

Suddenly, thick smoke billowed from the granary, making him cough.

Soon, he heard someone shout, “Fire!”

The identity assigned to him in this round surfaced in his mind.

He had three family members: his father, his stepmother, and a younger brother born to his father and stepmother.

His father and stepmother feared he would compete with his younger brother for the family fortune and tried to harm him multiple times. This fire was their doing!

1. This is the most severe punishment in ancient China. Essentially, the entire clan would be executed, including extended family members, and this went up to nine degrees of relation. Due to how ancient Chinese society highly emphasized filial piety, this punishment was considered one of the ten great crimes and the ultimate disgrace, with the entire family line being wiped out. However, based on historical records we have now, this punishment was fully carried out only once or twice. The most notable case is the one at the end of the Sui Dynasty, with a person named Yang Suigan receiving this capital punishment. ☜

Chapter 725: Gu Xie Is Unable to Endure It Anymore

The conflagration had appeared suddenly. Seeing the dire situation, Gu Xie knew that if he burned to death here, there would be no need to talk about filial piety.

Moreover, I’m currently a mortal and can’t use my powers.

It’ll be too late if I wait for the fire to die out or for rescue. There’s only one way to survive.

Gritting his teeth, he adjusted his posture and jumped down from the top of the granary.

My luck isn’t bad; I only broke my leg.

A day later, Gu Xie lay there in despair, devoid of all will to live. No one in the family was taking care of him. He didn’t even have the right to lie on a bed and could only lie on a straw mat covered with a straw “quilt.”

“Son, are you alright?” His father seemed to be concerned.

Gu Xie remarked, I’m lying here like this, and you ask if I’m alright? If you hadn’t set the fire, would I have been nearly burned to death?

If this were reality, he would have killed this “father” several times over now. But this was part of the trial testing filial piety. He could only suppress the rage in his heart and force a smile. “Father, I’m fine.”

His father breathed a sigh of relief. “I told you we didn’t need to get medicine from the physician—what a waste of money. You’ve been strong since childhood; you’ll recover even without medicine.”

“Father is right.”

During mealtime, Gu Xie’s stepmother complained in a shrill voice, “When will he get better? We can’t afford to keep a useless person in the house.”

Three months later, Gu Xie finally recovered and could work in the fields.

Another three months passed. Gu Xie’s father approached Gu Xie, saying that other families had wells, but they didn’t, and that he planned to have one dug.

This task naturally fell to Gu Xie. His father and stepmother couldn’t bear to let his younger brother do the work.

Gu Xie was physically strong. Grunting with effort, he swung the shovel and managed to dig a well three or four meters deep in half a day.

Just as Gu Xie wanted to rest for a while, a shovelful of dirt landed on his head. He looked up and found his father and younger brother filling the hole.

“What are you doing? I’m still down here!”

His father and younger brother turned a deaf ear, speeding up their shoveling to bury Gu Xie alive.

Gu Xie was furious. They’re not even pretending anymore!

Fortunately, while digging the well, he had carved small footholds into the wall to serve as a ladder. In a few quick moves, he used them to leap out of the well, startling his father and younger brother.

Covered in dust, Gu Xie demanded, “What are you doing?!”

His father quickly regained his composure. “We didn’t know you were down there.”

Gu Xie glared at his father hatefully. If not for this being a test, I’d bury this whole family alive!

Time passed.

Gu Xie seemed to have forgotten the two life-threatening crises and his family’s bullying. He remained respectful to his parents and kind to his younger brother. Unfortunately, his father contracted a serious illness that ultimately couldn’t be cured. His younger brother married into another family and moved to the city, never contacting them again.

In contrast, Gu Xie appeared extremely filial and was renowned throughout the village as a paragon of filial piety. Later, the story of Gu Xie’s filial piety reached the county, and the county magistrate promoted him to a constable to commend him.

Somehow, Gu Xie’s mother developed a gambling addiction. As a constable, Gu Xie ran into her multiple times during raids on gambling dens and secretly let her go each time. The county magistrate eventually found out and dismissed Gu Xie from his post.

Gu Xie successfully married and had children, living with his mother. Unfortunately, good times didn’t last long. His mother gambled away the family fortune. It was winter, and the family had no money and food for everyone.

Gu Xie’s wife discussed it with him. “We can give birth to more sons, but we only have one mother; let’s bury our son.”

Gu Xie agreed with his wife’s idea. One night, they went to dig a pit. Before they had dug deep, the shovel hit something.

“A jar?”

The couple opened the jar and found it full of glittering gold!

They were over the moon. With this jar of gold, we no longer have to bury our son, and our family can even become wealthy and famous!

His wife knelt on the ground, believing their filial piety had moved the heavens.

With the gold, Gu Xie’s family soon lived a life of luxury, moving into a large residence. Gu Xie’s mother lived out her remaining years in comfort and passed away peacefully.

Half a year later, the true owner of the gold found Gu Xie’s family and demanded they return it. However, they had already spent all the gold, and there was no way to return it.

Gu Xie was thrown into prison.

The illusion ended.

~~~

Gu Xie woke up, finding himself to be the last one to do so; Gu Junye and the others had awakened long ago.

Dai Bufan shook his head lightly upon seeing Gu Xie wake up. “You failed.”

“I failed?” Gu Xie was stunned. How did I fail when everything was fine? Everyone and all the villages within ten li knew about my filial piety!

“Putting aside that you still treated your family with respect despite their multiple attempts to murder you...

“...let’s talk about your stepmother’s repeated gambling. You didn’t stop her and even abused your authority for her. Not to mention your subsequent plan to bury your son, constituting an interrupted act of intentional homicide. In addition, you used the gold you unearthed to let your stepmother live out the rest of her life comfortably, making it impossible to return the gold, constituting the crime of misappropriation.“

Failing alongside Gu Xie were his aides. However, they weren’t as patient as he was. Under their families’ incessant bullying, they snapped and killed their entire families, never holding out until the constable stage.

Gu Xie pointed at Gu Junye and the others. “So they all passed?”

“Of course, they passed.”

Dai Bufan felt that letting Gu Xie leave directly might trigger him to take extreme actions, so he snapped his fingers and replayed Gu Junye’s illusion.

After Gu Junye jumped off the roof and broke his leg, he directly reported his parents to the county magistrate. The county magistrate deemed the parents guilty of attempted intentional homicide and sentenced them to ten years in prison.

He passed.

“Where is the filial piety in that?!” Gu Xie roared in rage. I clearly remember the third round tests filial piety.

“Letting one’s parents understand that they must not harbor malice toward others and that wrongdoing deserves its due punishment naturally aligns with filial piety.”

Dai Bufan replayed the Innate Daoist Priest’s illusion.

The Innate Daoist Priest was digging a well. When he saw his father and younger brother trying to bury him alive, he jumped out of the well and killed them both.

He passed.

“He killed people and still passed!” Gu Xie had also wanted to kill his father and younger brother at the time but had restrained himself.

“That was justifiable self-defense.”

Gu Xie pointed angrily at his subordinates who had failed. “Then why did they fail for killing people?”

Dai Bufan patiently explained, “Justifiable self-defense requires urgency. They endured bullying over time, resulting in anger building up in their heart until they finally snapped and erupted violently. They killed because of a minor incident at the time, which lacked urgency. It doesn’t constitute justifiable self-defense.

“Accumulating anger with no outlet is not the path of cultivation.”

Noticing that Gu Xie’s emotions were somewhat out of control, the Innate Daoist Priest stepped forward to offer consolation, though somewhat shyly. “Fellow Daoist Gu Xie, you’re too kind-hearted. How could you endure others wanting to kill you? That’s not good. You need to be decisive in killing, like me.”

Gu Xie could no longer suppress his fury. Ever since he started participating in the trials, he had suffered humiliation after humiliation. First, I was struck by lightning eighty-one times for no reason in the second round, then beaten to a pulp by Yun Zhi, leaving me with numerous fractures and not a single skin intact. Later, in the third round, I endured humiliation for the sake of filial piety, only for the Dao-Seeking Sect to tell me I failed and that I’m too kind-hearted!

They’ve gone too far with the bullying!

“Kind-hearted your grandfather!” Gu Xie wanted to send the Innate Daoist Priest flying with a sweep of his sleeve.

He had originally planned to pass the trials, enter the core areas of the Dao-Seeking Sect, and break it from within. Who would have thought that not a single member of our Great Yu Alliance would pass, experiencing a complete wipeout!

The ultimate disgrace!

I won’t endure it anymore! You all must die!

“How dare you harm others?!”

The Vast Sea Daoist Lord realized something was wrong the moment Gu Xie’s killing intent surged. This Gu Xie has been hiding his true strength! He boldly struck out, colliding with Gu Xie’s sleeve.

The two forces clashed, their energy shooting upward into the firmament.

You dare to kill the Old Ancestor? You must be tired of living!

Chapter 726: The Dao-Seeking Sect’s Foundation

“Transcendent Tribulation Stage?” The Vast Sea Daoist Lord knew he had misjudged Gu Xie’s cultivation realm the moment he exchanged blows with him.

Without activating one’s Incipient Dao Fruit, even a half-immortal would find it difficult to distinguish whether an opponent was at the Transcendent Tribulation Stage or a half-immortal.

“How dare you cause trouble at the Dao-Seeking Sect? You must be tired of living!” Although the Vast Sea Daoist Lord had paid little attention to the outside world for a long while, he still knew who the current Transcendent Tribulation cultivators were.

Gu Xie was not among them.

Then the answer is obvious—Gu Xie is an archaic cultivator!

“Are you the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord, Gu Mo?” The Vast Sea Daoist Lord remembered the Longevity Immortal Physique Gu Xie had displayed. The most famous individual with this physique was the cultivation genius from the early Great Yu era, the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord Gu Mo!

“I'll give you credit for having some discernment.” Gu Xie sneered. This person is merely a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator; he’s no match for me!

“Everyone, attack!” At Gu Xie’s command, his aides shed their disguises and revealed their true cultivation realms—the Transcendent Tribulation Stage!

A total of three Transcendent Tribulation cultivators had been hiding among the crowd!

Seeing the situation exacerbating, the River Spirit waved a hand. Countless bubbles rose from the river's surface and enveloped the mortals participating in the third round and the disciples organizing the trial, swiftly transporting them inside the Dao-Seeking Sect for safety.

“How did so many Transcendent Tribulation cultivators suddenly appear?” Dai Bufan was appalled. And who is that person fighting the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord?

“Senior Brother Dai, this matter has nothing to do with the two of us.” Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou quickly dissociated themselves from the matter to prove their innocence.

“...Do you two know who the person fighting the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord is?”

“Yes, we do. He is the Vast Sea Daoist Lord.”

“He is still alive?!” Dai Bufan was flabbergasted. He thought the Vast Sea Daoist Lord had perished long ago. “Wait, in other words, the heart devil Senior Sister Yun Zhi that appeared in the second round belonged to Senior Vast Sea?” He had assumed it was Gu Junye’s heart devil.

Lu Yang nodded.

~~~

“He is the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord?” The Innate Daoist Priest was taken aback and looked at Gu Junye.

Then who is Gu Junye?

Gu Junye’s expression was grave as he watched the spectacular display of clashing powers in the bamboo forest. He hadn’t restored his cultivation yet and could not participate in a battle of this level.

I severed three corpses back then to undergo the tribulation and become an immortal; never would I have imagined those three corpses to survive until now!

~~~

The River Spirit mobilized the power of the great array to confront the three Transcendent Tribulation cultivators from the Great Yu Alliance.

With the great array’s boost, he was equivalent to a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator. Fighting three opponents of the same level was overly strenuous.

“Senior River Spirit, we’re here to assist you!”

Two elderly figures appeared, blocking the path of the three Great Yu Transcendent Tribulation cultivators. They were none other than the Grand-Shifu Tang Shengyi and Elder Tao from the scripture library. Having sensed the battle in the bamboo forest, they came to join the battle immediately.

“Oh? I never expected the Dao-Seeking Sect to have so many Transcendent Tribulation cultivators. You’ve been hiding your strength, huh?!” The three Great Yu Transcendent Tribulation cultivators sneered. The Dao-Seeking Sect’s power is beyond our expectations, but not enough to affect the outcome.

After all, our Great Yu Alliance has more than just the three of us.

Suddenly, several powerful auras shot skyward from outside the Dao-Seeking Sect, causing the Grand-Shifu’s expression to change.

The opponent has two more hidden Transcendent Tribulation cultivators!

Wait, not just Transcendent Tribulation cultivators; there are also over twenty Fusion cultivators!

They’ve come out in full force!

Five Transcendent Tribulation cultivators and over twenty Fusion cultivators stood in two rows, their combined auras momentarily overwhelming the Dao-Seeking Sect’s.

“You dare to attack our Dao-Seeking Sect? You’re courting death!” Streaks of light shot across the sky, appearing on the battlefield.

“Shifu, we are here.” First Elder led the other seven elders to the bamboo forest. Appearing alongside the elders were the owner of the commercial street, the owner of the Hundred Fragrance Restaurant, the Vice Hall Leader of the Great Mission Hall, Dai Bufan, Ji Hongwen, and others...

All the Dao-Seeking Sect’s Fusion cultivators had gathered!

“Merely Fusion cultivators? They won’t stir any waves!” The Great Yu cultivators laughed arrogantly. Our side has a total of five Transcendent Tribulation cultivators!

One of the Great Yu Transcendent Tribulation cultivators brazenly struck out, extending a black hand toward First Elder. The black hand transformed into a diabolic claw made of smoke; anyone who came into contact with it would dissolve into pus!

Boom!

First Elder threw out an object resembling a brick, striking the diabolic claw. Its owner winced in pain and sharply retracted the claw.

The diabolic claw’s owner saw what had hit him clearly—a cyan-green porcelain pillow.

The immortal treasure, the Yellow Millet Dream Pillow, was originally held by the Everlasting Immortal Fairy and later became a precious supreme treasure of the Everlasting Creed. Chefs Liu and Gao had attacked the Dao-Seeking Sect with it, but were captured by the sect, and the pillow became First Elder’s magical treasure.

“What, afraid to fight me?” First Elder taunted as he brandished the Yellow Millet Dream Pillow.

His strength was on par with the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s; both were at the Half-Step Transcendent Tribulation Stage. With the boost from the Yellow Millet Dream Pillow, he possessed power comparable to a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator!

“You merely have one additional Transcendent Tribulation level combatant!”

The Great Yu side remained unafraid.

“Merely one more?” Clad in iron armor, Third Elder strode through the air and stood shoulder-to-shoulder with First Elder.

He delivered a ferocious punch, and the resulting wind from the fist howled, sending the Great Yu’s Fusion cultivators stumbling. Even the Great Yu’s Transcendent Tribulation cultivators felt immense pressure and had to assume defensive stances.

This fist rivaled a Transcendent Tribulation physique cultivator’s strike!

The iron armor was rusty and stained with blackened blood, looking like the most common battlefield gear. But anyone who knew its origin would not underestimate it.

This was the armor won by the Primordial Heavenly Sovereign during the campaigns at the end of the Great Yu era. It was soaked with the blood of his enemies, all at the Transcendent Tribulation Stage. A Fusion cultivator wearing this armor could match a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator!

Each of the Five Great Immortal Sects possessed methods comparable to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage. For the Dao-Seeking Sect, it was this armor!

“Now, the playing field has been leveled!”

The Grand-Shifu chuckled. A massive yellow bell descended from the sky, surrounded by mysterious runes of hundun primal chaos. Instantly, the bell emitted a deep, resonant hum that seemed to come from the distant past. The sound waves spread out like ripples, causing the very space around them to tremble faintly.

“The Hundun World-Suppressing Bell!” The Great Yu Transcendent Tribulation cultivators recognized the origin of the massive yellow bell.

During his tenure as sect leader, the Grand-Shifu had also been a mighty expert who roamed the cultivation world with few rivals; otherwise, he couldn’t have managed the Taciturn Daoist Priest and the others.

His life-bound magical treasure, the Hundun World-Suppressing Bell, was likewise renowned throughout the cultivation world. Countless famous individuals had fallen under its chimes.

“Kill!” The Grand-Shifu’s expression shifted sharply as he barked.

The bell’s chime resounded once more, and the two sides clashed in battle.

~~~

The Vast Sea Daoist Lord and the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord fought at an even higher altitude.

“Heaven’s Eye!” An eye appeared in the sky, from which a black light shot forth, catching the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord off guard.

At that moment, time suddenly slowed down, giving the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord enough time to react. He nimbly dodged the black light.

“Immortal Fairy, can you identify what the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord’s Incipient Dao Fruit is?”

“Hmm, since he has the Longevity Immortal Physique and just slowed time down, it should be the Longevity Incipient Dao Fruit.”

Chapter 727: The Longevity Incipient Dao Fruit and the Space Incipient Dao Fruit

“What is the Longevity Incipient Dao Fruit? Does it belong to our Everlasting Lineage?” Lu Yang asked.

“Let this immortal think how to explain it to you.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy lowered her head, tapped her forehead, and explained after serious contemplation. “To explain the Longevity Incipient Dao Fruit, we must start by explaining the Longevity Immortal Physique. Do you know about it?”

“I’ve heard a little. It’s said that those with the Longevity Immortal Physique have a lifespan several times longer than those at the same cultivation realm.”

“That explanation works, but it’s not comprehensive.”

Since the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord possessed the Longevity Immortal Physique, it meant he had likely lived from the early Great Yu era until now without slumbering, making him a true living fossil.

The Longevity Immortal Physique was exceedingly rare, and there were hardly any descriptions of it in texts. However, coincidentally, there was someone who possessed this physique in the ancient era.

“The Longevity Immortal Physique has two functions. One is just as you said—living longer. The other is accelerating one’s own time.”

“What does ‘accelerating one’s own time’ mean?”

“Take that Myriad Spells Daoist Lord as an example. If learning a spell normally takes him a full day, he can accelerate his speed twelvefold. To the outside world, it will look like he learned the spell in just two hours instead of an entire day.

“Drawing upon this same principle, the Longevity Immortal Physique also works during cultivation. Him cultivating for two hours is equivalent to others cultivating for a full day.

“Wasn’t it said that this Myriad Spells Daoist Lord was a cultivation genius with incredibly fast cultivation and spell-learning speeds? This is the reason.”

Lu Yang finally understood. So that’s how it is.

Essentially, the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord isn’t as terrifying as the world claims; all of it had been piled up through sheer time.

“Since he has the Longevity Immortal Physique, the easiest Incipient Dao Fruit to form would be the Longevity Incipient Dao Fruit. That’s just how lazy people are.

“The Longevity Incipient Dao Fruit inherits the Longevity Immortal Physique’s abilities, evolving from ‘Longevity’ to ‘Undying,’ and retains the time acceleration of the self.

“Didn’t you see it just now? The Myriad Spells Daoist Lord manipulated time to dodge the Vast Sea Daoist Lord’s Heaven’s Eye.”

Lu Yang nodded. With his own ability, he naturally couldn’t clearly see the process of the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord manipulating time. Hence, he had been borrowing the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s immortal consciousness to watch the battle from the beginning.

He saw it with perfect clarity.

“The superior versions of this type of Incipient Dao Fruit are my Everlasting Dao Fruit and the Epoch Dao Fruit. He’s considered half a member of our Everlasting Lineage.

“Let me demonstrate it to you.”

~~~

“There was no spell fluctuation just now; it was the ability of an Incipient Dao Fruit. You are a half-immortal?” The Vast Sea Daoist Lord narrowed his eyes at the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord.

Logically speaking, the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord shouldn’t have been able to dodge Heaven’s Eye at his level, yet he did.

The only explanation is that he’s a half-immortal.

“Heh, your discernment is not bad despite your lacking strength.” Confident of victory, the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord’s lips curled into a mocking smile.

The gap between a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator and a half-immortal cannot be bridged by any means.

“Lacking strength?” The Vast Sea Daoist Lord’s eyes turned icy as killing intent radiated from him. This is my first time encountering a cultivator who dares to evaluate me like this!

The Myriad Spells Daoist Lord was about to say something more when he suddenly raised his hand and slapped himself, causing both him and the Vast Sea Daoist Lord to pause for a moment.

The Myriad Spells Daoist Lord looked at the Vast Sea Daoist Lord in bewilderment. Is this his technique?

~~~

“You saw that, right? This immortal can control his actions at will,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy said smugly. “How’s that? Should I make him slap himself a few more times?”

Lu Yang, “...”

“Big Senior Sister wants the Senior Vast Sea to gain combat experience. Immortal Fairy, you should behave.”

Lu Yang suddenly thought of another question. “Doesn’t the Longevity Incipient Dao Fruit mean that if he condenses the full Dao Fruit, he would possess the abilities of both the Everlasting Dao Fruit and the Epoch Dao Fruit?”

That would be terrifying.

“In theory, yes. However, the Longevity Incipient Dao Fruit has significant problems.

“First, while it has the ‘undying’ characteristic, it doesn’t reach the level of the Third-in-Command, who can self-detonate and recover at will. At most, he can survive a few fatal injuries. Its time manipulation ability also can’t compare to the Epoch Incipient Dao Fruit.

“In the ancient era, there was a half-immortal with the Longevity Incipient Dao Fruit, and he died at the hands of the Epoch Immortal when he was still a half-immortal.

“Second, as long as this immortal and the Epoch Immortal exist, he can never condense the complete Dao Fruit.

“Third, our Everlasting Lineage has high requirements for one’s temperament. Someone with his temperament cannot condense a Dao Fruit.

“At the half-immortal level, blindly meditating in seclusion is useless. What’s important is comprehension. Perhaps some mundane daily occurrence can provide you with inspiration, clearing the clouds and revealing the sky to shed light on your path of cultivation, thereby allowing you to improve.

“In cultivation, merely piling up time doesn’t yield results.”

“Even if that’s the case, the Longevity Incipient Dao Fruit is still very powerful. Can Senior Vast Sea really win?” Lu Yang was worried, and not without reason. How do you fight someone who can control time and doesn’t die?

“He can win.”

~~~

Neither half-immortal, ancient or modern, dwelled on why the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord had suddenly slapped himself. They resumed their intense battle.

“Raging Waves of Stormy Seas!”

The Vast Sea Daoist Lord extended two fingers and performed Shadow-Swap Teleportation, summoning the waters of the East Sea. He had once roamed the East Sea and left a mark on its seabed, allowing him to summon the seawater above that mark at any time.

The waters of the East Sea descended from the sky, pouring down upon the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord.

Even with his time control, facing such a large-scale spell made escape difficult, unless he fled the Dao-Seeking Sect, but that would defeat his original purpose.

An invisible barrier held back the seawater, suspending the East Sea’s waters in the air and submerging both the Vast Sea Daoist Lord and the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord.

The Myriad Spells Daoist Lord produced a spear. This was his proud magical treasure that was only a step away from being an immortal artifact. The spearhead was engraved with a Reverse Five-Elements Spell Seal that was capable of breaking through anything composed of the five elements, such as the East Sea’s waters.

Time accelerated. The Reverse Five-Elements Spear became too fast to see as it pierced through the seawater and thrusted toward the Vast Sea Daoist Lord’s back.

“Freeze!” The Vast Sea Daoist Lord had long noticed the Reverse Five-Elements Spear. With a light shout, the seawater froze, transforming into a giant iceberg. The faint chill it emitted could be felt even by the Transcendent Tribulation and Fusion cultivators fighting below.

Ice also belonged to the five elements. As it was within the Reverse Five-Elements Spear attack range, the spear penetrated the Vast Sea Daoist Lord’s body, the massive shockwaves even splitting the iceberg into two.

Unexpectedly, the Vast Sea Daoist Lord was completely unharmed, while the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord had a fist-sized penetrating wound in his abdomen.

“Transplanting Flowers and Trees... No, this is a spatial method!” The Myriad Spells Daoist Lord spat blood. He knew the power of the Reverse Five-Elements Spear best.

Initially, he thought the Vast Sea Daoist Lord had transferred the injury to him, but he quickly realized that wasn’t the case. Executing Transplanting Flowers and Trees required multiple conditions, which hadn’t been met earlier.

He used a spatial technique!

What seemed like the spear piercing the Vast Sea Daoist Lord was actually him transferring the pierced part of himself to the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord.

The Space Incipient Dao Fruit!

Chapter 728: Counter Each Other

“I didn’t expect you to possess an Incipient Dao Fruit too!” The Myriad Spells Daoist Lord wiped the blood from the corner of his mouth with his thumb. The wound on his abdomen rapidly healed as if it had never appeared.

The ability of the Longevity Incipient Dao Fruit—Undying.

“Time acceleration, wound recovery...” The Vast Sea Daoist Lord lacked the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s vast knowledge, so he could only analyze the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord’s Incipient Dao Fruit abilities based on clues from the battle.

I wonder how many times he can use that wound recovery ability. It’ll be troublesome if he can execute it indefinitely.

“Reverse Scale Dragon-Summoning Technique!”

“Ten Thousand Trees Harmony!”

“Shining Sun and Moon!”

“Cyan Lotus Crossing Calamity!”

During the accelerated time, the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord unleashed over ten different spells in one go. This was the benefit of time acceleration; in the time it took others to cast one spell, he could overwhelm his opponents with sheer quantity!

The shadow of a coiling dragon manifested. Bodhi seeds took root upon landing, growing into towering trees that merged with the dragon shadow, transforming into a Bodhi ancient dragon that roared across heaven and earth.

The sun and moon appeared together, an unusual phenomenon only seen in antiquity, their forces of yin and yang dazzlingly brilliant.

A cyan lotus formed from pure magical power drifted out, each petal brimming with destructive energy.

“Go!”

The Myriad Spells Daoist Lord lived up to his title. The dozen spells were diverse and comprehensive. Mastering any one would take others significant time. Only the Myriad Spells had the time to learn this many spells.

Even if someone could defend against a few spells, they couldn’t possibly defend against all of them.

To his surprise, the Vast Sea Daoist Lord smiled nonchalantly, letting the spells strike him without sustaining a single injury.

“Oh no!” The Myriad Spells Daoist Lord sensed something amiss and accelerated time again, hastily shifting his position. Immediately after, all those spells landed on his previous location, causing an earth-shattering explosion.

“Purple Heaven Divine Lightning!” The Vast Sea Daoist Lord turned the ice back into water. Bright heavenly lightning fell into the water, filling the entire area with the power of lightning.

No matter how fast the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord was, he could only be forced to assume a passive defensive position when facing an unavoidable attack.

“What, is this the level of the legendary Myriad Spells Daoist Lord?” The Vast Sea Daoist Lord taunted. He had a Lightning Spirit Root and excelled in lightning spells.

In terms of fame, the Vast Sea Daoist Lord’s status as the Resurgence Ancestor was certainly less renowned than the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord, the genius celebrated through the ages. But greater fame didn’t equate to greater strength.

Some Incipient Dao Fruits countered each other, but clearly, the Longevity Incipient Dao Fruit didn’t counter the Space Incipient Dao Fruit.

“I presume you were always overshadowed by the Second Imperial Preceptor in the early Great Yu era.” The Vast Sea Daoist Lord strolled through the water as endless thunderbolts rained down incessantly, striking the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord into a state of rapture and agony.

The Myriad Spells Daoist Lord realized he couldn’t fight in the water any longer. He cast a Water-Repelling Mantra to split the East Sea waters into two, which would give him a chance to dodge the lightning.

“What do you mean?!” The Myriad Spells Daoist Lord’s emotions were unstable.

“Did I hit a sore spot?” The Vast Sea Daoist Lord continued to pick at his wound. “The Second Imperial Preceptor wielded the Karma Incipient Dao Fruit, which could erase his own existence, making him perfect for assassination.

“Although you can automatically recover from injuries, it’s not infinite. Eventually, the Second Imperial Preceptor would wear you down to death. His Incipient Dao Fruit inherently countered yours!”

“Shut up!” The Myriad Spells Daoist Lord snapped as he seemed to recall some unbearable memory. He unleashed Three Heads Six Arms and stopped time for a few breaths.

“Shared Life and Death!” The Myriad Spells Daoist Lord cast a curse, linking his life with the Vast Sea Daoist Lord’s. This move ignored spatial defenses; both of them would be injured and die simultaneously.

Furthermore, since he had the “undying” trait, only the Vast Sea Daoist Lord would die!

This move worked against most half-immortals, but it still couldn’t deal with the Second Imperial Preceptor. Bringing up curses in front of the Karma Incipient Dao Fruit was simply a joke.

Destructive energy gathered in the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord’s hand. He clenched his fist and smashed his own head to pieces.

Transcendent Tribulation cultivators had self-healing abilities, but this destructive energy inherently countered healing. Unless one used the power of an Incipient Dao Fruit, self-recovery was impossible!

Contrary to the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord’s expectations, the Vast Sea Daoist Lord’s head did not explode. It was as if the latter hadn’t been affected by the Shared Life and Death curse.

The Vast Sea Daoist Lord chuckled but didn’t intend to explain.

“Immortal Fairy, what’s going on here?” Lu Yang was puzzled.

“It’s a pretty clever method. He did sustain the injury, but when he got struck, he used spatial power to hold his head together. It’s like smashing a watermelon and then gluing it back together. That way, being injured or not makes no difference.”

Lu Yang was amazed. He never thought the Incipient Dao Fruit could be used in this manner. No wonder Big Senior Sister said Ancestor Vast Sea could handle the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord.

None of those locked in fierce combat in the bamboo forest noticed a figure stealthily slipping into the Dao-Seeking Sect.

In truth, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy and Lu Yang had noticed but didn’t intervene.

Because that figure was heading toward Heaven’s Gate Peak.

~~~

“The Dao-Seeking Sect is really hard to deal with. Even His Excellency is entangled in a bitter battle,” the figure muttered quietly.

He was one of the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord’s aides, and his mission was to infiltrate the sect to find the Yu Emperor’s treasure.

This was originally a backup plan. After all, no one expected the Dao-Seeking Sect’s hidden strength to force the Great Yu Alliance into such an arduous battle.

Fortunately, the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord had devised strategies beforehand and prepared a contingency plan. If both sides reached an impasse, one person would sneak into the Dao-Seeking Sect to seize the Yu Emperor’s treasure while the sect’s interior was empty and vulnerable.

As long as we find the Yu Emperor’s immortal artifact, we can turn the tide!

He was a cultivator from the mid Great Yu era and a once-renowned Transcendent Tribulation cultivator with the title of “Yellow Springs Venerable Lord.” He had once submerged several large cities in the Yellow Springs, delighting in the grievous wails of those living beings.

The legends of the Nine-Netherworlds Creed contained records of the “Yellow Springs,” stating that souls after death must be cleansed in the Yellow Springs before entering the Nine-Netherworlds.

The Yellow Springs mentioned here originated from the Yellow Springs Venerable Lord’s deeds.

The Yellow Springs Venerable Lord had a natural talent for treasure hunting, surpassing even the Treasure-Seeking Mice of the Demon Region. The moment he stepped into the Dao-Seeking Sect, he sensed the aura of treasures.

The richness of the treasure aura was unlike anything he had ever encountered in his life.

“It’s definitely the Yu Emperor’s treasure!”

Suppressing his excitement, the Yellow Springs Venerable Lord followed the aura.

“This is the mountain. According to the intelligence, this place is called Heaven’s Gate Peak. It seems the Dao-Seeking Sect’s treasury is right here.

“Serves you right, Dao-Seeking Sect! You were originally a faction of Great Yu, yet you defected to Great Xia. Your destruction today is heavenly justice, inevitable divine punishment for your misdeeds!”

Halfway up the mountain, he bumped into a puppet carrying a hoe.

As Lu Yang often practiced with his sword on the mountain, the trees on Heaven’s Gate Peak had suffered severe losses. The puppet had no choice but to take on the important responsibility of replanting trees.

The puppet glanced at the Yellow Springs Venerable Lord, stopped in its tracks, and blocked his path.

“Get lost!” the Yellow Springs Venerable Lord said irritably, swatting at it with his hand.

A mere shabby puppet. It’s nothing.

Clang!

The Yellow Springs Venerable Lord’s hand slapped the puppet, producing a crisp metallic sound, but the puppet didn’t budge an inch.

His face was filled with disbelief as he cried out involuntarily, “A Transcendent Tribulation-level puppet?!”

The puppet looked down at the Yellow Springs Venerable Lord’s iron hand, then slowly raised its hoe.

Chapter 729: Why Insist on Seeking Your Own Death?

“Oh no!” The Yellow Springs Venerable Lord felt an ominous feeling welling within, as if the puppet wasn’t raising a hoe but a sharp heavenly saber.

“Yellow Springs Secret Art!”

As the hoe descended, the Yellow Springs Venerable Lord hastily employed a life-preserving secret art, transforming his entire body into Yellow Springs water.

The Yellow Springs water was split by the hoe. The two water spheres retreated backward and merged back into one before reforming into the Yellow Springs Venerable Lord’s figure.

“Huff, huff, huff...”

The Yellow Springs Venerable Lord looked at the puppet with lingering fear. It was just a swing of the hoe, yet it had forced me into a desperate situation and a life-and-death peril.

How could the Dao-Seeking Sect have a puppet of this level?

To his knowledge, even the Puppeteer Sect, one of Great Xia’s S-class sects and the most skilled in crafting puppets in the current age, couldn’t produce a puppet like the one before him.

Who exactly crafted it?!

The Yellow Springs Venerable Lord’s eyes flickered with a trace of fear. The Dao-Seeking Sect’s foundation is truly terrifying. Even while facing an invasion, they still have the capacity to guard their treasury with a Transcendent Tribulation-level puppet.

Soon, the fear in his eyes vanished, replaced by thick mockery. I’m not someone who can be scared off by a mere puppet. This puppet is made of a special material that is extremely hard; it’s difficult to dismantle it by brute force.

“But the gap between a puppet and a cultivator cannot be bridged by puppeteering techniques alone!

“I hereby establish the rule: [Within Heaven’s Gate Peak, spirit energy cannot be used to activate magical treasures.]”

Transcendent Tribulation cultivators possessed the ability to establish rules. No matter how brilliant the puppeteering techniques, they would hit walls everywhere when faced with the power of rules.

Puppets fell under the category of magical treasures. There were two ways to activate a puppet: one was to have a puppeteer control them secretly, and the other was to have the puppet move autonomously.

A Transcendent Tribulation-level puppet required the puppeteer to have cultivation minimally at the Fusion Stage.

If this puppet before me is controlled, the puppeteer definitely isn’t at the Transcendent Tribulation Stage.

If this puppeteer were at the Transcendent Tribulation Stage, they would control the puppet while also participating in the fight themselves, which isn’t happening.

If it is not controlled by a puppeteer, a puppet operating autonomously is merely an inanimate object and no match for me at all!

The wooden puppet was crafted based on a female appearance, but its creator had not carved any facial features.

It tilted its head slightly. Although it couldn’t display any expression, one could imagine a look of confusion on its face.

Bang!

The puppet punched the Yellow Springs Venerable Lord right in the face. It caught him off guard and knocked out two of his front teeth.

“How is this possible?!”

The Yellow Springs Venerable Lord was so flustered that he ignored his lost teeth. He was certain the established rule was active. Moreover, he had set a small range for the rule, such that it has strong binding power, preventing even himself from using magical treasures.

Yet this puppet can move freely!

The puppet clearly had no intention of explaining. It kicked the Yellow Springs Venerable Lord and sent him tumbling.

The Yellow Springs Venerable Lord’s gaze grew increasingly fierce. He had originally wanted to end the fight quickly. After all, he had secretly sneaked into the sect, and if he was discovered by the Dao-Seeking Sect, it could alert those in the bamboo forest, shifting the battlefield here.

But I can’t afford to care so much now.

“Netherworld specters and wraiths, the Yellow Springs ferry them, three sighs at the Naihe River of Forgetfulness!”

The Yellow Springs spawned, corroding the earth. Thousands of ghosts and evil spirits roamed, emitting resentful sighs. Their grievances soared skyward, nearly materializing. Heaven’s Gate Peak seemed to transform into a living hell.

The Yellow Springs Venerable Lord didn’t hold back. This was his ultimate move, and the method by which he had dominated an entire era with a proud smile. Cultivators of that time would fall into trepidation and despair upon hearing the words “Yellow Springs.”

This technique was too ostentatious. Whether it was disciples taking shelter in the Dao-Seeking Sect’s core areas or the elders fighting in the bamboo forest, they all noticed the commotion at Heaven’s Gate Peak.

At first, they grew tense, realizing an enemy had infiltrated. But when they saw the location was Heaven’s Gate Peak, they acted as if nothing had happened and continued engaging their current opponents.

The puppet appeared as if it hadn’t seen the Yellow Springs Venerable Lord’s move. Holding the hoe, it strode forward and stepped into the corrosive Yellow Springs without any damage to its feet.

The malevolent ghosts living in the Yellow Springs howled and swooped toward the puppet. But it simply swung the hoe, dispelling all ghosts and evil.

“How is this possible?!”

The Yellow Springs Venerable Lord was dumbfounded. This is my strongest move! The puppet can’t possibly be unscathed!

The puppet swung the hoe. Its movements were simple yet unavoidable. Each strike carried the terror of heaven collapsing and earth cracking. In no time, it had beaten the Yellow Springs Venerable Lord black and blue.

Seeing the hoe with the aura of death being raised again, the Yellow Springs Venerable Lord didn’t hesitate. Ignoring the side effects, he unleashed the Yellow Springs Secret Art once more and sped toward the summit of Heaven’s Gate Peak.

I can’t get tangled with it any longer. Only by finding the Yu Emperor’s immortal treasure can I find a way to break out of this situation!

The puppet watched the Yellow Springs Venerable Lord flee and did not pursue him.

“It’s right here!” The Yellow Springs Venerable Lord sensed an intensely rich treasure aura. It’s getting closer and closer!

Charging through a grove of trees, he followed the treasure aura to a cave. He punched the cave entrance open, and the treasure aura immediately spilled out. This was a peerless fragrance he had never smelled before!

The Yu Emperor’s treasure is here!

The Dao-Seeking Sect’s treasury was vast and comprehensive. The further in he went, the more precious the items became.

The Yellow Springs Venerable Lord ignored those Fusion and Transcendent Tribulation-grade treasures. He reached the deepest part of the treasury, where he saw immortal artifacts casually placed on the ground. His eyes were filled with avarice.

“The Immortal Dao Array Diagram, the Immortal-Exterminating Sword Array, Nine-Dragon Big Dipper Shield...”

Suddenly, as if he sensed something, he looked up at a fruit placed on a desk. His body began to tremble uncontrollably.
