As the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord’s aide, he had once seen him display his Incipient Dao Fruit. It was an ethereal fruit containing the Dao of longevity and myriad spells along with the power of time; it was infinitely profound and wondrous.

But the fruit on the desk was complete and not ethereal in the slightest. It was perfect and flawless.

The Myriad Spells Daoist Lord’s long sigh from that time was still etched in the Yellow Springs Venerable Lord’s memory.

“Only a solidified fruit is a true Dao Fruit. When will my fruit become complete?”

Now, a solidified, complete fruit lay before his eyes, yet immense panic surged within him.

Is this the legendary Dao Fruit?

Why is it here?

The immortal artifacts here were relics left by the Yu Emperor. Then what about this Dao Fruit?

Has the Yu Emperor really gone to the outside world?

Various doubts flooded his mind, accompanied by an indescribable sense of horror.

A long, drawn-out sigh sounded.

“Why insist on seeking your own death?”

The Yellow Springs Venerable Lord whirled around. At the cave entrance stood a female cultivator holding a cup. The aroma wafted through the air, seemingly encompassing the charm and flow of Dao.

This was freshly picked Wudao Enlightenment Tea from this year, also the highest-quality Wudao Enlightenment Tea in the world.

The female cultivator sipped her tea delicately, blowing away the Dao essence in the aroma, as if she hadn’t been the one who spoke just now.

The Yellow Springs Venerable Lord tried to speak, but found his body rigid and immobile like a clay statue. He could only watch helplessly as the female cultivator walked toward him step by step.

The female cultivator extended a finger and touched the Yellow Springs Venerable Lord’s forehead. His body dissipated bit by bit until it turned into nothingness.

Chapter 730: Would You Like to Get Up First?

“So the puppet I fight every day is at the Transcendent Tribulation Stage?!” Lu Yang was dumbfounded upon witnessing everything that transpired on Heaven’s Gate Peak through the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s immortal consciousness.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy giggled, unsurprised. “I told you long ago that the sect treasury is guarded.”

Lu Yang recalled the memory. Back when he went to Yun Zhi to ask for the patent royalties from the flying carriage, Yun Zhi took him to the treasury to get spirit stones, and he was worried that it was too easy to open the treasury door. Moreover, since Yun Zhi wasn’t always at Heaven’s Gate Peak, he felt the treasury was insecure.

At the time, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had reassured him about the treasury’s safety.

“Wait, you knew all along that the puppet was at the Transcendent Tribulation Stage, yet you never stopped me whenever I fought it?” Lu Yang asked with a stormy expression.

“You seemed to be enjoying the fights,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy said with schadenfreude.

I had done it on purpose.

~~~

High up in the air, the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord found the Vast Sea Daoist Lord an intractable opponent. After the sudden commotion from the Yellow Springs Venerable Lord on Heaven’s Gate Peak, everything fell silent, likely because he had already been murdered.

This implies that the Dao-Seeking Sect has other hidden experts. Continuing the battle is unwise.

Furthermore, the Vast Sea Daoist Lord was difficult to deal with; any direct attack toward him would be redirected.

The Myriad Spells Daoist Lord left a clone to restrain the Vast Sea Daoist Lord while he turned on his heels.

But before he could escape the Dao-Seeking Sect, he crashed into an invisible barrier with a solid thud.

“Spatial barrier?”

“Did you think the Dao-Seeking Sect is a place you can come and leave as you please?” As the Vast Sea Daoist Lord spoke, he performed a spatial slice, shredding the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord’s clone into smithereens.

The Myriad Spells Daoist Lord’s face was so dark that water could drip from it. It seems we’re destined to have a life-and-death battle today.

“The cosmos has no limits, Myriad Spells Return to One!” The Myriad Spells Daoist Lord accelerated time and transformed into a thousand-armed Buddha, effortlessly combining various attacks.

The five elements, yin and yang, reality and illusion, wind and lightning, souls and spirits—all manner of attacks were launched simultaneously. It was like a deity separating heaven and earth. The world shattered, and manifold energies that constituted the world overflowed, forming a tornado of spells!

Even a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator would die upon coming into contact with Myriad Spells Return to One!

He didn’t care about the Great Yu Alliance members’ lives—he was betting the Vast Sea Daoist Lord would care!

The Myriad Spells Daoist Lord bet correctly; the Vast Sea Daoist Lord indeed cared.

The Vast Sea Daoist Lord activated his Space Incipient Dao Fruit to absorb all the attacks into an alternate space.

This was the opportunity the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord seized!

The Vast Sea Daoist Lord wielded an Incipient Dao Fruit, not a full Dao Fruit, so the space he could open was limited. The Myriad Spells Daoist Lord refused to believe the Vast Sea Daoist Lord could block the vast number of attacks and still have the capacity to set up a spatial vortex around himself as defense.

“Die!”

The Myriad Spells Daoist Lord concentrated destructive energy at his fingertip and pierced through the Vast Sea Daoist Lord’s abdomen.

“Jumping around with time acceleration was so annoying. I’ve finally caught you now!”

The Vast Sea Daoist Lord’s icy voice rang out. The Myriad Spells Daoist Lord immediately felt a sense of foreboding and tried to pull his hand back to escape, but his arm was already anchored in the Vast Sea Daoist Lord’s abdomen and couldn’t be withdrawn!

The Myriad Spells Daoist Lord decisively severed his right hand and continuously used time acceleration to put distance between himself and the Vast Sea Daoist Lord.

“Too late!”

The Vast Sea Daoist Lord had already placed a spatial mark on the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord. No matter how fast the latter moved, he could catch up to him!

The Myriad Spells Daoist Lord needed time to heal his injury—an extremely short time that was less than a breath. However, the Vast Sea Daoist Lord didn’t even give him that bit of time, pursuing him relentlessly and forcing him into an utterly wretched state.

“Flesh and bones reborn, Lifespan Curse!” The Myriad Spells Daoist Lord yelled, removing the spatial mark. Once again, he used a curse technique to link his lifespan with the Vast Sea Daoist Lord’s, such that both of them would exhaust the same amount of lifespan!

This was a unique move that the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord had created. After all, others would find it useless even if they learned it.

One’s lifespan was closely related to one’s cultivation realm. If both parties’ cultivation realms were the same, there was no need for this move. If their cultivation realms differed, all the more was there no need for this move, since a lower-realm cultivator’s lifespan couldn’t possibly be longer than that of a higher-realm cultivator.

Only someone like the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord, who was born with the Longevity Immortal Physique and a long lifespan, could use this move against a cultivator of the same realm.

“Lifespan Acceleration!” The Myriad Spells Daoist Lord rapidly consumed his own lifespan. Under the curse’s effect, the Vast Sea Daoist Lord’s lifespan also drained rapidly.

In a contest of lifespan, the Vast Sea Daoist Lord certainly couldn’t outlast the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord.

“Spatial Collapse!”

Immense gravitational force appeared around the Vast Sea Daoist Lord and the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord, distorting time and slowing its flow to a crawl. The rapidly depleting lifespans now trickled away extremely slowly.

“Damn it.” The Myriad Spells Daoist Lord hadn’t anticipated this move.

“Just die!” The Vast Sea Daoist Lord attacked with his fists and feet, engaging in close combat.

While the Vast Sea Daoist Lord’s fist techniques were exceptional, they were ineffective in the face of the Vast Sea Daoist Lord’s spatial transfer.

Boom!

The Vast Sea Daoist Lord kicked the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord, sending him flying like a kite with a severed string.

Spotting Lu Yang, the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord’s eyes lit up, and he flew toward him. “Right, this kid has the Yu Emperor’s immortal sword!”

“Oh no!” The Vast Sea Daoist Lord suddenly realized the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord’s intention. But without the spatial mark, he couldn’t catch up.

Just as the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord thought he could seize the immortal sword, his body suddenly disobeyed him. He stumbled and fell to his knees with a thud before Lu Yang.

Everyone watched this scene in disbelief. Both the Dao-Seeking Sect and the Great Yu Alliance ceased fighting simultaneously, staring with eyes wide and mouths agape.

Without a doubt, it was the Everlasting Immortal Fairy controlling him.

Lu Yang was silent for a moment, then took a step to the left.

I don’t dare to accept a half-immortal kneeling to me.

The Myriad Spells Daoist Lord thought it was an incident and felt utterly humiliated. He turned left and lunged fiercely at Lu Yang in a bid to seize the immortal sword.

Right then, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy feared Lu Yang would get hurt and hastily made the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord stop.

The Myriad Spells Daoist Lord had just assumed a posture of a ferocious tiger descending the mountain when he was forced to halt. Due to inertia, his head hit the ground directly.

He was prostrate on the ground.

Lu Yang was silent again. The Myriad Spells Daoist Lord keeps paying respects; would it be impolite if I keep dodging?

“Uh, would you like to get up first?” Lu Yang suggested awkwardly.

Although our stances differ, he’s 200,000 years my senior after all, and his cultivation is also much higher.

The Myriad Spells Daoist Lord finally realized the previous occurrences weren’t accidents. Someone is definitely playing tricks and controlling me from behind the scenes!

Who is it?!

It’s an immortal! An immortal possessing a superior Dao Fruit to mine is in the Dao-Seeking Sect!

The Myriad Spells Daoist Lord wanted to flee, but the Everlasting Immortal Fairy assumed he still wanted to harm Lu Yang and directly commanded him not to move.

The Vast Sea Daoist Lord arrived and trapped the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord using spatial confinement. “Whew, finally settled.”

After an exhilarating battle and having captured the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord alive, the Vast Sea Daoist Lord’s confidence soared by leaps and bounds.

In battles between half-immortals, achieving victory is extremely difficult, and capturing the opponent alive is all the more so.

Chapter 731: Bountiful Harvest

It was extremely hard to decide the outcome in battles between half-immortals. Events such as the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s ten-day self-detonations and the Second Imperial Preceptor getting blasted for ten days were common.

Similarly, if left unchecked, a fight between the Vast Sea Daoist Lord and the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord could easily last eight or ten days.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s secret interference allowed this battle to conclude earlier.

However, the Vast Sea Daoist Lord was unaware of all this.

The Myriad Spells Daoist Lord struggled, but to no avail. The spatial confinement pinned him firmly within that space; without the Vast Sea Daoist Lord’s permission, escape was impossible.

Never had he imagined that he would encounter an immortal with a superior Dao Fruit in the Dao-Seeking Sect. Is the legendary Epoch Immortal here, or is the immortal who governs the “Undying” Dao Fruit here?

No matter the case, it indicates the Dao-Seeking Sect is incredibly terrifying.

At this moment, the way he looked at Lu Yang completely changed. With an immortal in the Dao-Seeking Sect, the immortal sword Lu Yang possesses can’t possibly have escaped the immortal’s notice.

But how could an immortal leave such a peerless immortal sword in the hands of a Nascent Soul cultivator?!

The answer is obvious—the immortal highly values Lu Yang, even bestowing him the immortal sword!

Lu Yang couldn’t help but feel that the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord was looking at him strangely, but he couldn’t pinpoint what exactly was odd.

The Great Yu Alliance wanted to flee, but the Dao-Seeking Sect wouldn’t let them. They had always believed in pursuing cornered enemies relentlessly instead of letting them off.

The Grand-Shifu Tang Shengyi fought especially fiercely. The other elders watching this scene were reminded of unpleasant childhood memories.

“Shifu’s combat skills seem much stronger than before.” First Elder transmitted an auditory message to his junior brothers and sister while smashing enemies with the Yellow Millet Dream Pillow.

“Absolutely. Looking at him now, he could probably take on two opponents by himself.”

“When did Shifu become so powerful?”

What the elders didn’t know was that while the Grand-Shifu guarded Incarceration Peak, he often spent his free time consulting the prisoners about combat techniques. The prisoners captured in the last two years were prominent figures like the Sixth Yu Emperor, Apex Transcendent Tribulation cultivators, half-immortals, and an Imperial Preceptor from the late Great Yu era—all legendary, battle-hardened powerhouses.

When the Grand-Shifu asked them questions, how could they dare hide anything? They naturally disclosed everything, and the Grand-Shifu’s combat skills improved rapidly.

“Spatial Cage!” The Vast Sea Daoist Lord activated his Incipient Dao Fruit to trap all the Great Yu Alliance cultivators within the bamboo forest. Not a single one could escape.

“Hahaha, trying to run? Do you think you can get away?”

After capturing the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord, the Vast Sea Daoist Lord’s confidence had skyrocketed. In the Dao-Seeking Sect, I am the strongest aside from Yun Zhi!

“Finally, it’s all settled.” Dai Bufan ended his fight and let out a long sigh. They had managed to tide through this crisis without mishap.

Who would have expected a perfectly normal disciple entrance trial to suddenly turn into a half-immortal battle, with both half-immortals even participating in the trials?

“With the imminent arrival of the Great Era, it appears all sorts of evil monsters are emerging. Previously, Junior Brother Lu and Junior Brother Meng were just unlucky to have coincidentally encountered high-level battles,” Dai Bufan murmured to himself.

“Junior Brother Lu, Junior Brother Meng, prepare to wrap up.”

Due to the emergency earlier, everyone participating in the third round was brought into the Dao-Seeking Sect. Among them, only Zhuang Ping, Zhou Xing’er, Gu Junye, and the Innate Daoist Priest had passed the trials.

Apart from Gu Junye and the Innate Daoist Priest, the other participants in the third round still looked shaken. Witnessing the Dao-Seeking Sect’s foundation and a half-immortal battle firsthand would frighten even cultivators out of their wits, much less mortals.

The Dao-Seeking Sect disciples escorted the eliminated candidates out of the sect. Their elders were overwhelmed with emotions upon seeing their juniors safe and sound.

They were sensible people. When the battle erupted, and they knew their juniors were at the center of it, they had already prepared for the worst, not expecting them to emerge unscathed. The joy of survival overshadowed the disappointment of failing the Dao-Seeking Sect’s selection.

None of the Dao-Seeking Sect’s four newly recruited disciples had elders accompanying them, so farewells weren’t a problem.

Zhuang Ping’s mother was imprisoned and couldn’t come.

Zhou Xing’er’s elders always looked down on her and wouldn’t come.

Gu Junye had come alone.

Nothing more needed to be said for the Innate Daoist Priest; the Dao-Seeking Sect was his home.

~~~

In the bamboo forest, all the Great Yu Alliance cultivators were rounded up. The Innate Daoist Priest also spotted two familiar Fusion cultivators—the very ones who had invited him to join the Great Yu Alliance. After he refused, they had informed the Chess-Observing True Lord about his possession of the Golden Cicada Shell.

“So they are from the Great Yu Alliance.” Realization dawned upon the Innate Daoist Priest. He didn’t expect the Great Yu Alliance to be captured so quickly.

Dealing with the Great Yu Alliance wasn’t the elders’ responsibility; the Grand-Shifu would handle it. Having observed all three rounds of the trials, the elders were secretly discussing the new batch of disciples through auditory messages.

“This Gu Junye fellow is not bad. He can become my disciple,” First Elder said with a smile. This was Dai Bufan’s idea. Both of them had a Water Spirit Root, so Dai Bufan could teach him. That would save me the effort as Shifu.

“Zhou Xing’er demonstrates considerable talent in planting. Coincidentally, I haven’t taken a disciple for years. How about nurturing one to look after my herb garden for me?” Grandpa Ba declared.

“Then Zhuang Ping shall go to me. This kid has a connection with Hongwen; it was Hongwen who assessed his character back then,” Fourth Elder stated with a smile, not minding that Zhuang Ping only had a Triple Spirit Root.

Of course, it was still too early to determine who would accept these disciples. Becoming master and disciple went two ways, requiring both the master’s approval and the disciple’s consent.

These three had just come to the Dao-Seeking Sect and didn’t know anyone. They would be given a month to decide who they would like to have as their shifu.

“What about the Founding Ancestor? Should he become my disciple?” Eighth Elder was eager, following the Innate Daoist Priest’s wish to be treated as an ordinary disciple.

“Are you really not afraid of Shifu breaking your legs?” Third Elder sighed and removed his armor.

At the mention of their shifu, even Eighth Elder, who was proficient in all sorts of scams and deception, grew fearful.

The matter with the Innate Daoist Priest was an intractable issue. After asking around, none of the elders dared to accept him as a disciple, afraid their shifu would casually throw them into Incarceration Peak.

The eight elders didn’t dare, but someone else did.

That person strode toward the Innate Daoist Priest. “Qi Tong, are you willing to cultivate with me?”

The speaker held immense weight in the Dao-Seeking Sect. It was none other than the Vast Sea Daoist Lord.

Eighth Elder, “...”

Those in the dark looked enviously at the Innate Daoist Priest, thinking he had received a tremendous fortuitous opportunity to be accepted as a disciple by a half-immortal.

Those in the know experienced a range of complicated feelings. They were astonished that the Resurgence Ancestor was still alive, and were even more surprised by how clear his motives were.

“I’m willing!” The Innate Daoist Priest didn’t care who his shifu was. Having a peaceful environment for cultivation was enough for him.

Overall, the Dao-Seeking Sect had a bountiful harvest today. Not only did they recruit four new disciples, but they also gained one half-immortal, five Transcendent Tribulation cultivators, and over twenty Fusion cultivators to join Incarceration Peak.

A happy ending for everyone. A cause for celebration.

Chapter 732: Zhu Tian: Why Have So Many Immortals Suddenly Popped Up?

The great battle that unfolded at the Dao-Seeking Sect couldn’t be concealed; the disciples participating in the entrance trials and their family members had all witnessed it.

Soon, the news spread through every street and alley.

“Heavens, even the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord has emerged! He’s a peerless genius from the legends! Who would have thought he’d already become a half-immortal?!”

“And his gang of followers—five Transcendent Tribulation cultivators and over twenty Fusion cultivators! Good grief, that’s nearly half the strength of the Demon Region!”

“That’s nothing. The most terrifying thing is that they ambushed the Dao-Seeking Sect but ended up being captured by them instead!”

Previously, people thought the Dao-Seeking Sect only had one Transcendent Tribulation cultivator and a method comparable to one—the standard for an immortal sect. Who could have imagined the Dao-Seeking Sect possessed such a terrifying foundation?

After this battle, the Dao-Seeking Sect firmly established its position as the head of the Five Great Immortal Sects.

“The Dao-Seeking Sect’s Resurgence Ancestor from fifty thousand years ago, the Vast Sea Daoist Lord, is also still alive! The world thought he was at the Transcendent Tribulation Stage, but he had secretly advanced to a half-immortal!”

“The Dao-Seeking Sect is truly fearsome.”

“I have a nephew who took part in the Dao-Seeking Sect’s entrance trials and happened to witness the entire process. There’s one detail no one has mentioned yet.”

“What detail? Please share, Fellow Daoist.”

“You know of Prodigy Lu Yang, right?”

“Who hasn’t heard of Lu Yang? He's a cultivator who challenged Divine Transfiguration cultivators at the Foundation Establishment stage—a peerless genius!”

“That’s not all. According to my nephew, after the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord was defeated, he knelt before Lu Yang. However, Lu Yang didn’t want to be bowed to and shifted a step to the left. Despite that, the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord persisted and adjusted his position, kowtowing to Lu Yang directly with impeccable posture!”

“What? A half-immortal knelt to Lu Yang?! How is that possible?!”

“I didn’t want to believe it either, but my nephew saw it with his own eyes. That’s the truth!”

The Taciturn Daoist Priest and Chieftain Jin were drinking and eating nearby, where they overheard the entire discussion.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest was astonished. “Founding Ancestor Vast Sea is still alive?” I am the sect leader, yet I wasn’t aware of this matter, only finding out about it through others’ discussions.

Chieftain Jin was also surprised. He never expected the Dao-Seeking Sect to have a half-immortal too. Looking at the current situation, who knows how many mighty figures are hiding in the shadows? I hope the Little Ancestor will be resolved to work hard and make the Qiongqi Tribe rank within the top ten in the upcoming Battle of the Great Era.

He encouraged himself, “I can’t slack off either.” Having followed the Taciturn Daoist Priest for most of this year, he had undergone a complete transformation.

“Big Brother Taciturn, who are we scamming next?”

~~~

Demon Region, Demon City.

In an ancient-style palace, Zhu Tian stared blankly at the intelligence report handed to him by a subordinate.

“This isn’t right. I waited over two hundred years without a single half-immortal appearing. Why are half-immortals popping out of the ground like radishes as soon as I become the ruler of the Demon Region?

“Setting aside Jiang Lianyi, the Nightmare Supreme Lord, the Void Emptiness Supreme Lord, the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord, the Vast Sea Daoist Lord... why have so many half-immortals suddenly appeared?”

Didn’t I slumber from the ancient era until now because I wanted to reign supreme and enjoy the pleasures of absolute authority in an era without half-immortals?

If I had known this era would be so lively, I might as well have kept sleeping until the next era. Why did I have to come to join the fray in this era?

“Judging by how lively things are, I’m afraid even immortals may make an appearance... Oh wait, no, Big Brother Lu Yang’s mental space already houses one immortal.”

Zhu Tian grimaced, feeling extremely troubled. “Even if I’m the number one below immortals, I’m afraid I won’t fare well in the Battle of the Great Era.

“Is it too late to go back to slumber now?”

~~~

Incarceration Peak had never been as bustling as it was today. In the past, prisoners were captured one by one. But today was different. A total of thirty individuals joined the Incarceration Peak family.

If Incarceration Peak were considered a faction, it would be a top-tier force on par with the Demon Region.

When the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord entered Incarceration Peak, his pupils constricted sharply as if he had seen a ghost.

Wu Youdao, the Nightmare Supreme Lord, and the Void Supreme Lord were all here, along with many other familiar Great Yu cultivators.

No, not just many familiar ones—every Great Yu cultivator I know who has slept until now is here!

When and how were all these people captured and brought here?!

Especially Wu Youdao—if he’s here, where is Jin Buqun?

Jin Buqun was the Second Imperial Preceptor.

The Nightmare Supreme Lord and the Void Emptiness Supreme Lord are both here. Weren’t they captured by the ancient Heavenly Court...? Could it be that the Dao-Seeking Sect is the public identity of the ancient Heavenly Court?

One terrifying theory after another surfaced, becoming more horrifying the more he mulled over them.

The Myriad Spells Daoist Lord knew his defeat at the Dao-Seeking Sect wasn’t unjustified. The Dao-Seeking Sect’s strength far exceeds what has been displayed!

The Vast Sea Daoist Lord escorted the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord and the others into Incarceration Peak and used his Incipient Dao Fruit to reinforce each prison cell.

“Then I’ll leave the rest to you.” The Vast Sea Daoist Lord called out toward the entrance of Incarceration Peak and strode away.

The Myriad Spells Daoist Lord looked back, wanting to see who the Vast Sea Daoist Lord was speaking to.

At the entrance stood two figures, one male and one female, both of whom the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord recognized.

Lu Yang and Yun Zhi.

Why are these two here?

Wait! The Myriad Spells Daoist Lord recalled the heart devil Yun Zhi from the second round of the trials. If Yun Zhi wasn’t Gu Junye’s heart devil but the Vast Sea Daoist Lord’s, then exactly what cultivation realm has Yun Zhi reached to become his heart devil?!

And why is this Lu Yang fellow here?

Yun Zhi didn’t give the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord any time to contemplate, tossing him into a room isolated from external detection.

“Heh, don’t dream of getting any information from me...”

Yun Zhi cupped her fists toward Lu Yang. “Senior, please step in.”

“Aiya, you still need to rely on this immortal in the end.”

A figure that made the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord’s blood run cold emerged. He felt the pressure originate from the bottom of his soul. It was the absolute control of a superior entity over a lesser being.

An immortal!

In a superior position than mine—the wielder of the Undying Dao Fruit!

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy gleefully darted out from within Lu Yang and tapped the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord between his eyebrows. “This immortal commands you: you must answer all questions in full without lying.”

“Yes.” The Myriad Spells Daoist Lord’s mouth moved against his will.

“You can start asking him now.”

“Many thanks for your assistance, Senior.”

“Which faction do you come from?”

“We come from the Great Yu Alliance. I am the Alliance Leader.”

“When did you awake?”

“I possess the Longevity Immortal Physique and did not slumber. I have lived continuously from the early Great Yu era until now.”

“Why did you attack our Dao-Seeking Sect?”

“For the Yu Emperor Wu Yao’s immortal treasure. I saw Lu Yang holding Wu Yao’s immortal sword and suspected the Dao-Seeking Sect was in possession of his other treasures. If I obtain an immortal artifact, my strength will increase significantly. That was why I devised a plan to infiltrate the sect and coordinate from the inside and the outside to conquer it.”

Oh crap, Lu Yang thought. So it was I who attracted them. I can’t let Senior Brother Dai find out; it’d ruin my image in his heart.

Yun Zhi furrowed her brow slightly, somewhat baffled. “From where did you learn that I killed Wu Yao and obtained all his treasures?”

“What?!” The Myriad Spells Daoist Lord’s eyes widened abruptly. He was so flabbergasted and rendered speechless, as if he had been struck by lightning. It took him some time to process the information.

Wu Yao is dead? And you killed him?

If I had known this, I would have had to be kicked in the head by a donkey to come to your Dao-Seeking Sect!

Chapter 733: Question and Answer

The Myriad Spells Daoist Lord wished he could become an immortal right there and then, condense the Longevity Dao Fruit, reverse time, return to yesterday, and resolutely refuse to ever enter the Dao-Seeking Sect.

What kind of damned place is the Dao-Seeking Sect? Despite living for two hundred thousand years, this is my first time hearing of an immortal getting killed!

Since Yun Zhi could eliminate Wu Yao, she must be an immortal.

And this unknown female who possesses the Undying Dao Fruit is also an immortal.

That makes two immortals in the Dao-Seeking Sect.

With this kind of strength, why bother being one of the Five Great Immortal Sects? Why not just replace Great Xia outright?

“Replace Great Xia... that seems feasible too,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy commented, stroking her chin as she seriously considered the idea.

Isn’t it said that each dynasty can only last one hundred thousand years? It happens to be the transition period now. I can follow the trend of the times, join forces with Lass Yun to unify the Central Continent, and become the emperor.

“Lu Yang, what do you think about this immortal establishing a Great Bean (Dou) Dynasty?

“This immortal will be the Dou Emperor then.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy counted on her fingers. “We can take turns becoming the emperor. Lass Yun will be the second Dou Emperor, you’ll be the third, and you can let anyone you want be the fourth.”

Lu Yang, “...”

Immortal Fairy, your naming sense is, as always, truly... indescribable.

Acting as a sycophantic minister, Lu Yang lavished praise upon the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. “The Immortal Fairy is remarkable! Abandoning bloodline succession in favor of an abdication system and allowing the competent to rise—this is something Great Qian, Great Yu, and Great Xia never achieved. This act will surely make your name resonate through the ages and be revered by later generations, establishing you as a wise emperor of all time!”

“Of course, this immortal is remarkable.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy put her hands on her hips and tilted her chin up slightly, her visage tinged with pride.

Yun Zhi ignored the insincere Lu Yang and the Everlasting Immortal Fairy who was nearly floating with pride and continued questioning. “With Wu Yao’s treasure in the Dao-Seeking Sect, you should have easily deduced that someone in the sect was capable of killing him. What caused you to exclude that possibility?”

“I thought the Yu Emperor had left this world and gone to the world outside the Box. I assumed your Dao-Seeking Sect members had merely been lucky to stumble across his relics.”

“The Yu Emperor had a way to leave this world?!” Lu Yang was astonished. The World Box was jointly forged by the Four Ancient Immortals to trap the mastermind behind the scenes. Even someone as powerful as the mastermind couldn’t leave. How did the Yu Emperor do it?

“He likely did. Over these two hundred thousand years, I met the Yu Emperor multiple times. Since I was considered his junior and had no conflicting interests with him, his attitude toward me was rather friendly. He revealed to me his desire to go to the external world.

“His Dao Fruit was the Replacement Dao Fruit, which revolves around exchange. Anything that belonged to him could be used as a bargaining chip.

“I suspect the reason he allowed the Great Yu Dynasty to fall was that he wanted to sacrifice it. In fact, it could be that he didn’t simply let it collapse but accelerated its demise. The concurrent natural and man-made disasters and the abject misery of the people in the late Great Yu era might not have been coincidental. Perhaps he first sacrificed the Great Yu Dynasty’s fortune, then the dynasty itself.

“In short, his idea was to sacrifice the Great Yu Dynasty in exchange for a method to reach the external world.

“I originally thought he had gone to the external world after that. But during the Great Yu era, I detected traces of his activity twice, though I never saw him.

“Nineteen years ago, an intense aura suddenly appeared in Yu Province—it belonged to the Yu Emperor. The aura vanished in an instant, and the change in its aura was unusual, so I surmised the Yu Emperor had left this world.”

“Yu Province?” Yun Zhi nodded. This roughly matched the location and process of her battle with the ancient immortal.

If the person I exchanged blows with was indeed the Yu Emperor, he might really have used that opportunity to discard his Dao Fruit, sacrifice himself, and fake his death to escape to the external world.

At that time, Wu Yao had tried to corrupt the power of the national fortune. This power was connected to millions of civilians; regardless of whether his attempt succeeded, it would shake the karma of all civilians under heaven. Realizing the dire situation, Yun Zhi had no choice but to go all out.

That battle concluded quickly. Yun Zhi was also uncertain whether Wu Yao had died or escaped to the external world.

But it doesn’t make much difference. The result in both cases is the removal of this Yu Emperor as a variable.

Lu Yang was stunned.

Nineteen years ago?

Wasn’t that precisely when I had transmigrated here after my death?

Holy crap, could my previous life have been in the external world, and you, Wu Yao, replaced yourself out and replaced me in?

“By the way, Immortal Fairy, can you ask the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord if he ever felt a Dao Fruit suppression before? We can use this piece of information to determine if the Epoch Immortal is still alive.” Lu Yang remembered another matter.

The Longevity Dao Fruit had two Dao Fruits superior to it: the Everlasting Dao Fruit and the Epoch Dao Fruit.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy cast the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord a disdainful glance. “That won’t work. He hasn’t fully mastered his Longevity Incipient Dao Fruit and can’t sense the suppression from a superior Dao Fruit. You might have a better chance with that individual with the Longevity Immortal Physique in the ancient era.”

“He has lived two hundred thousand years and still hasn’t fully mastered it?” Lu Yang was shocked. The Myriad Spells Daoist Lord didn’t just live for two hundred thousand years; he also accelerated his cultivation process with his Longevity Immortal Physique.

“I told you, the key to mastering an Incipient Dao Fruit is comprehension, not piling up time. Those with poor comprehension can’t become immortals even if they live a million years.”

“Do you know the whereabouts of the Four Ancient Immortals?” Yun Zhi asked directly.

The Myriad Spells Daoist Lord shook his head. “No, I don’t know.”

“There is an immortal-tier great array around the sun that prevents anyone from approaching it. Do you know who created this array?”

The Myriad Spells Daoist Lord showed a strange expression; he clearly knew the inside story. “There are two immortal-tier great arrays around the sun. The first was left by the First Qian Emperor. He claimed to have established a new order upon the ancient ruins. Having lofty aspirations, he firmly believed that even the sun and moon in the sky belonged to him. He forbade anyone from approaching and thus set up the first immortal-tier great array.

“After Great Qian was destroyed and Wu Yao established the Great Yu Dynasty, he repeatedly tried to approach the sun to observe the power of the sun and moon. However, he couldn’t break through the array left by the First Qian Emperor.

“In his fury, he set up another immortal-tier great array. That way, the First Qian Emperor couldn’t obtain the sun either.”

Lu Yang, “...”

Do you two founding emperors have a screw loose?

“How many immortals were born in the Great Yu era?”

“Two. One was the Yu Emperor Wu Yao, and the other was the Imperial Preceptor Guan Shanhai.”

“The First Imperial Preceptor Guan Shanhai?”

“Yes. Both of them became immortals with the help of their nation-founding ceremonies.”

“Do you know what the Imperial Preceptor Guan Shanhai’s Dao Fruit was?”

“No, I don’t.”

“How many immortals were born in the Great Qian era?”

“To my knowledge, there was only the First Qian Emperor. After all, he left an immortal-tier great array on the sun. As for whether anyone else became an immortal, I don’t know.”

“Last question: do you know of the Ember Legacy Dynasty?” Yun Zhi asked calmly.

Upon hearing this, the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord’s pupils constricted sharply.

Chapter 734: The Vanished Ember Legacy Dynasty

“You know of the Ember Legacy Dynasty too?!”

“Too?” Yun Zhi realized the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord knew about the Ember Legacy Dynasty.

Ever since learning of the Ember Legacy Dynasty’s existence from the Everlasting Secret Domain, Yun Zhi had tapped into all her connections to inquire about it. But neither the First Xia Emperor Jiang Ping’an nor the recently captured Nightmare Supreme Lord and the Void Emptiness Supreme Lord had heard of the Ember Legacy Dynasty.

This had once caused Yun Zhi to doubt the dynasty’s existence.

Finally, she encountered someone who knew about the Ember Legacy Dynasty.

“This place of yours is secure, right? Besides you three, no one else will know what I’ve said, right?” The Myriad Spells Daoist Lord had to disclose everything he knew under the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s control.

“Of course,” Yun Zhi replied.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy and Lu Yang concurred. With the three of them present, this was the safest place under heaven.

If not for the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s presence, the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord would never have been willing to speak of the Ember Legacy Dynasty. The fact that he dared discuss matters regarding Wu Yao with his aides but never mentioned the Ember Legacy Dynasty spoke volumes.

Considering there are two immortals here—one who killed the Yu Emperor and one who possesses the Undying Dao Fruit—I should be able to rest assured.

“Initially, I didn’t know of the Ember Legacy Dynasty’s existence either. I’m not trying to brag, but I have visited every scripture library in the world, including the one in Great Yu’s imperial palace, to learn numerous spells.

“Not a single book mentioned the Ember Legacy Dynasty.

“It wasn’t until I became a half-immortal, faked my death, and went into hiding that I pieced together clues from remnants in secret domains, hints dropped by Wu Yao, and murals in dilapidated temples. That was when I learned of the Ember Legacy Dynasty.

“But when I returned to those secret domains containing clues about the Ember Legacy Dynasty, I found that they had been damaged along with the dilapidated temples.”

Lu Yang frowned. “When exactly was the Ember Legacy Dynasty established?”

“After the ancient era, before the Great Qian Dynasty.”

“What?!” Lu Yang was astonished. A dynasty was established during that period?

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy isn’t aware of the Ember Legacy Dynasty’s existence. Does that mean it was established after the four immortals sealed off the world?

“People say an immortal battle occurred in ancient times, where the stars were refined into continents. From then on, the legacies were severed, and even the ancient language was lost. It was upon the ancient ruins that the First Qian Emperor established the Great Qian Dynasty.

“In fact, this is a mistaken belief.

“After the ancient immortals refined the stars into continents, the Ember Legacy Dynasty was established, and it used the ancient language. After one hundred thousand years, the dynasty perished.

“The reason for its fall is unknown, but one thing is certain—someone deliberately erased all traces of the Ember Legacy Dynasty.

“And that someone was an immortal!

“That immortal erased all evidence of the Ember Legacy Dynasty’s existence—buildings, mortals, cultivators, books, and even the language... everything was gone.

“It was as if they wanted to sever everything related to the Ember Legacy Dynasty. Anyone who knew of the dynasty’s existence risked being eliminated by that immortal.

“In the late Great Yu era, I befriended another half-immortal with the Daoist title Wooden Seal Savant, and he also knew of the Ember Legacy Dynasty. Our original plan was to establish the Great Yu Alliance together. He didn’t have the Longevity Immortal Physique, so he chose to slumber. We agreed that I would wake him up when the Great Era arrives.

“But to my surprise, he perished before the Great Era even began.

“Every five thousand years, I would check on the Wooden Seal Savant’s condition. Thirty thousand years ago, I went to his cave domain as usual. But when I arrived, I found him dead, with his chest pierced right through!”

The Myriad Spells Daoist Lord’s voice quivered. “There were no signs of a struggle. Even though he was in slumber, if someone had tried to ambush him, his instincts would have sensed the danger, and he would have risen to fight. Even if he was outmatched, he shouldn’t have been killed in one blow.

“His killer wasn’t a half-immortal but an immortal!”

At this point, the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord showed a fearful expression. The Wooden Seal Savant’s demise had left a deep psychological trauma in him. “This is why I repeatedly asked you whether this place is safe to confirm no one else would eavesdrop. Once that immortal learns of what was said here, my fate would be grim too.”

“So that’s how it is,” Yun Zhi mused. She never expected such hidden circumstances behind the Ember Legacy Dynasty’s existence.

That immortal who went to great lengths to conceal the dynasty’s existence is likely the true reason the ancient legacies were broken.

At first, Yun Zhi couldn’t find any information about the Ember Legacy Dynasty and had assumed it had vanished for the same reason as the Everlasting Immortal Fairy—erased by the mastermind with some special method.

But judging from things now, the reason for its thorough disappearance is someone else.

“What is the relationship between the Ember Legacy Dynasty and the Four Ancient Immortals?” Yun Zhi asked. She remembered there were ruins of the Ember Legacy Dynasty with an androgynous statue of the Everlasting Immortal in the Everlasting Secret Domain.

The Myriad Spells Daoist Lord replied cautiously, “I saw a mural in a dilapidated temple. It was severely damaged, and I could only make out that it depicted the Ember Legacy Dynasty’s founding, with four imposing figures carved on it. This is only my speculation, but I speculate that the Ember Legacy Dynasty was jointly established by the Four Ancient Immortals.” Uncertain of Yun Zhi and the other two’s stance toward the ancient immortals, he emphasized it was merely speculation.

Judging by this trio’s lack of knowledge of the Ember Legacy Dynasty, the members of their ancient Heavenly Court likely entered collective slumber before the dynasty’s founding and only recently awakened.

Wait, that’s not right either. Two of these three are immortals; is there any need for them to slumber?

The Myriad Spells Daoist Lord felt a chill run down his spine as a bold conjecture struck him. Could your ancient Heavenly Court be fake?

He dared not continue this line of thought, fearing he would be silenced. He even wanted to slap himself. Why do you have to be so clever and think so much?!

“The Four Ancient Immortals founded the Ember Legacy Dynasty... an immortal who erased the dynasty’s existence... Could this be related to the Epoch Immortal’s fall?” Lu Yang mumbled. If so, this unknown immortal’s power is likely extremely terrifying.

“What? The Epoch Immortal fell?” The Myriad Spells Daoist Lord perked up upon hearing Lu Yang’s murmur.

He was immediately met with unfriendly looks from Lu Yang and the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, and he laughed awkwardly.

“What was his purpose in concealing the Ember Legacy Dynasty’s existence?” Yun Zhi was puzzled. Does the dynasty hold some indescribable secret?

Yun Zhi hadn’t expected the matter of the Ember Legacy Dynasty to involve another immortal, and a ruthless one at that.

She glanced at Lu Yang and suddenly remembered he was only at the Nascent Soul Stage, not yet the time for him to know about immortal-level gambits. “Little Junior Brother, leave the matter of the Ember Legacy Dynasty to me. Don’t get yourself involved.”

Lu Yang scratched his head. Is Big Senior Sister overestimating me? I’m just an Intermediate Double Infants cultivator. Even if I want to investigate the Ember Legacy Dynasty, my cultivation level wouldn’t allow it.

Chapter 735: The Popular Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou

Lu Yang felt that the matter of the Ember Legacy Dynasty sounded extremely dangerous.

The Wooden Seal Savant was sleeping peacefully, yet he was killed in his sleep just because he knew about the Ember Legacy Dynasty.

Nowadays, no one in the cultivation knows about the dynasty. I can also imagine that immortal’s methods weren’t gentle, likely killing everyone who was in the know, which resulted in the thorough erasure of the Ember Legacy Dynasty.

As the saying goes, a wise man doesn’t stand under a collapsing wall. Naturally, I must stay as far away as I can.

“But what indescribable secrets does the Ember Legacy Dynasty hold?” Lu Yang couldn’t figure it out. He had been aware of its existence for a long time, but no great fortuitous opportunity or terror had befallen him.

“Strange.”

“Little Junior Brother, your focus should be on cultivation now. Do not involve yourself in matters of immortals.” Yun Zhi hauled Lu Yang out of Incarceration Peak to prevent him from learning too much.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy snickered. This demonstrates who holds a higher place in Lass Yun’s heart.

“Oh, and Senior, you go out too.” Yun Zhi chased the Everlasting Immortal Fairy out as well. Given her nature, she’d probably turn around and dump everything she learned onto Little Junior Brother.

With the important questions done, the only thing left was ascertaining the veracity of the answers. After asking the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord, they could cross-check it with his aides later.

“The Ember Legacy Dynasty existed for one hundred thousand years, which is to say that this immortal has been dead for four hundred thousand years?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy felt she had suddenly aged another one hundred thousand years.

“Immortal Fairy, your point of focus seems a bit different from the others’.”

As the two spoke, they ran into the Vast Sea Daoist Lord, who was heading deeper into the Dao-Seeking Sect.

“Senior Vast Sea, what are you doing?”

“Don’t tell anyone you saw me,” the Vast Sea Daoist Lord hastily muttered as he continued to fly inward.

Lu Yang was puzzled as to why the Vast Sea Daoist Lord appeared to be in a hurry. Only when he reached the Nine Peaks of the Dao-Seeking Sect did he discover the reason.

While he and Yun Zhi were interrogating the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord, various major sects had sent visitation requests, hoping to visit the Dao-Seeking Sect and witness the legendary Vast Sea Daoist Lord.

Representatives from the Nine Great S-Class Sects and the other four Great Immortal Sects had arrived, making the Dao-Seeking Sect exceptionally lively. After all, chances to meet a half-immortal were rare. Not everyone was like Lu Yang, who had an immortal inside him and ran into half-immortals when he went out.

The Vast Sea Daoist Lord was probably hiding deep within the Dao-Seeking Sect because he didn’t want to meet so many people.

Since the Taciturn Daoist Priest was often away and Yun Zhi, the person-in-charge, was at Incarceration Peak, First Elder had no choice but to take charge and host the guests.

“Founding Ancestor Vast Sea is currently in seclusion. Everyone, you may leave your gifts and return to wherever you came from.” First Elder spoke politely and with proper etiquette, fully displaying the deportment of a representative from a major sect.

Ever since First Elder learned that the Vast Sea Daoist Lord was alive, his backbone had straightened considerably. In the past, he wouldn’t have dared speak like this even if he was on home turf.

The facts proved that the Grand-Shifu made the right decision by choosing not to inform the Dao-Seeking Sect’s higher-ups that the Vast Sea Daoist Lord was still alive.

The visitors from the various major sects fumed, blowing their beards and scowling with eyes wide, but they dared not cause a scene.

~~~

“Old Lu, over here!” Lu Yang heard Meng Jingzhou’s voice and looked up to see the latter on the second floor of the Hundred Fragrance Restaurant, beckoning to him like a brothel courtesan.

Lu Yang went upstairs and saw many familiar faces.

“Lan Ting, Bai Ming, Yan Tianzhi, all of you came too,” Lu Yang greeted them with a smile. The major sects had also brought their outstanding juniors.

Man Gu, Tao Yaoye, Li Haoran, and Meng JIngzhou were also present as the Dao-Seeking Sect’s outstanding juniors.

“Your Dao-Seeking Sect has been making a splash.” Bai Ming laughed and smacked Lu Yang’s shoulder lightly, full of envy. All he had heard on his journey here were discussions about the Dao-Seeking Sect.

“It’s just luck, all luck.” Lu Yang smiled modestly.

“It’s lucky for us that you’re only making waves now. If it had been a few days earlier, I’m afraid those who wanted to join our sect would have flocked to yours instead.”

The Five-Elements Sect had just finished recruiting disciples a few days ago.

“The same goes for the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace. When my senior and junior sisters went to assess the characters of the mortals and informed them they could join us, many mentioned they wanted to join the Dao-Seeking Sect and become your junior sister, Senior Brother Lu Yang.” Lan Ting’s tone carried a hint of resentment.

If it weren’t for our earnest persuasion, this year’s intake would likely have been less than half of previous years.

Tao Yaoye suddenly felt a strong sense of crisis.

“Were there any who wanted to become my junior sister?” Meng Jingzhou asked, pointing at himself.

Lan Ting’s expression turned strange as she hesitantly nodded. “There were some too.”

Meng Jingzhou was elated, thinking his charm was not inferior to Lu Yang’s.

“Senior Brother Meng, everyone outside knows your identity as the Eldest Young Master of the Meng Family. Your story of remaining unflustered despite having beauties in your embrace and your single-minded devotion to pursuing immortality has also spread.”

“So?”

“So those young ladies privately call you the ‘Aloof and Noble Buddha Scion of the Imperial City’ and want to become the Buddha Scion’s wife.

Meng Jingzhou’s face turned dark.

Despite having been silent all this time, Yan Tianzhi couldn’t hold back a giggle. His contagious laughter soon got everyone laughing.

“We’re all at the Intermediate Nascent Soul Stage now, right? How about we find a place to spar?” Bai Ming suggested they had eaten and drunk their fill.

“Let’s spar then.” Everyone was at an age where they enjoyed combat and readily agreed.

~~~

News that Lu Yang and the others would be fighting on the arena stage spread quickly. Lu Yang’s reputation was far too resounding. Even among the numerous talents in the Dao-Seeking Sect, his unique feats stood peerless.

“Our sect is going to fight other immortal sects!”

“Really? Who’s fighting?”

“Senior Brother Lu, Senior Brother Meng, Senior Brother Li, Senior Brother Man, and Senior Sister Tao.”

“So many people!”

“Quick, quick! We’ll miss it if we’re too late.”

The area around the arena stage was packed, and the onlookers’ eyes were full of excitement.

The newly recruited disciples—Zhuang Ping, Zhou Xing’er, Gu Junye, and the Innate Daoist Priest—had also come to watch.

“Well, who’s fighting whom?”

“Junior Sister Lan Ting, how about you and I have a match?” Tao Yaoye took the initiative to approach Lan Ting, holding a red paper umbrella with half her face shrouded in shadows.

“Sure. Please go easy on me then, Junior Sister Tao.”

“Barbarian Tribe?”

“Yes.”

“Then it’s us two.” Yan Tianzhi was concise. Their Five-Elements Sect’s battle tattoo cultivation method originated from ancient tribes. With an actual Ancient Barbarian like Man Gu here, how could his desire for battle not surge?

“Junior Brother Li Haoran, you don’t seem to have much of a reputation outside. I wonder how your methods are?” Bai Ming smiled. Both Man Gu and Tao Yaoye were famous in the outside world, but Li Haoran was an exception—he was never seen taking action in public, as if he didn’t exist.

“You’ll know once you try.” Li Haoran wasn’t afraid of Bai Ming. He was suspected of possessing a Reincarnation Incipient Dao Fruit, and his origins were unclear. If he left the Dao-Seeking Sect, he would likely draw unwanted attention. This was why he didn’t have a prominent reputation.

But my reputation doesn’t equate to my combat skills.

“So, it’s just the two of us left?” Lu Yang didn’t expect the matchups to be decided so quickly.

Only he and Meng Jingzhou remained on the field.

Chapter 736: Contests

“Old Lu, don’t worry, I won’t make your defeat too embarrassing.” Meng Jingzhou valued their brotherhood and promised to show Lu Yang some mercy to maintain his dignity.

Lu Yang’s face darkened. Meng Jingzhou, you really have no shame! I can’t use my Seven Star Sword Set or Village in Palm. Do you want me to blast you with a mouthful of Three Flavor True Fire?

The Seven Sword Star Set and Village in Palm were moves he had used under the identity of Young Creed Leader Lu, so he couldn’t deploy them as Lu Yang in public. The Immortal-Exterminating Sword Array was also reserved for Young Creed Leader Lu and couldn’t be brought out.

If his opponent were another cultivator of the same level, Lu Yang was confident he could win without resorting to those trump cards.

But it was different against Meng Jingzhou. He had no chance if he didn’t get serious.

“Then I’ll make a compromise—I assure you I won’t use the Single’s Curse Fist. How’s that?” Meng Jingzhou proposed magnanimously.

Lu Yang suspected no one dared to fight Meng Jingzhou because no one dared to risk being hit by the Single’s Curse Fist. Getting struck would mean suffering a fate as tragic as Meng Jingzhou’s for the rest of their lives.

Of course, Lu Yang wasn’t much better; his Lu-Style Arhat Fist was equally fearsome.

“...How about you don’t make a compromise? Try using it on me. Let’s see whose fate is tougher.” Having survived numerous immortal trials, Lu Yang refused to believe the Single’s Curse Fist could harm him.

Meng Jingzhou pretended not to hear him.

I’m not stupid. This grandson Lu Yang stirs up trouble all the time and encounters endless fortuitous opportunities. Who knows if he might form a marriage bond with a half-immortal or an immortal one day? I dare not use the Single’s Curse Fist on him.

“Old Lu, if you don’t speak, I’ll take it as you’ve agreed to our fight!” Meng Jingzhou smirked.

Once the fight starts, it doesn’t matter whether Lu Yang agrees or not!

~~~

“Junior Sister Tao, it has been a year since we last met. I wonder how much your cultivation has progressed. It can’t have stagnated, right?” Lan Ting flicked her fingers, launching countless air vortices. Despite appearing weak, they could actually severely injure an ordinary Intermediate Nascent Soul cultivator.

Tao Yaoye spun her umbrella and pivoted on her toes, deflecting the cyclone attacks from all directions. Her movements were graceful, as if she was dancing.

“Junior Sister Lan, you’ve overly concerned yourself. Cultivation emphasizes perseverance; consistent effort will eventually pay off. Countless people in this world yearn for the chance to cultivate but never obtain it. Compared to them, I am very fortunate.”

Lan Ting chuckled and took a gentle step. Faint glows lit up across the arena stage, setting up several interlocking great arrays.

“Junior Sister Tao, you do know how to be content. Speaking of which, you actually invented that marvel, the Dreamlike Bubble Mirage, which is very popular among mortals. I see it’s developing rapidly; you must have invested considerable effort, right? If you had focused that attention on cultivation instead, you might have achieved even greater results.”

Tao Yaoye smiled sweetly, her hands not slowing as she closed the red paper umbrella and transformed it into a spear that struck the great array’s focal point.

“The Dreamlike Bubble Mirage is the fruit of Senior Brother Lu Yang’s and my wisdom; he even gave its name. If I didn’t pour some effort into it, wouldn’t that have let our hard work down?”

Lan Ting used her waistband to prepare for battle, blending reality and illusion and using softness to overcome hardness.

“I’ve also watched the Dreamlike Bubble Mirage a few times, especially the Longevity Affinity, which depicted fellow disciples marrying and accompanying each other for eternity. It must have made many others envious.

“Illusions are like dreams. Junior Sister Tao, for you to have conceived such a heartfelt illusion, one can’t help but wonder how many times you’ve experienced it in your dreams. I heard those who master illusions often struggle to distinguish them from reality. I hope you don’t follow in their footsteps and become trapped in illusions.”

Tao Yaoye smiled sweetly again. “Thank you for your concern, Junior Sister Lan. However, you’ve had few interactions with Senior Brother Lu Yang. I’m afraid you don’t know that he’s the most adept at seeing through illusions. With him around, there’s no risk of me being trapped in illusions.

“Even if I were truly trapped, Senior Brother Lu Yang would come to rescue me.”

Lan Ting activated her nascent soul to deploy the Two Genesis Qi as weapons in an attempt to snatch Tao Yaoye’s red paper umbrella. “Senior Brother Lu Yang has the interests of the world at heart. If you were in trouble, he would naturally help. But the world has countless people in distress. I’m afraid he might not be able to spare you the attention then. It’s best that you learn to save yourself.”

Tao Yaoye moved lithely as she twisted her wrist to evade the Two Genesis Qi attack and enveloped Lan Ting in an illusion.

“My senior brother and I will roam the world with our swords, punishing evil and rescuing those in distress together. If I were to encounter trouble then, he would naturally help me. Junior Sister Lan, since you’re an outsider, you probably won’t experience such scenarios.”

~~~

As someone with a Five-Elements Immortal Physique, Bai Ming had formed a unique Five-Elements nascent soul, which displayed five colors.

The five-colored nascent soul clenched its tiny hand, summoning metal, wood, water, fire, and earth elemental attacks.

“Go!” The five elemental spells bombarded Li Haoran simultaneously.

The Jinwu Crow True Flame cawed, the heat blurring one’s vision. Shrouded within the true flame were several flying daggers. Weak Water supported the Jinwu Crow True Flame. Earthen walls from the ground on four sides, trapping Li Haoran. Following this, countless trees sprouted from beneath the ground, laced with poison and covered in thorns.

“The Five-Elements Immortal Physique truly lives up to its name.” Despite facing the five different elemental attacks, Li Haoran remained composed. A flame appeared in his palm, which he slapped toward the Jinwu Crow True Flame.

He used an imitation Jade Cleansing Bottle to collect the Weak Water, smashed the earthen walls with a heavy hammer, refined the incoming flying daggers for his own use with artifact refinement techniques, and severed the endlessly sprouting trees with his Bodhi Arm.

His actions left the disciples below the stage amazed.

Dealing with the five attacks separately without a hint of panic showed off Li Haoran’s incredible composure in battle.

“Simultaneously unleashing five attacks is nothing. I can unleash six!” Li Haoran chuckled and activated his nascent soul.

With a thunderous explosion, Li Haoran was blown to pieces. It startled Bai Ming, who thought Li Haoran’s cultivation had gone awry.

“Look, Senior Brother Li can still move!” someone below shouted excitedly.

Within the smoke and dust, six entities were moving rapidly—Li Haoran’s head, torso, and four limbs.

Bai Ming’s eye twitched. Even when he fought with diabolic creed members, he had never encountered such a bizarre combat style.

Li Haoran’s head spat out the Six Ding Divine Fire, while his torso rammed straight into Bai Ming. His hands held refined gourds that inhaled and exhaled yin and yang qi, capable of attracting souls. The boots on his feet were covered in iron nails laced with poison that would shoot out instantly if blocked, catching the opponent off guard.

Six attacks launched simultaneously!

Bai Ming and his nascent soul dealt with the attacks together. The barrage of various divine abilities and spells was overwhelming, and the hidden mechanisms in the sundry magical treasures often pushed him into intractable situations.

Suddenly, Li Haoran’s hair flew out. Each strand stiffened like steel needles, transforming into a high-speed rotating flying wheel that lunged at Bai Ming!

“You’ve been wearing a damned wig all this time?!”

Bai Ming looked at the adjacent arena stage with envy. Why are Tao Yaoye and Lan Ting fighting pretty harmoniously, while my battle here is fraught with lethal danger everywhere?

Chapter 737: The Strongest Single!

Yan Tianzhi and Man Gu were evenly matched in their duel.

Yan Tian didn’t hold back, immediately unleashing his three great battle tattoos—the Shield Ghost, the Taotie, and the Zhuyan. He had inscribed the Zhuyan mark upon reaching the Nascent Soul Stage.

The two demons and one ghost roared behind Yan Tianzhi, creating faint ripples in the space around them, a sight that awed those who witnessed it.

Man Gu summoned his Ancestor Assembly Nascent Soul. Whichever ancestor’s appearance the nascent soul took on, Man Gu would possess that ancestor’s abilities. Thus, his combat power at the Nascent Soul Stage fluctuated the most.

Fortunately, the ancestor that manifested this time was a legendary figure. He had once followed the Everlasting Immortal Fairy and gained some fame in ancient times.

Man Gu merged with his nascent soul. Instantly, his entire aura transformed, becoming ancient, mysterious, and powerful.

“Roar—” Carrying a massive octagonal purple-gold hammer, Man Gu looked fearsome and menacing. His roar alone matched the imposing presence of Yan Tianzhi’s three great battle tattoos.

This was the most common combat method of the Ancient Barbarian Tribe—yelling a couple of times to intimidate the opponent before fighting.

At the same time, long recitations of Words of Sages were played, completely out of place with the current atmosphere.

“Is it not a joy to have friends coming from afar...

“In a company of three, one must be my teacher...”

The talismans pasted on the hammer’s handle could play Words of Sages—the sole evidence that proved Man Gu was a Confucian cultivator.

Yan Tianzhi fused with the Shield Ghost. A shield as tall as a person appeared before his arms, swirling with a dark aura. Shield in hand, he charged, the Taotie and the Zhuyan flanking him as they rushed toward Man Gu.

The octagonal purple-gold hammer swept through the arena. This was the Nine Heavens Surging Lightning Hammer Technique that Man Gu had learned. The hammer technique was as swift and fierce as lightning, capable of shaking the nine heavens and resonating through the universe.

Man Gu had slain a Divine Transfiguration great demon that infiltrated Mount Yan in Great Xia. That demon had been pulverized by this very hammer. An ordinary Nascent Soul cultivator wouldn’t dare face even a single blow from the hammer.

Empowered by the ancestor’s nascent soul, Man Gu’s Nine Heavens Surging Lightning Hammer Technique reached new heights. Although the ancient ancestor hadn’t learned this specific hammer technique, he had once followed the Everlasting Immortal Fairy and had an innate combat intuition. After he possessed Man Gu, the latter displayed improvement across the board, except in intelligence.

The Taotie opened its maw, devouring from all directions. The Zhuyan swept its staff across the arena. The massive hammer fell like surging lightning, sending out shockwaves with every strike.

Both combatants took to the sky simultaneously, entangled in a battle mid-air.

The heavy hammer was swung like the wind in Man Gu’s hands, a testament to the strength bestowed by his Ancient Barbarian bloodline.

Boom!

The hammer hit the shield. Yan Tianzhi felt as if endless ocean waves were crashing against him, the unceasing force affecting his organs and meridians.

“Exhilarating!” Yan Tianzhi laughed heartily. I haven’t experienced such a satisfying and intense fight in a long time!

~~~

Under the effect of the Lu-Style Arhat Fist, Meng Jingzhou had become bald, truly living up to his title as the Imperial City’s Buddha Scion.

“Sword Control Art!” Surrounded by sharp sword qi, Lu Yang raised two fingers. The Sword-Cleansing Pond shot forth like a dragon emerging from an abyss, charging toward Meng Jingzhou like a freight truck.

“Heaven-Shaking Six Forms!” Meng Jingzhou had become proficient in this move. His seemingly plain punch contained power capable of splitting mountains. It resonated with heaven and earth, drawing in the surrounding spirit energy. The sound of his punch alone constituted a sonic attack.

The fist and the pond clashed.

Meng Jingzhou was forced half a step back. The Sword-Cleansing Pond still edged out slightly in terms of raw strength.

Lu Yang tried to have his Unbeatable Nascent Soul fly into Meng Jingzhou’s body and kindly help the latter rise to become a Three Infants mighty expert.

However, Meng Jingzhou failed to recognize this act of kindness and fled swiftly, adamantly refusing to let the Unbeatable Nascent Soul touch him.

“Golden Bird True Flame! Three Flavor True Fire!”

“Nirvana True Fire!”

The three great true fires collided. Two bird cries resounded simultaneously, and a huge explosion ensued. Flames shot skyward, turning the arena into a furnace where two agile figures battled within the inferno.

Amidst the flames, the Pure Yang Taiji Diagram reappeared. The six-armed adept’s fist technique thundered, forcefully shaking the Sword-Cleansing Pond.

Lu Yang used the Tree-Planting Mantra to create a clone and have each of them wield the Qingfeng Sword and the Mingyue Sword, but they were at a disadvantage.

“Look! It’s Three Heads Six Arms!” a Prison Suppression Sect disciple exclaimed, unable to believe his eyes.

“How is this possible?!” This was a mighty divine ability most revered by physique cultivators. He hadn’t heard of anyone executing it at the Nascent Soul Stage.

“Bald head, Three Heads Six Arms—this is the Angry-Faced Vajra from our Buddhist guardians!” A Hanging Monastery senior male disciple’s eyes lit up upon seeing Meng Jingzhou.

Within the flames, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou conversed while fighting.

“Don’t forget you still owe me a chance to show off,” Meng Jingzhou reminded Lu Yang.

He was referring to the finals in the Intermediate Golden Core category. Lu Yang had asked me to concede and let him show off first, promising me a turn in the future.

But we’re already at the Intermediate Nascent Soul Stage, and that grandson Lu Yang still hasn’t fulfilled his promise.

Lu Yang fell silent for a moment. If Meng Jingzhou hadn’t reminded him, he would have forgotten about this matter.

Lu Yang remained composed, consciously slowing his sword techniques. “Of course, I remember. I just haven’t found the right opportunity until now.”

Meng Jingzhou’s six eyes looked askance at Lu Yang. You little brat, it’s more like you forgot your promise, right?

Sword light and fist shadows intertwined. The ethereal and nimble sword qi sought gaps in Meng Jingzhou’s defense. Transformed into the Angry-Faced Vajra, Meng Jingzhou used his fists to control qi, neutralizing the barrage of rapid sword attacks.

“Heaven-Shaking Six Forms!”

Performing Heaven-Shaking Six Forms with six arms increased the technique’s power severalfold. With the Qingfeng Sword held crosswise before his chest, Lu Yang was sent flying backward, tumbling twice before falling off the arena stage.

“What?! It’s actually Senior Brother Meng who won!”

“During the Intermediate Golden Core finals, Senior Brother Meng lost to Young Creed Leader Lu, who fought to a draw with Senior Brother Lu. How could Senior Brother Lu lose to Senior Brother Meng?!”

“This shows that the three are similar in power. Any slight difference can affect the final outcome!”

“What a terrifying Single’s Spirit Root. The predecessors probably don’t compare to Junior Brother Meng.”

“Truly the strongest single.”

“If Junior Brother Meng remains single, his future will be boundless.”

Hearing the discussions below, Meng Jingzhou’s face darkened. You might as well not have praised me.

Lu Yang was caught by the Sword-Cleansing Pond when he fell. Climbing out, he pointed toward a nearby mountain summit with slight puzzlement.

“Why is everyone flying out? Did something major happen?”

The representatives from the various major sects seemed to share one mind, simultaneously flying out of the reception hall and swarming toward the Dao-Seeking Sect’s mountain gate like bees.

Soon, a curious senior male disciple investigated the situation.

“The sect leader has returned. The elders and sect leaders from the various major sects have gone to receive him.”

Meng Jingzhou gazed into the distance, noticing the representatives from the other sects holding gleaming weapons. No matter how he looked at it, it didn’t seem like a welcoming party for the Taciturn Daoist Priest.

Lu Yang fell silent. Shifu must have heard that the Vast Sea Daoist Lord is still alive and rushed back specifically to pay respects to the Founding Ancestor.

It’s just that he forgot he isn’t the only one who wants to see the Vast Sea Daoist Lord.

Chapter 738: The Taciturn Daoist Priest Returns to the Sect

Not far from the Dao-Seeking Sect, two furtive figures drew near.

“Big Brother, can I enter the Dao-Seeking Sect as a demon?” Chieftain Jin’s brows were tightly scrunched up in worry.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest stroked his beard and pondered for a moment. “Our sect always treats everyone equally, not discriminating between demons and humans. But I’m not sure about Founding Ancestor Vast Sea. Perhaps he might not look favorably upon demons.

“How about this? You hide here, while I’ll go ahead and scout the path.”

“Be careful, Big Brother.”

“Don’t worry. I’ve roamed the jianghu for so many years. When have I ever run into an accident?”

The Taciturn Daoist Priest’s appearance was a far cry from his usual slovenly image. He now wore a clean and elegant Daoist robe and had his hair tied in a neat bun, with a few strands of beard swaying gently in the wind.

With steady and measured steps, he walked toward the mountain gate.

Soon, Chieftain Jin watched as the visiting major sects detected the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s presence. Cultivators swarmed out from the Dao-Seeking Sect, shouting and pursuing the Taciturn Daoist Priest.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest fled in disarray, nearly being caught several times.

Witnessing this scene, Chieftain Jin trembled like a leaf, thinking that human cultivators were even more ferocious than demons. Despite his fear, a trace of gratitude welled up in his heart. He used himself as bait to lure out the danger and ensure my safety—I really didn’t misplace my loyalty and trust in calling him Big Brother.

“Big Brother truly values brotherhood. I’ll speak with the Little Ancestor next time to see if our families can form an alliance. With the Vast Sea Daoist Lord and the Little Ancestor, we have two half-immortals overseeing things. It shouldn’t be difficult to secure a spot in the top ten during the Battle of the Great Era.”

~~~

“Old Taciturn Scoundrel, I dare you not to run!” Every Fusion cultivator visiting the Dao-Seeking Sect had some sort of grudge with the Taciturn Daoist Priest.

Although they didn’t manage to pay respects to the legendary Vast Sea Daoist Lord on this trip, being able to see the Taciturn Daoist Priest in person made the journey worthwhile.

“You still dare to chase me? Be careful of Founding Ancestor Vast Sea settling accounts with you all later!” Even while the Taciturn Daoist Priest was fleeing in panic, he didn’t forget to threaten the crowd.

He felt that his luck had been consistently poor for most of this year. My misfortune has been endless. I’ve been found and pursued time and time again. Now, I can even bump into so many familiar faces at the sect entrance.

“Maybe I should go pay respects at the Buddhist sects?”

The Taciturn Daoist Priest hesitated. Recalling his second disciple’s reputation in the Buddhist Kingdom—“as if the Buddha had passed away”—he figured the Buddhist sects wouldn’t grant blessings upon Ye Zijin’s shifu.

A saber ray grazed him, jerking the Taciturn Daoist Priest out of his thoughts. “Fleeing for my life is the priority. I’ll ruminate over my luck another time.

“Human and Sword as One!” With a soft cry, the Taciturn Daoist Priest fused with his long sword. The sword morphed into a streak of escaping light, moving at extreme speeds.

“One Sword Into Ten Thousand Swords!” The sword shimmered and multiplied into tens of thousands of copies.

Each replica was identical to the original in length, style, pattern, and even the sword tassel. Even if one probed with their spiritual consciousness, they wouldn’t be able to distinguish which was the original sword.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest was hidden right within one of these swords.

“Dharma Eye, open!”

“Heavenly Eye, reveal!”

“All karma is in the tray!”

“Demon-Revealing Mirror!”

“Fire-Perceiving Clarity!”

People from all backgrounds displayed their mighty abilities, determined to capture the Taciturn Daoist Priest.

Unfortunately, the Taciturn Daoist Priest was not so easily caught. This escape method of his was rooted in Sword Dao and subsequently enhanced with guidance from the “Thief Ancestor” and his own comprehension, culminating in his current success. If one wasn’t at the Transcendent Tribulation Stage, they could forget about capturing him.

~~~

“Shifu sure is popular.” Lu Yang sighed at the mountain gate, with Gan Tian standing beside him.

The sky was a dazzling blur of flying swords, and even the Everlasting Immortal Fairy complimented the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s talent.

Disciples from the Dao-Seeking Sect and other major sects had gathered here, their heads swiveling up, down, left, and right as they followed the group of flying swords.

With their elders chasing the Taciturn Daoist Priest, regardless of whether they could catch up to him, they couldn’t possibly return to the Dao-Seeking Sect. Lan Ting and the others couldn’t continue sparring either; if they kept fighting, they might lose sight of their masters.

Of the four battle groups, only Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou’s pair managed to decide a winner, and it was an internal strife at that.

While watching the battle, Meng Jingzhou seized the chance to point at his shiny, bald head. “Old Lu, use your Longevity Art.”

Lu Yang activated the Longevity Art, placing his hand firmly on Meng Jingzhou’s head, where hair miraculously grew. It was truly a case of “an immortal caresses my head, binding my hair and granting me longevity.”[1]

The flying swords traveled farther and farther away. Qiu Jin’an and the others followed, eventually becoming mere specks in the distance.

“Then we shall take our leave here.” Bai Ming and the others hastily bid farewell before chasing after their masters.

The Dao-Seeking Sect disciples waited at the entrance for roughly a quarter of an hour before the disheveled and grimy Taciturn Daoist Priest returned to the sect on his flying sword.

It was unclear whether the dirt covering him was from being pinned to the ground and getting beaten up or from his narrow escapes through the hail of attacks.

In any case, he had finally returned, albeit barely safe and sound.

“Hahaha, no need for such a welcome, everyone. You may disperse.” The Taciturn Daoist Priest waved his hand, acting as if he wasn’t the one in dire straits.

Nevertheless, the Taciturn Daoist Priest was the sect leader and still held authority. When he told the crowd to disperse, they followed suit and didn’t welcome him at all.

“Gan Tian has become a Fusion true lord now. Not bad, not bad. It seems your trip to the Demon Region was quite fruitful.” The Taciturn Daoist Priest was slightly surprised by Gan Tian’s cultivation speed. According to his estimates, she should have taken another two or three years to advance to the Fusion Stage.

This suggests that she had gained some unexpected harvests from her trip to the Demon Region.

“Little Lu is already at the Intermediate Nascent Soul Stage, and Little Meng too.” The Taciturn Daoist Priest clicked his tongue in amazement. As expected of promising great seeds for the Great Era. My own cultivation was fast enough back in the day, but I never thought the youngsters nowadays would surpass even me.

“By the way, did the Phoenix Ancient Ancestor visit our sect?” The Taciturn Daoist Priest’s question caused Lu Yang’s body to stiffen.

“Shifu, why do you ask?”

“A while back, the Phoenix Ancient Ancestor came looking for me with the book Dragon Phoenix Transformation and gave me a thrashing. I pondered but didn’t remember leaving my name on it. I figured someone must have informed the Phoenix Ancient Ancestor.”

Lu Yang laughed awkwardly. “The Phoenix Ancient Ancestor has extensive powers, with eyes and hands that reach the heavens. Perhaps she knows karmic methods and calculated it herself.”

“Is that so? I also heard the Phoenix Ancient Ancestor claims to be a member of our Heavenly Court Creed. What’s that all about?”

Just as Lu Yang was struggling with how to explain this to his shifu, Meng Jingzhou volunteered valiantly. “Put simply, Old Lu awakened the slumbering Phoenix Ancient Ancestor, and she recognized Lu Yang as her senior brother.”

A question mark popped out.

Clearly, the overly simplistic explanation had exceeded the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s realm of understanding.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest temporarily skipped over the matters he couldn’t understand and asked eagerly, “What about Founding Ancestor Vast Sea? Is he really alive?”

“Not only is Founding Ancestor alive, but another founding ancestor is also alive.”

“Who?” The Taciturn Daoist Priest mentally ran through the list of founding ancestors but couldn’t think of who else should still be alive.

“The Innate Daoist Priest. Old Meng and I happened to be out on a mission when we encountered the Innate Daoist Priest, who had dispersed his cultivation to cultivate anew, so we brought him back.”

The Taciturn Daoist Priest fell silent for a moment. “Are there other matters I am unaware of?”

Lu Yang counted on his fingers as he mused. “Nothing much else. It’s just that when Old Meng and I were out, we ran into the Void Emptiness Supreme Lord and the Nightmare Supreme Lord. Seeing that we were no match, we asked Big Senior Sister for help.

“Then there was the Great Yu Alliance, led by the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord. They had their sights set on the immortal sword in my possession and wanted to sneak into the sect for a robbery, but were rounded up in one fell swoop.

“I reckon most of the Great Yu cultivators are in our Incarceration Peak now. There are probably hardly any left outside.”
