The Taciturn Daoist Priest’s silence stretched even longer. He knew about the matters regarding the Void Emptiness Supreme Lord and the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord, but he hadn’t known that all these incidents were connected to Lu Yang.

I’ve lived for two thousand years, yet the stir I’ve caused can’t compare to the harvests my youngest disciple reaps in a single year.

“Little Lu, have you considered taking over the role of sect leader now?”

1. This came from one of Li Bai’s poems. ☜

Chapter 739: Spring and Autumn Writing Style

Lu Yang shook his head like a rattle-drum[1], firmly refusing his shifu’s proposal.

Judging by the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s tenures as acting sect leader for three days and three months, he figured it wasn’t a leisurely position. It’s more appropriate for an esteemed, virtuous, and scholarly cultivator like Big Senior Sister to assume such a role.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest was gratified. I didn’t expect my youngest disciple’s Dao heart to be so steadfast, remaining unmoved even when faced with the monumental fortuitous opportunity to take over the position of sect leader.

“Is Little Zhi around?”

“Big Senior Sister is at Incarceration Peak, interrogating the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord and a few Transcendent Tribulation cultivators whose names we don’t even know. Should I call her out?”

The Taciturn Daoist Priest breathed a sigh of relief. As long as she’s not here. “No need, no need. I was just asking casually.” Although he had been quite well-behaved recently, he felt an inexplicable sense of guilt whenever he saw his eldest disciple.

Nevertheless, the Taciturn Daoist Priest was happy to see that both his third and fourth disciples had achieved success in their cultivation upon his return to the sect. “I wonder when the five of us, shifu and disciples, will be reunited. Your Second Senior Brother hasn’t returned for a hundred years. He caused too much of a stir in the Buddhist Kingdom to the point that even I was implicated. Those from the Buddhist sects find me an eyesore now.”

The Taciturn Daoist Priest shook his head. What a rebellious disciple, stirring up trouble and implicating his shifu. How many times have I taught him? When causing trouble outside, remember to conceal your identity. I’ve emphasized this repeatedly, yet he just can’t remember.

On the flip side, since Ye Zijin didn’t return to the Dao-Seeking Sect after stirring up trouble, in a way, he prevented drawing calamity to the sect. To this day, the Buddhist Kingdom still frequently sent missives to the Dao-Seeking Sect, hoping the sect would promptly take Ye Zijin back.

Every time, the Taciturn Daoist Priest would fob them off with excuses like “a general outside cannot always obey the sovereign’s orders.”

Lu Yang thought to himself, Shifu, the Buddhist sects’ dislike for you probably has little to do with Second Senior Brother.

Despite having never met this Second Senior Brother and only seen his portrait, Lu Yang had heard many legends about him.

Minor incidents—such as Ye Zijin’s daily sarcastic remarks that caused senior Buddhist monks to break their precepts, his vigorous promotion of the Blissful Chan cultivation method, and his impersonation of the Buddha statue to enjoy offerings—should be put aside for now.

Apart from that, Ye Zijin had suggested to many senior monks that they learn the Phoenix Tribe’s Nirvana method. This way, when the monks passed away in a seated posture and self-immolated, they could not only produce many śarīra relics,[2] but also live another life. The Buddhist Kingdom would then have a continuous supply of śarīra relics, enjoying immense benefits.

Based on the Buddhist Kingdom’s advocated theory of accumulating merit through releasing lives,[3] Ye Zijin proposed an even more advanced theory. Since “giving birth is also a form of releasing lives,” he encouraged the monks to give birth to more children to accumulate merit.

However, the Buddhist Kingdom’s senior monks were too rigid in their old-fashioned ways and couldn’t accept Ye Zijin’s overly advanced thinking. Not only did they reject his proposals, but they also repeatedly sent pursuers to capture him.

Fortunately, Ye Zijin had learned a slew of escape skills from the Taciturn Daoist Priest, which allowed him to navigate the Buddhist Kingdom safely.

Lu Yang had also heard that some pessimistic monks believed that Ye Zijin’s birth heralded the arrival of the vipralopa era, when dharma was coming to an end. Ye Zijin had even obtained the evaluation of “as if the Buddha had passed away” because of this.

According to the founder of Buddhism, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, the vipralopa era was a term she had made up because she thought it sounded cool.

“Your Second Senior Brother is also a cultivation genius. If not for Little Zhi, he would be the one with the highest cultivation talent of his generation. It’s a pity he was born at the wrong time.

“By the way, where is our founding ancestor, the Innate Daoist Priest?” As the sect leader, the Taciturn Daoist Priest felt it was necessary to pay respects to the founder of the Dao-Seeking Sect.

“I’ll go look for him.” Lu Yang also had no idea where the Innate Daoist Priest had gone off to.

~~~

After searching around, Lu Yang found the Innate Daoist Priest eating skewers in the barbeque shop.

Upon seeing Lu Yang, the people in the barbeque shop thought he was here for inspection.

Lu Yang quickly urged Chef Gao and the others to stand down. “It’s fine, it’s fine. Everyone, go about your business. I’m here for him.

“Founding Ancestor, my shifu said he would like to meet you.”

“Your shifu? The current sect leader of the Dao-Seeking Sect?”

“Yes.”

The Innate Daoist Priest quickly slurped the remaining bits off his two skewers. “Let’s go then.”

~~~

Lu Yang escorted the Innate Daoist Priest to the summit of Heaven’s Gate Peak, where the Taciturn Daoist Priest had been waiting for some time. The latter immediately knelt and kowtowed. “Ye Wanli, the current Dao-Seeking Sect Leader, pays his respects to the Founding Ancestor.”

“I can’t accept such a grand bow. Please rise quickly. Moreover, I am now just an ordinary disciple of the Dao-Seeking Sect. There is no need to treat me this way.”

The Taciturn Daoist Priest’s eyes lit up. “In that case, Founding Ancestor, are you in need of a shifu? What do you think of me?”

Lu Yang thought, No wonder Shifu and Eighth Elder are close brothers who shared open-crotch pants as kids. Their train of thought is exactly the same.

He kindly reminded him, “Founding Ancestor Vast Sea has already taken him as a disciple.”

The Taciturn Daoist Priest, “...”

“By the way, Founding Ancestor, could you tell me about the early days of the Dao-Seeking Sect’s founding? To be frank, I am actually a writer, and I always strive to promote the Dao-Seeking Sect. You hold the firsthand historical accounts of the sect. You can speak, and I’ll record. By joining our strengths, we are bound to enhance the reputation of our Dao-Seeking Sect further.”

“That’s a good thing,” the Innate Daoist Priest said cheerfully. He held quite a favorable impression of the Taciturn Daoist Priest. This sect leader must have contributed significantly for the Dao-Seeking Sect to achieve its current success.

“Speaking of how the Dao-Seeking Sect was founded, we have to start from 120,000 years ago. According to the customs of that time, Void Refinement cultivators would either join a sect or establish one themselves to have a stable and safe place to cultivate. I chose the latter.

“The Heaven Strategy Sect’s divination was the most accurate. I only spent one hundred thousand spirit stones to have them calculate a place with good feng shui for me. The people from the Heaven Strategy Sect told me that these one hundred thousand spirit stones weren’t for them but an offering to Heaven—it was a token of sincerity. After they informed me of the auspicious site’s location, they also cautioned me to arrive at the designated time, otherwise it would affect my fortune.

“Unfortunately, it was dark at the time, and my cultivation level was fluctuating, making even flying difficult. On top of that, I had a tendency of getting lost. If that had gone on, I definitely wouldn’t have reached the auspicious site on time. Thus, I asked an old farmer working in the fields for directions.

“The old farmer pointed me in a direction, and I finally arrived at the auspicious site at the break of dawn.

“After the sect was successfully established, since my reputation and the terms I offered were pretty good, many Void Refinement fellow Daoists were willing to join my sect, and many promising seedlings also enrolled as disciples. That was when the Dao-Seeking Sect began to take shape.”

The Taciturn Daoist Priest nodded along and murmured affirmations while lowering his head to write down the points.

During the late Great Yu era, the world was dark, and people’s hearts were filled with anxiety. For stability and safety, the Innate Daoist Priest decided to establish a sect.

The Innate Daoist Priest consulted Heaven with sincerity. In turn, Heaven pointed out a clear path for him and stated that time was tight, urging him to act swiftly.

The period before dawn was the darkest. Acting according to Heaven’s will, the Innate Daoist Priest faced numerous difficulties. Not only was his cultivation affected, but he also lost his way. Fortunately, with the help of the common folk, he overcame these hardships and finally arrived at the location indicated by Heaven.

The Innate Daoist Priest established the Dao-Seeking Sect, and the dark world welcomed the light of dawn. At that time, many like-minded individuals believed the world was turbulent and unsafe. Influenced by the Innate Daoist Priest’s charisma, they voluntarily joined the Dao-Seeking Sect. With that, the Dao-Seeking Sect grew increasingly powerful...

After the Taciturn Daoist Priest finished recording, he looked up at the Innate Daoist Priest. “Founding Ancestor, please continue?”

1. The bolanggu, also known as a pellet drum or rattle drum, is a traditional Chinese toy that is said to have been created about 3500 years ago in the Shang Dynasty. You probably have seen it in Chinese period dramas as one of the most popular children’s toys. ☜

2. These are relics found in the cremated ashes of Buddhists. They can also refer to crystal-like or pearl-shaped objects. The crystalline structures are said to be formed due to the high temperatures from cremation. ☜

3. The original idea is to show mercy by sparing lives, such as letting captive animals live. ☜

Chapter 740: One Sword Into Ten Thousand Swords

The Innate Daoist Priest was immersed in his memories from 120,000 years ago, while the Taciturn Daoist Priest held a brush, recording the Innate Daoist Priest’s memoirs. If one ignored the contents of the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s notes, this would be a harmonious scene between the young and the old.

The Innate Daoist Priest spoke from dawn until dusk, only stopping when the barbeque skewers he had eaten at noon were completely digested.

Lu Yang and Gan Tian swept their spiritual consciousness over what their shifu had written down. Worried that the Innate Daoist Priest couldn’t accept the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s overly advanced publicity concepts and might do something extreme, like an ancestor beating up an unworthy descendant, they tacitly agreed not to mention the matter.

Moreover, they couldn’t exactly say that what their master recorded was wrong. At the very least, every sentence originated from the Innate Daoist Priest’s words. They could at most call it slightly embellished.

“So Second Senior Brother learned his skill of inverting black and white from Shifu,” Gan Tian remarked through an auditory message.

All the dregs of the Taciturn Daoist Priest had been absorbed by Ye Zijin. No wonder he has such a terrible reputation in the western Buddhist Kingdom.

“If Second Senior Brother learned it from Shifu, then where did Shifu learn these skills?”

“From Eighth Elder. Wasn’t it said that Shifu was raised by Eighth Elder through all the shitty hardships of child rearing?”

“Then what about Eighth Elder? Our Grand-Shifu doesn’t seem to be that kind of character, does he?”

“He’s a self-taught talent.”

“Exceptionally gifted, indeed.”

As the Innate Daoist Priest had yet to begin cultivating, he lacked spiritual consciousness. Seeing the Taciturn Daoist Priest rapidly taking notes and filling several pages densely, he knew this reigning sect leader had recorded everything he said and nodded in satisfaction.

“Work hard. I have high hopes for you.”

The Innate Daoist Priest was in high spirits. It’s rare to find someone who doesn’t mind my long-windedness and is willing to listen to me talk about history.

The more he looked at the Taciturn Daoist Priest, the more he found him pleasing to the eye. Of course, it might also have been because both of them were prone to getting lost.

Receiving the Innate Daoist Priest’s approval, the Taciturn Daoist Priest immediately declared, “Rest assured, Founding Ancestor, I will definitely promote your glorious deeds of establishing the Dao-Seeking Sect!”

“Good, good, good! With people like you in the sect, how could the sect not prosper?!”

“By the way, Founding Ancestor, do you know where Founding Ancestor Vast Sea is?” The Taciturn Daoist Priest hadn’t finished paying respects to all the prominent figures.

The Innate Daoist Priest shook his head. “I don’t know.”

The Dao-Seeking Sect was vast, and without a way to contact the Vast Sea Daoist Lord, no one could find him.

“Oh, your eldest disciple and the previous sect leader might be able to find Vast Sea.”

The Taciturn Daoist Priest grimaced and didn’t continue that line of conversation. Everyone knows that Little Zhi and Shifu are definitely aware of where the Vast Sea Daoist Lord is.

“It’s getting late. I should head back first.” The Innate Daoist Priest yawned. After jabbering on for most of the day, he was exhausted.

“Let me see you off,” the Taciturn Daoist Priest offered enthusiastically. He wasn’t afraid of revealing the Innate Daoist Priest’s identity by escorting him. After all, the Innate Daoist Priest’s public identity was the Vast Sea Daoist Lord’s disciple, making his seniority second in the Dao-Seeking Sect.

After seeing off the Innate Daoist Priest, the Taciturn Daoist Priest returned to Heaven’s Gate Peak. “Come come, both of you, tell me everything that’s happened since I left last time.”

The Taciturn Daoist Priest had heard about the major events regarding the Demon Region, half-immortals, and the like on his journey, and they were all connected to Lu Yang. Now that he had the chance to question the person involved, he wasn’t going to waste it.

The last time the Taciturn Daoist Priest returned was just after the sect celebration ended, when Lu Yang was only at the Golden Core Stage. Now, Lu Yang was already at the Intermediate Nascent Soul Stage. A lot must have happened in that time.

Since it was his personal experience, Lu Yang recounted it eloquently.

As he spoke, Lu Yang realized something was amiss. “Wait, hasn’t it only been slightly over a year since I advanced from the Intermediate Golden Core Stage to the Intermediate Golden Core Stage? How did so many things happen?”

The Taciturn Daoist Priest listened happily. These are all source materials for storytelling! They’re far more eventful than the Founding Ancestor’s experiences.

The Founding Ancestor just had difficulties establishing the sect and contended with cultivators of the same realm.

But look at Lu Yang here. Although he’s only at the Nascent Soul Stage, the enemies he provokes are minimally at the Transcendent Tribulation Stage. On a good day, he can even attract a couple of half-immortals.

If Lu Yang’s troublemaking ability had been around in the Founding Ancestor’s era, the Great Yu Dynasty would have perished twenty thousand years earlier. The Great Yu Imperial Preceptor then was only at the Transcendent Tribulation Stage.

“...The Myriad Spells Daoist Lord suddenly kowtowed just like that. I was quite surprised too.” Lu Yang naturally couldn’t reveal anything about the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, so he insisted it was a coincidence.

However, in the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s eyes, it didn’t matter whether it was a coincidence. “Alright, rest for a day. I’ll impart to you the sword technique One Sword Into Ten Thousand Swords tomorrow.”

The last time the Taciturn Daoist Priest returned to the sect, he had wanted to teach this move, but Lu Yang’s cultivation level was insufficient. This technique required the Divine Transfiguration Stage, and Lu Yang had just qualified for it.

~~~

At dawn, Lu Yang was dressed in his training attire and held his Qingfeng Sword, brimming with energy.

“Originally, I wanted to teach you both ‘Human and Sword as One’ and ‘One Sword Into Ten Thousand Swords,’ but since you were unwilling to learn ‘Human and Sword as One,’ let’s leave it at that.

“You have already achieved the prerequisite conditions: sword follows the heart, a clear mental state, qi and sword merged, and movement and stillness as one.”

Usually, only a Sword Dao genius at the Divine Transfiguration could reach these four states. But as someone with a Sword Spirit Root, Lu Yang had already attained these realms while comprehending the Sword Dao.

“Keep the inner mind clear, discard distracting thoughts, and focus on the Sword Dao. Drive the sword qi to leave the body and take form. Merge your spiritual consciousness with the sword qi to achieve autonomous differentiation of sword qi. With a single thought, transform it into tens of thousands of sword qi.

“Just like this.”

The Taciturn Daoist Priest extended his index finger, and a strand of sword qi leaped forth. As he gently swayed his finger, the afterimages left by the sword qi in the air transformed into numerous additional strands of sword qi.

Lu Yang marveled at the sight, never expecting sword qi could be used in such a way.

“Sit cross-legged, calm the heart, relax, and be natural. Your hands must be clenched tightly, and your eyes must look straight. Qi circulates through the loops, cycling without cease...” The Taciturn Daoist Priest taught the heart mantra of the sword technique.

Lu Yang’s talent in Sword Dao was not at all inferior to his talent in spells. A little guidance was enough for him to understand.

Shing! Accompanied by thousands of strands of sword qi, the Qingfeng Sword left its scabbard, its cry resembling a dragon’s roar.

“Go!” Lu Yang gave a soft cry. The Qingfeng Sword soared into the sky, followed by thousands of sword qi. It was akin to a massive army charging in the sky with the Qingfeng Sword as the general commanding the troops.

With a thought from Lu Yang, the thousands of sword qi solidified, forming thousands of replicas of the Qingfeng Sword.

“Success!”

Lu Yang brought two fingers together and pressed downward. The thousands of Qingfeng Swords fell like rain, whistling through the air as they struck the ground. Turf was ripped up, trees toppled, and the earth was riddled with holes.

If a Basic Divine Transfiguration cultivator had been standing below, they would have been turned into a hedgehog.

Lu Yang was elated. In just half a day, he had mastered ‘One Sword Into Ten Thousand Swords,’ the technique that had stumped countless Sword Dao geniuses.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest was gratified and nodded. This youngest disciple learns sword techniques even faster than me back in the day.

Neither shifu nor disciple noticed the puppet secretly watching them from the shadows with an eerie gaze.

“Since it works with the Qingfeng Sword...” Lu Yang had a new idea. He put away the Qingfeng Sword and took out the Sword-Cleansing Pond.

“Qi circulates through the loops, cycling without cease... Go!”

The Sword-Cleansing Pond shot skyward and multiplied into thousands of copies in the air, forming an oppressive mass like storm clouds had gathered.

“Fall!”

The Sword-Cleansing Ponds plummeted like a meteor shower, carrying an unavoidable sword intent as they crashed into the ground. The firm earth was dented considerably, and even an Intermediate Divine Transfiguration cultivator would be crushed to death by this sword technique.

“As I thought, the Sword-Cleansing Pond is even more powerful!”

The Taciturn Daoist Priest looked at the Sword-Cleansing Pond in bewilderment.

“Why does this thing look so familiar?”

Chapter 741: Sect Civil War

“Isn’t this the Sword-Cleansing Pond I used frequently?” the Taciturn Daoist Priest wondered. No wonder it looks so familiar. I often used the Sword-Cleansing Pond to cleanse my violent energy in my youth.

This was a treasure passed down through generations of the Dao-Seeking Sect. Even the Grand-Shifu had frequently used the Sword-Cleansing Pond to cleanse his violent energy, lest he lose his temper and beat the Taciturn Daoist Priest to death.

From this perspective, the Sword-Cleansing Pond was the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s savior.

Noticing his shifu’s reaction, Lu Yang explained sheepishly, “Well, I heard about the legends of you and Grand-Shifu and wanted to emulate you both, so I was comprehending the Sword Dao by the Sword-Cleansing Pond. It was probably because I got too close that the Sword-Cleansing Pond latched onto me.”

As if confirming Lu Yang’s words, the Sword-Cleansing Pond circled him joyfully.

“You know what, the Sword-Cleansing Pond is indeed an extremely useful offensive magical treasure.”

The Sword-Cleansing Pond was much easier to use than the Qingfeng Sword. While the Qingfeng Sword was an immortal sword, Yun Zhi had placed layer upon layer of seals on it. For Lu Yang, it was just a sword commensurate with his cultivation level.

But the Sword-Cleansing Pond was different. Not only was its quality top-notch, but it also shared a tacit understanding with Lu Yang, allowing the latter to move it as effortlessly as his own arm.

With One Sword Into Ten Thousand Swords, it smashed the ground full of pits and craters, demonstrating immense power.

“If you put it that way, the Sword-Cleansing Pond is indeed pretty useful.” As a master in Sword Dao, the Taciturn Daoist Priest could also see the Sword-Cleansing Pond’s power.

Unfortunately, he and the Sword-Cleansing Pond were destined to meet but not fated to be together. The opportunity went to Lu Yang, and the Taciturn Daoist Priest could only silently offer his blessings.

“Come, sword techniques require repeated practice to master. Try it a few more times.”

Lu Yang nodded and obediently activated the Sword-Cleansing Pond. Once again, the sky was filled with numerous Sword-Cleansing Ponds, shrouding Heaven’s Gate Peak in darkness.

“One Sword Into Ten Thousand Swords, fall!”

Boom! Boom!

With his previous success, executing it this time went even more smoothly.

“Haha, Old Nine, I never expected you could also teach disciples.” First Elder’s hearty laughter came from the air.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest disliked this remark. “Shoo shoo, what do you mean by ‘I could also teach disciples?’ Look at Little Zhi, Little Jin, Little Tian, and Little Yang—which one of them wasn’t taught by me?”

First Elder scoffed. “That’s enough. You make it sound like Little Zhi’s high cultivation has anything to do with you.”

Whoosh, whoosh, whoosh. As if they had discussed this beforehand, one elder after another flew to Heaven’s Gate Peak; even Sixth Elder, who rarely showed herself, came over.

As soon as Sixth Elder arrived, everyone tacitly switched to communicating through their spiritual consciousness.

“It’s been a long time since we senior and junior brothers have gathered. Why don’t we take this chance to spar a bit?” First Elder proposed with a smile.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest’s face darkened. “Last time you said that, you all ganged up on me and beat me half to death, then even made me sect leader afterward.”

“Old Nine, that’s where you’re wrong. So many people covet the position of sect leader. The eight of us remembered our bond as fellow disciples, which was why we reluctantly gave it up and let you become sect leader. Yet you blame us for it now?”

The Taciturn Daoist Priest chuckled dryly. It’s not like this is my first day roaming the jianghu. How could I believe your nonsense?

“Don’t worry, we’ll have a fair exchange this time. Just like the old days, it’ll be a casual spar with no teams. Nine people, free for all.”

“That’s more like it.”

The eight elders and the Taciturn Daoist Priest exchanged smiles, as if recalling their youthful days under the tutelage of the Grand-Shifu.

“Let’s have a round.”

Nine renowned Fusion cultivators of the current era commenced battle atop Heaven’s Gate Peak. The Taciturn Daoist Priest’s Sword Dao, First Elder’s dreamscape spells, Grandpa Ba’s arrays, Third Elder’s physique cultivation, Fourth Elder’s Confucian cultivation, Fifth Elder’s artifact refinement techniques, Sixth Elder’s Immaculate Immortal Physique, Seventh Elder’s pill-concoction techniques, and Eighth Elder’s talismans—all were peerless with the highest attainments among those of the same realm.

Although the Taciturn Daoist Priest and First Elder were already at the Half-Step Transcendent Tribulation Stage, the battlefield was unpredictable. When the nine of them started fighting, it wasn’t a situation where higher cultivation guaranteed victory.

The elders rarely fought, so the Dao-Seeking Sect disciples quickly selected the closest vantage points to watch the battle. A battle between Fusion cultivators could shake heaven and earth; there was no need to observe from directly underneath like Lu Yang.

“Who do you think will win?”

“Sixth Elder’s Immaculate Immortal Physique is impervious to all spells. Within the domain of immortal physique, Sixth Elder is unbeatable!”

“The Immaculate Immortal Physique may be powerful, but it’s not yet unbeatable.”

“I think it’ll probably be First Elder. I heard he was a tough character in his youth. It’s only in his old age that he began cultivating his character, digging holes everywhere and building tombs illegally.”

“Yes yes, I heard from the elders in my family that First Elder has quite a few enemies in the imperial city, and they’re minimally third-rank officials,” said a senior male disciple who lived in the imperial city. Although his family wasn’t as prominent as the Meng Family, it was still considered an influential ancestral clan in the imperial city.

“If you put it that way, then our sect leader is stronger than First Elder. The streets of the imperial city are full of our sect leader’s enemies.”

“You're underestimating our sect leader. It’s not only the imperial city that is full of his enemies—it’s the entire cultivation world. Regardless of whether it’s the Central Continent, the Demon Region, or the Buddhist Kingdom, just find any cultivator who’s lived two thousand years and ask them. Who doesn’t have a grudge against our sect leader?”

“Why does your tone sound somewhat proud?”

“Of course, I’m proud. Despite enemies everywhere, our sect leader is still alive and kicking. That’s skill.”

The nine Fusion cultivators fought in a chaotic battle, each dishing out their mighty abilities. It was as if the heavens were collapsing and the earth was splitting. The commotion was far greater than when Lu Yang was practicing his sword technique.

The hard soil at Heaven’s Gate Peak was like mud in the hands of the elders, manipulated at will. Trees toppled as if swept by a hurricane, completely uprooted and leaving not a blade of grass standing.

The elders first attacked the strongest—the Taciturn Daoist Priest and First Elder. Arrays combined with talismans, and pill-concocting techniques combined with artifact-refinement techniques... These two were no pushovers either; their Sword Dao and dreamscape spells displayed their might, unpredictable and ever-changing.

But under the joint assault of the seven elders, the two still showed signs of fatigue and gradually revealed openings.

Just as the disciples were speculating about who would be the ultimate victor, a puppet shot into the sky and swatted the elders down one by one, as if it was dropping dumplings into a pot. Only when it reached Sixth Elder did it strike a bit more lightly.

Despite their exceptionally talented cultivations, the elders and the sect leader couldn’t retaliate at all. Just like that, they were defeated and crashed to the ground, thoroughly disoriented.

They looked up and saw the puppet standing before them, holding a large bundle of hoes. Without a word, it handed each of them a hoe and pointed at the scene of devastation on Heaven’s Gate Peak.

Its meaning was clear—no one was leaving today until the mess was cleaned up.

Witnessing this sight, Lu Yang felt fortunate that his cultivation was too low to be qualified to participate in battles of this level.

The puppet handed the last hoe to Lu Yang.

Remembering the scene of him performing One Sword Into Ten Thousand Swords, Lu Yang quietly accepted the hoe and joined the elders’ land-levelling crew.

~~~

Outside the Dao-Seeking Sect, Chieftain Jin was still anxiously awaiting news from the Dao-Seeking Sect.

“It’s been a whole day. Why hasn’t Big Brother sent any message? Is the Dao-Seeking Sect too dangerous? Can’t he let me in?

“Or has Big Brother forgotten about me?”

Chapter 742: Immortal

The Taciturn Daoist Priest was a cultivator with a steadfast Dao heart. He had lingered in the Dao-Seeking Sect for three full days just to see the Vast Sea Daoist Lord.

Unfortunately, the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s sincerity failed to move the Vast Sea Daoist Lord, who never showed himself.

Left with no other choice, the Taciturn Daoist Priest had to abandon the idea. After teaching Lu Yang for three days, he swiftly departed.

Lu Yang respected his shifu and abided by the Dao, waving goodbye to the Taciturn Daoist Priest at the mountain gate.

When the Taciturn Daoist Priest was a distance away from the mountain gate, the Fusion cultivators guarding the entrance for several days finally saw that the time was ripe. They swarmed forward, determined to execute the “Old Taciturn Scoundrel” on the spot.

The scene was one of extreme chaos.

Lu Yang was still young and couldn’t bear to witness scenes of parting and death. Fighting back tears, he silently turned around, choosing not to watch the ensuing events.

~~~

Upon returning to Heaven’s Gate Peak, he ran into Yun Zhi, whom he hadn’t seen for three days.

“Big Senior Sister, are you done with the interrogation?”

“It’s done. My stance remains the same: the matter of the Ember Legacy Dynasty is very dangerous. Do not involve yourself.” She pondered for a bit, feeling that her statement might not be intimidating, so she added, “Do you remember the Time Terminus Flower in the herb garden?”

Lu Yang nodded. Of course, I remember. The little herb king, the Time Terminus Flower, was extremely beautiful. Legend said it would only bloom in its most beautiful form when the world ended and living beings were in misery, to the point that even time would freeze for it.

“Previously, I found it strange. According to historical records, no major event could be considered a world-ending catastrophe where living beings were plunged into abject misery. Yet, when the sect’s predecessors found the Time Terminus Flower, it had already bloomed.

“I originally thought the legend was mistaken.

“Until just now, I went to the herb garden and asked the Time Terminus Flower some questions. Only then did I finally confirm that it was precisely during the fall of the Ember Legacy Dynasty that it bloomed.

“Of course, it itself is unaware of this.

“Do you get it now? Someone capable of ending the world and plunging living beings into misery can only be an immortal, and a wicked one at that. This is not an entity you can afford to provoke.”

Lu Yang nodded like a chick pecking grains. With my frail constitution, I certainly won’t involve myself in the matters of the Ember Legacy Dynasty.

“By the way, Big Senior Sister, I remember you saying a while back that there are no immortals in the world. What did you mean by that?” Lu Yang suddenly asked. This was something Yun Zhi had casually mentioned during his first year in the Dao-Seeking Sect, when he was cultivating at Heaven’s Gate Peak and had yet to reach the Foundation Establishment Stage.

But we now have the Five Ancient Immortals, the Qian Emperor, Yu Emperor, Imperial Preceptor, and whatnot—that’s quite a few immortals. How could there be no immortals in the world?

“The ‘immortal’ I was talking about doesn’t refer to cultivators who have condensed a Dao fruit. Regarding this point, Senior Immortal Fairy should understand.

“An immortal does not age or die, is not born nor extinguished, is not bound by lifespan limitations, wanders freely between heaven and earth, and is not constrained by any rules.

“This line is from Words of Sages and is also the original definition of ‘immortal.’ It appeared even earlier than the Nine-Layers Immortals and the others.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy emerged from Lu Yang’s body. “Lass Yun is not wrong. This was the original definition of ‘immortal.’ Later, we gradually figured out the ‘Incipient Dao Fruit’ and the ‘Dao Fruit,’ so we began to call all cultivators who condensed a Dao Fruit ‘immortals.’”

Lu Yang nodded instinctively. “So that’s how it is...” He suddenly realized something amiss in the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s words. “Wait, Immortal Fairy, did you just say ‘we figured out the Incipient Dao Fruit and the Dao Fruit?’”

“That’s right. The Incipient Dao Fruit was something we, the Five Ancient Immortals, came up with.”

“Do you remember that the Epoch Immortal’s original form is the Jianmu Tree? His strength was equivalent to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage.

“When I was at the Qi Training Stage, he was at the Transcendent Tribulation Stage. When I was at the Nascent Soul Stage, he was at the Transcendent Tribulation Stage. When I reached the Transcendent Tribulation Stage, he was still at the Transcendent Tribulation Stage. Why do you think that was the case? Was it because he was unwilling to obtain an Incipient Dao Fruit?”

Lu Yang vaguely sensed a shocking possibility, but he still followed along with the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. “Why is that?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy tittered. “It’s because he alone couldn’t derive the Incipient Dao Fruit. Only until all five of us reached the Transcendent Tribulation Stage and joined forces did we manage to derive the Incipient Dao Fruit.

“Of course, it was mainly thanks to me. The Heaven Mandate Immortal and the others were just freeloaders.

“Back then, after we figured out the Incipient Dao Fruit and the Dao Fruit, when it was time to name them, we thought the title ‘immortal’ was not bad, so we called cultivators who possessed a Dao Fruit ‘immortals.’”

Lu Yang sucked in a cold breath. Immortal Fairy, so you are also one of the founders of the cultivation system, huh?

And your naming sense isn’t bad either. I thought you would have come up with names like “Unbeatable Stage” or something.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy continued, “According to the original definition of ‘immortal,’ there’s indeed no one in this world who can be called an immortal.”

Lu Yang thought that he should perhaps show the Everlasting Immortal Fairy more respect from now on. She’s both a pioneer of the Dao Fruit system and the founder of Buddhism.

“Oh, the Heaven Mandate Immortal was the one who came up with the name ‘immortal.’ My proposals of ‘Unbeatable Stage’ and ‘Doudou Stage’ were unanimously vetoed by them.”

She stamped her foot in anger. “With how much effort I put in, what’s wrong with naming the realms after me? And they still opposed it! How incorrigible!”

Lu Yang, “...”

Immortal Fairy, you could have left out those last few sentences.

~~~

Lu Yang was ultimately someone who had weathered great storms and broadened his horizons alongside the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. After learning this astonishing part of history that could astound both the past and the present, he quickly calmed his mind and still chose to cultivate step by step.

I’m still far from becoming an immortal. There’s no point thinking about things that far.

There is no concept of time in cultivation. Time slips away, days and months shuttle by.

In the blink of an eye, Lu Yang had cultivated for an hour.

“Old Lu, wanna go out and play?” Meng Jingzhou couldn’t stand seeing Lu Yang cultivate. He rushed to Heaven’s Gate Peak and eagerly urged Lu Yang to go out and have some fun—a truly despicable act.

Fortunately, Lu Yang’s heart was like an old Buddha in meditation, unwavered by external influences.

“Let’s go to the East Sea.”

“Let’s go.” Lu Yang leaped up from the large rock.

His Dao heart was not steadfast enough, and he was bewitched by Meng Jingzhou. Just like that, a promising cultivation seedling fell, evoking regretful sighs from bystanders.

“But why did you suddenly think of going to the East Sea?” Lu Yang was puzzled. There must be a reason.

“Isn’t the old horse from the Dragon-Horse Tribe? His hometown is in the East Sea. He wants to visit his family, and I naturally agreed.

“Since the old horse is going to the East Sea, I reckon the two of us can take this opportunity to go together. Neither of us has been to the East Sea before.”

“Good brother.” Lu Yang was touched. Old Meng never forgets me when it comes to good things like going out to have fun.

In truth, Meng Jingzhou had another reason for going to the East Sea.

The past few days, people kept calling him the ‘strongest single’ and encouraged him to remain single to ensure boundless prospects. His face was too thin-skinned to handle such praise, so he wanted to hide outside for some peace and quiet.

The East Sea was a good place—far away and without acquaintances.

There’s no need to tell Lu Yang about this, lest he start praising me too. That would defeat the purpose of going out.

“Just the two of us?”

“I was planning to invite Junior Sister Tao and the other two as well. After all, it’s rare that we get to go on a long trip.”

Chapter 743: Sealing the Bloodline

Upon hearing that she could go to the East Sea with Lu Yang, Tao Yaoye happily agreed.

Li Haoran was the same. Upon hearing they could go out, he immediately agreed, fearing Lu Yang might change his mind.

“Go to the East Sea? Great, great.” Man Gu’s eyes lit up, but then he remembered something and showed a troubled expression.

“What’s wrong?” Lu Yang asked.

“Isn’t the East Sea full of sea tribes? Brother Lu, you know my bloodline. Although it becomes extremely powerful when fighting sea tribes, it also enrages them. I’m worried that as soon as I arrive at the East Sea, I’ll be surrounded by sea tribes before I even do anything.”

Lu Yang recalled that this was the blessing the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had bestowed upon the Ancient Barbarian Tribe.

“That is indeed a problem... Immortal Fairy, do you have any good solutions?” Lu Yang pondered a moment and decided it was quicker to inquire with the culprit directly.

“Of course. Just use the Unbeatable Nascent Soul and beat up all the sea tribes that surround you.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy waved her little fists around with “heihei” and “aha” sound effects, as if there were invisible enemies in the mental space.

“...Is there a more peaceful method?” Lu Yang had always advocated avoiding force whenever possible.

“This immortal could reluctantly enhance the Barbarian boy’s bloodline effect. That way, even Fusion seafolk would grow fearful of him, ensuring you five can roam the East Sea unimpeded. Although this would attract the hatred of Transcendent Tribulation seafolk, how many Transcendent Tribulation cultivators could there be in the East Sea? You won’t run into them.”

“...Can we try another method?” Lu Yang heard that the East Sea had the Dragon Palace and Nine Major Sea Tribes, which meant there were at least ten Transcendent Tribulation cultivators. Furthermore, it was reasonable to assume that a behemoth like the Dragon Palace couldn’t have only the Old Dragon Emperor at the Transcendent Tribulation Stage.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy relented. “Then the only option left is sealing—temporarily sealing the Ancient Barbarian bloodline and removing the seal after leaving the East Sea.”

Lu Yang was overjoyed. “Let’s go with this method!”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy drew an extremely abstruse array.

“What is this?”

“A sealing array. Your cultivation isn’t sufficient to draw it. Have your Second Elder draw it.”

“Gotcha.”

~~~

The group found Grandpa Ba at the entrance of the herb garden. He was lying on a deck chair and humming a comfortable tune, a palm-sized leaf covering his face. Two leaves that were half a person’s height hovered above his head and swayed gently, serving as cattail-leaf fans.

“Grandpa Ba, we need your help with something.”

Grandpa Ba opened his eyes and removed the leaf from his face, looking somewhat uncomfortable under Lu Yang and the others’ earnest gazes. “Just shoot. Don’t look at me like that.”

“The few of us are planning to go play at the East Sea for a couple of days. It’s just that Man Gu’s bloodline tends to draw hatred. Coincidentally, I found a bloodline-sealing array in an ancient text, so we came to ask for your help.”

“I see. That’s easy enough. What does the array look like?”

“Here.” Lu Yang took out the array transcribed from his mental space.

Grandpa Ba took it and marveled, “As expected of an ancient array. The design is exquisite.

“Wait a bit, I’ll get it done in two hours.” For an unfamiliar array, Grandpa Ba would need to study it carefully before he could draw it. Layers, stroke order, and the amount of spirit energy used—these aspects required research and experimentation.

Two hours later, Grandpa Ba had Man Gu lift his shirt. He slapped his belly and left an ancient seal on it.

“Settled. Speaking of which, I’ve sealed someone’s bloodline before, but the sealing array you found is much more elaborate, Lu Yang.”

“Who did you seal it for?” Lu Yang asked curiously.

“A friend I made in my youth—Ao Ran from the East Sea Dragon Palace.”

“You have a friend from the Dragon Palace?” Lu Yang’s group was surprised. They thought the Dao-Seeking Nine was as notorious in the East Sea as they were in the Demon Region. They had even prepared themselves to be enemies of the world.

Grandpa Ba glared at Lu Yang and the others. “What are you talking about? What’s wrong with me having a friend from the Dragon Palace? The one with enemies everywhere is Old Nine.”

Lu Yang uttered, “Oh.” So it’s similar to the situation in the Demon Region. Our mental preparation wasn’t in vain.

“He possesses the purest Dragon bloodline. He asked me to seal most of his bloodline so that the strength he displayed outwardly would be weaker.”

“Why would he do that?” Lu Yang and the others were baffled.

“So that when someone provoked him, he could declare with a dark expression, ‘You forced me to release the seal.’”

Lu Yang, “...”

“Be careful when you go to the East Sea. Although the Dragon Palace keeps order, the situation there is still quite chaotic.”

“Quite chaotic?”

“The East Sea isn’t just home to seafolk; there are humans too. The sea tribes live in the sea, while the humans live on the islands. Due to historical reasons, the two races have longstanding grievances with each other, and conflicts constantly break out. Moreover, it’s outside Great Xia’s jurisdiction, so fights can get out of hand.”

Even Meng Jingzhou was hearing about this for the first time. None of them knew much about the East Sea.

Only Li Haoran had a better understanding of the East Sea due to his past life memories, especially since the Nine-Netherworlds Creed had expanded its operations there or conducted some secret transactions. No matter how long Great Xia’s reach was, it couldn’t extend to the East Sea. The smuggling business the Nine-Netherworlds Creed was currently involved in had been expanded during Qin Haoran’s time as creed leader.

Qin Haoran had another reason for expanding operations overseas—if creditors ever came knocking, he could flee to the East Sea.

Unfortunately, this diabolic path leader was bound by love and trapped himself in Great Xia.

Grandpa Ba kindly reminded them, “By the way, none of you have been to the sea before, so your swimming abilities are probably not great. Before going to the East Sea, it’s best to exchange for a Water-Repelling Pearl, which can help you move freely underwater. They’re available in the Great Mission Hall.”

Unlike the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s Water-Repelling Mantra, which drained moisture from both friend and foe alike, the Water-Repelling Pearl genuinely repelled water.

“Can I ask what Shifu had done in the East Sea?”

“Oh, there’s plenty. For instance, he had an ambiguous relationship with the Dragon Palace’s princess.”

Lu Yang was flabbergasted. Despite Shifu’s old age and fading looks, I didn’t expect him to have been a debonair man in his youth. “Shifu had an ambiguous relationship with the Dragon Palace’s princess?!”

“It wasn’t exactly ambiguous. It’s just that when Old Nine was young, he needed a supreme treasure from the Dragon Palace to save someone. That treasure was the Dragon Palace princess’s favorite magical treasure, which she stored inside her stomach. Thus, Old Nine shrank himself, entered the princess’s stomach, and stole the treasure. After the incident came to light, Old Nine kept calling the Dragon Palace’s princess ‘mommy.’”

Lu Yang, “...”

~~~

The five thanked Grandpa Ba and headed to the Great Mission Hall, each exchanging for a Water-Repelling Pearl. The pearls were exorbitant, but the five had accumulated many contribution points from missions, so the cost was negligible.

When the senior female disciple at the Great Mission Hall saw all five of them exchanging for Water-Repelling Pearls, she quickly called Dai Bufan over.

Dai Bufan initially thought Lu Yang was taking the four somewhere to pull off some grand scheme. He only exhaled a sigh of relief after hearing they were just accompanying the old horse to visit relatives and seizing the chance to play in the East Sea for a couple of days.

“Go on, go on. Have fun.”

Chapter 744: The Search for The Longevity Immortal Herb

The five of them squeezed into the carriage. The old horse’s heart was set on returning home. A journey to the East Sea would usually take four or five days, but this time, they reached the Great Xia border, Ming City, in just half a day.

After having their identities verified, the five entered the city to apply for exit documents.

“Name?”

“Lu Yang?”

“Identity?”

“Disciple of the Dao-Seeking Sect.”

“What is your purpose for going to the East Sea?”

“Travel.”

“Alright, you may proceed.”

“Hmm? Why are there so many people?” Meng Jingzhou noticed three large ships at the departure port. Judging by the insignias on the ship, they belonged to Great Xia’s government.

Is the imperial court sending envoys to visit the East Sea Dragon Palace?

“Excuse me, brother, what are those three large ships about to depart?” Meng Jingzhou randomly stopped a kind-looking passer-by.

“You’re talking about that? I heard those are the fleet organized by the Second Imperial Prince to go out to sea.”

“Why is the Second Imperial Prince going out to sea?”

That person lowered his voice mysteriously. “From what I heard, the Xia Emperor is gravely ill, with little lifespan left. The Second Imperial Prince heard there is a longevity medicine at the East Sea, so he organized three large ships to the East Sea to search for this medicine.”

Meng Jingzhou naturally knew the Xia Emperor had a limited lifespan left, but he hadn’t expected the news to have spread among the common folk.

“Immortal Fairy, does longevity medicine really exist in the world?” Lu Yang asked upon overhearing Meng Jingzhou’s conversation with the passer-by.

“In any case, this immortal doesn’t recall cultivating such an immortal herb.” As the leader of the Everlasting Lineage, she could make everyone in the world live forever if she wished.

“I remember now, I did cultivate it once. That was when the Nine-Layers Immortal was researching the power of yin and yang. He had the jade rabbits and jinwu golden crows mate, but after prolonged mating, they became listless with their energy depleted, so he asked me to think of a solution.

“Hence, I cultivated one Longevity Immortal Herb, ground it into powder, mixed it with water, and fed it to the jade rabbits and jinwu crows.

“From this perspective, this immortal also shares some credit for the Nine-Layers Immortal’s results from the research on yin-yang power.”

Lu Yang clicked his tongue. This Longevity Immortal Herb sounds far more effective than any yang-boosting medicine. The jade rabbits and jinwu crows that the Nine-Layers Immortal bothered to study must have at least been at the Fusion Stage.

“However, one Longevity Immortal Herb can only grant longevity to one person. If a whole bunch of jade rabbits and jinwu crows ate it, it merely prolonged their lifespan and lost the longevity effect.

“Aside from that, I’ve never cultivated a Longevity Immortal Herb again.”

“How is the Longevity Immortal Herb cultivated?” Lu Yang felt that this was a skilled craft; learning it could save the Xia Emperor.

“Simple. Just take a drop of this immortal’s blood and drip it onto any random plant. One drop of blood can cultivate one Longevity Immortal Herb.”

Lu Yang, “...”

It sure is simple, but it can’t be mastered.

“I haven’t heard of the Heaven-Mandate Immortal and the others cultivating longevity herbs either. Those fools probably couldn’t cultivate them either. It’s hard to say for half-immortals.”

“Can half-immortals cultivate Longevity Immortal Herbs too?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy rolled her eyes, her voice languid. “How’s that possible? Half-immortals can’t even achieve longevity themselves, so what Longevity Immortal Herbs can they cultivate?

“If they were a half-immortal from the Everlasting Lineage, such as one with an Undying Incipient Dao Fruit or Imperishable Incipient Dao Fruit, they could cultivate spirit herbs that greatly extend one’s lifespan.

“By the way, Second-in-Command, are you sure you don’t want an Everlasting Incipient Dao Fruit? It’s free, no charge,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy urged Lu Yang again.

“No, I want to rely on my own efforts to cultivate an Incipient Dao Fruit.” I can’t be someone like Li Haoran, eating soft rice and living off women.

Seeing Lu Yang reject her again, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy looked quite regretful. “You’ll need to work hard then. Look at Li Haoran, he’s already a half-immortal, while you’re only at the Two Infants Stage.”

“It’s called the Double Infant Stage... Wait, what do you mean Li Haoran is already a half-immortal?”

“Li Haoran has a Reincarnation Incipient Dao Fruit, so he’s a half-immortal, of course.” As the founder of cultivation realms, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy held the final right of interpretation.

Lu Yang’s expression changed as he turned his gaze toward Li Haoran, who was currently applying for his exit documents. To think that despite Li Haoran having the slowest cultivation progress among us five, he actually has the highest cultivation level.

“What’s your purpose for going to the East Sea?”

“Returning home to visit family.”

“Then I wish you a pleasant family visit.”

“Thank you.”

Lu Yang and the others noticed a commotion behind them after they finished their customs clearance.

“Look, it’s a demon!”

“True, it’s become a demon spirit!”

The five turned around and saw the old horse standing on two legs, one leg resting on the counter and the other holding up the carriage while going through the exit procedures. It was a bizarre scene that appeared completely out of place.

It was no wonder there was such a commotion. Even Lu Yang and the others would have taken a second look.

After the old horse finished saying thank you, he put down the carriage and resumed walking on four legs, passing by five dumbfounded individuals with a gait as steady as an ordinary horse.

“Let’s go, what are you standing around for? Haven’t you seen me walk upright before?” The old horse urged the five inexperienced individuals. Judging by their reaction, they need more training and exposure.

“I thought you were going to stow away to the East Sea, old horse.”

The old horse snorted and ignored Meng Jingzhou. How can I admit that I had originally come to Great Xia as a stowaway and was nearly caught by the authorities?

Such embarrassing matters are best left unsaid.

~~~

“Whoa, it’s the sea!” They were ultimately young at heart. Seeing the blue waves and ocean sprays, they couldn’t help but feel excited.

Tao Yaoye was so excited that she removed her shoes and stepped onto the soft sand, letting the seawater cover her feet. The cool sensation felt inexplicably comfortable, and she kept smiling.

Lu Yang acted better; he had seen the sea in his previous lifetime.

Of course, the sea in his previous life couldn’t compare in size to the East Sea before him, nor would hundred-meter-long whales perform diving acrobatics above the sea in his past life.

They saw a hundred-meter-long whale leap out from the water, soaring a thousand meters high before plunging headfirst back into the sea with a boom, like a bomb exploding on the surface and sending waves rolling.

There were also schools of fish floating on the sea surface, lining up to form a suspended fish bridge. Glittering under the sunlight, it was like a massive bridge cast from gold and silver. Two lovers started from opposite ends, met in the middle, and expressed their feelings to each other in a romantic atmosphere.

Both scenes were distinctive features of the East Sea border. The only difference was that for the former, the whales enjoyed diving, while for the latter, the fish forming a bridge was a paid performance.

The three large ships searching for the Longevity Immortal Herb set sail. The crew members were in high spirits, determined to find the legendary herb and extend the Xia Emperor’s lifespan.

These large ships were built by the most skilled shipbuilding cultivators the Second Imperial Prince could find. Not only were the ships enormous and operated like a small city, with a total of nine deck levels and all kinds of supplies available, but they were also powered by spirit stones. Once they set sail, their speed surpassed that of flying vessels by severalfold, making them arguably the fastest means of transportation on the sea.

Then, the crew saw a horse-drawn carriage galloping rapidly across the sea’s surface. The horse glanced back at the three large ships in disdain before accelerating again, swiftly leaving the ships behind. Faint cheers could even be heard from within the carriage.

After all, no matter how fast the large ships were, they couldn’t outpace a great demon king returning home to visit family.

Chapter 745: Danger, Danger, Extreme Danger!

Faced with the old horse’s rapid pace, the crew members could only stare helplessly as the old horse overtook them.

No matter how desperately they burned spirit stones, such a large ship could never surpass the old horse, unless they asked a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator to step in and carry the large ship while running across the sea surface.

The old horse paid no mind to the three large ships, its four hooves moving swiftly, and even occasionally let out cheerful whinnies.

The Dragon-Horse Tribe was located in the southern part of the East Sea. After leaving the port, the old horse headed straight south.

Ming City’s port was three hundred li from the East Sea. These three hundred li belonged to Great Xia’s territory, but this stretch of ocean was inconvenient for Great Xia to manage. After all, Great Xia couldn’t process exit documents on the sea surface; they could only periodically send cultivators to patrol the waters.

After the old horse ran three hundred li, a mist rose over the sea, making it impossible to distinguish the direction.

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou found this scene familiar. When they went to the Demon Region, they had encountered a similar situation—they had to pass through a fog to reach the Demon Region.

The old horse was very familiar with the mist; he could reach the East Sea even with his eyes closed.

“It seems fog is deployed in all four cardinal directions,” Meng Jingzhou mused. “But for what purpose?”

“Probably to prevent ordinary people from knowing they live inside a giant box,” Lu Yang replied. Judging from things now, the fog isn’t harmful.

“Box? What are you talking about?” Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou’s discussion wasn’t hushed, so Tao Yaoye and the other two heard it.

Among the three, only Li Haoran possessed memories of his past life and wore an expression that indicated he was already aware. Tao Yaoye and Man Gu had never left Great Xia and hadn’t experienced passing through such fog.

“It’s like this. According to Old Meng’s and my research, the Four Ancient Immortals refined the stars into six continents, causing the world to take on the shape of a box...”

After listening to the whole story, Tao Yaoye and Man Gu were flabbergasted. They hadn’t expected the world’s shape to be completely different from what they imagined—they had been living inside a vast, boundless box.

Man Gu's excitement eclipsed his surprise. He knew traveling with Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou would broaden his horizons. “So the Ancient Nameless One finally has a name?” He remembered when he first joined the Everlasting Creed, the branch leader had told the three of them that it was the Ancient Nameless One who refined the stars.

Li Haoran also couldn’t maintain his composure. Qin Haoran’s memories didn’t contain anything about the Four Ancient Immortals refining the stars.

While the five were chatting, the old horse had already pulled them through the mist, arrived at the East Sea, and stopped at an island.

“If this island hasn’t changed its name, it should still be called Douyun Island. This is a gathering place for cultivators in the area. Two months from now, we will reconvene on this island.” The old horse spoke in human tongue again.

This had been agreed upon beforehand. The old horse was returning home to visit family; it couldn’t possibly bring all five of them along.

Lu Yang and the others had travelled to the East Sea for the purpose of seeing the world, not to see the old horse’s relatives.

Hence, before setting out, they had agreed to split up after reaching the East Sea and reconvene at a certain location to return to the Dao-Seeking Sect.

“See you, old horse.”

The five waved goodbye to the old horse.

After alighting from the carriage, the sea breeze brushed against their faces. This was an atmosphere absolutely impossible to experience in Great Xia.

“Where to now?”

“None of us has been to the East Sea before. Let’s get a map first. Alternatively, Junior Brother Li, can you draw a map of the East Sea?”

Li Haoran revealed a troubled expression and sighed. “The last time Qin Haoran came to the East Sea was a hundred years ago. And you all should know that this is the East Sea, not Great Xia.”

“So?”

“So even if mighty experts fight and turn everything upside down, it won’t return to its original state. When sea tribes fighting over territory leads to changes in ownership, the map of the East Sea will also change. Only cultivators who have lived in the East Sea for a long time will know what the current map looks like.

“The sea tribes have a strong sense of territory. I could draw a map from a hundred years ago, but routes that were safe a hundred years ago aren’t necessarily safe now. You wouldn’t want to be shot down by sea tribes while flying, right?”

“That’s quite troublesome, but it’s not a big problem. Didn’t the old horse say that this Douyun Island is a gathering place for East Sea cultivators? There should be maps here.”

“Right. It’s also a good chance to interact with East Sea cultivators.”

After some discussion, considering the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s far-reaching reputation, and given that Grandpa Ba only mentioned he had one friend in the Dragon Palace but didn’t specify how many enemies he had, it was reasonable to infer that, aside from Ao Ran in the Dragon Palace, everyone else was an enemy.

The five put on black cloaks. Lu Yang, Meng Jingzhou, Tao Yaoye, and Man Gu altered their appearances before feeling safe enough to set foot on the island.

Li Haoran didn’t need to change his appearance. Lu Yang and the other three had often gone out on missions and were quite famous, so they might be recognized. However, Li Haoran had barely left the Dao-Seeking Sect, so no one knew him.

“We come from a renowned major sect. Even if we aren’t flamboyant when going out, we shouldn’t have to be this sneaky, right?” Meng Jingzhou grumbled helplessly.

After stepping on the island, Meng Jingzhou realized their attire was common among East Sea cultivators—most wore black robes.

According to Grandpa Ba, East Sea cultivators were usually more or less involved in some trouble, which was why they always acted cautiously. If their deeds were committed in Great Xia, they would face at least three years of imprisonment.

“Anyone who comes to the East Sea to sell clothes would suffer a huge loss.” Meng Jingzhou clicked his tongue, shrewdly dismissing a business opportunity.

Lu Yang shot Meng Jingzhou a sidelong glance. “East Sea cultivators aren’t as perverted as you imagine. They wear black robes over their clothes; they aren’t exhibitionists wearing only a black robe.

“It looks like this is a market district. It’s just that the cultivation levels of these cultivators...”

Lu Yang scanned the area with his spiritual consciousness. The marketplace occupied most of this vast island, and among the bustling crowd of cultivators, there wasn’t even a single Foundation Establishment cultivator.

The cultivators with the highest cultivation were two individuals at the Advanced Qi Training Stage.

Oh wait, it should be called the Great Perfection Level Nine Qi Training Stage.

“What’s there to fear about low cultivation levels? We’re here to ask for a map, not to fight.”

“Fellow Daoist, may I ask if you have a map of the East Sea?” The sociable Meng Jingzhou stopped a passer-by who appeared to be in a hurry.

The passer-by didn’t expect Meng Jingzhou to suddenly grab him and quickly shook off his hand. “Go to the Treasure Pavilion to buy a map! Why are you asking me?” With that, he quickened his pace to get away from Meng Jingzhou.

“I was just asking for directions. Why act so cautiously?” Meng Jingzhou muttered.

Li Haoran had some experience in this regard. “Maps are considered important resources in the East Sea. Not everyone will share such information with you. Why don’t we go to the Treasure Pavilion he mentioned?”

“Might as well.”

The Treasure Pavilion was the largest shop in the Douyun Island market district. One of the two Great Perfection Level Nine Qi Training cultivators whom Lu Yang had detected with his spiritual consciousness was stationed here.

“Dear guests, what would you like to buy? To be frank, our Treasure Pavilion has everything you could want—magical treasures, talismans, array diagrams, visualization paintings...” the steward at the Treasure Pavilion introduced their offerings with a faint pride.

Our Treasure Pavilion Leader is a big shot at the Half-Step Foundation Establishment Stage. He possesses a remnant Foundation Establishment-grade spirit treasure and can be called the number one below the Foundation Establishment Stage!

“Do you have maps?”

“Yes, of course.”

“Give us the best map you have. We want one that marks safe sea zones.”

“Right away.” The steward instructed a disciple to fetch a wooden box from the warehouse.

“Thank you for your patronage. That will be ten spirit stones.”

Meng Jingzhou casually whipped out ten spirit stones without batting an eye, his largesse startling the steward.

Could this person be a Level Seven Qi Training great cultivator?

Meng Jingzhou opened the map, and the other four moved closer to look.

They found that it was indeed a map, but it only covered a twenty-li radius of sea. The marked dangerous locations were all races they had never even heard of.

Little Spirit Fish Tribe: Highest cultivation—Level Eight Qi Training Stage. Dangerous!

Sea Bullock Tribe: Highest cultivation—Level Nine Qi Training Stage. Dangerous!

Ink-Black Octopus Tribe: The old ancestor is suspected to have broken through the Qi Training Stage. Extremely Dangerous!

Chapter 746: Banquet

Meng Jingzhou rubbed his forehead, his tone full of helplessness. “Do you have a larger map? One that perhaps marks locations like the Xuanwu (Black Tortoise) Tribe or the Kunpeng Tribe?”

The steward was startled by Meng Jingzhou’s words. “The Xuanwu Tribe and the Kunpeng Tribe are legendary races! The sea areas they inhabit are forbidden zones for living beings; humans cannot get close. How could we possibly know their locations?”

Meng Jingzhou recalled the Kunpeng Tribe elder who had visited his home during the New Year. The elder seemed quite genial and had even given him lucky yasui money.[1]

Meng Jingzhou was somewhat regretful. The old horse dropped us off too early; he should have at least gone deeper into the East Sea to find a place with Nascent Soul cultivators. This damned place doesn’t even have a Foundation Establishment cultivator.

“Where can we find a Nascent Soul cultivator to ask for directions...” Lu Yang pondered. He suddenly had a flash of insight, realizing he had cornered himself into a dead end.

“We’re worried about being attacked by sea tribes while flying over the sea, which is why we wanted to buy a map and find a safe route.

“But why do we need to find a safe route? We can just fly east and brute-force our way through. After all, the sea tribes around here don’t even have Foundation Establishment cultivators. By the time they react, we’d already be gone.”

Meng Jingzhou saw the light. “Exactly! If we keep flying east, we’re bound to run into Nascent Soul cultivators or seafolk eventually.”

The steward listened to the five’s discussion with trepidation. Could these five be legendary Nascent Soul old monsters?

It’s hard to see a Nascent Soul old monster in a decade, so how had five suddenly popped out today?

The five paid no attention to the steward’s reaction. Having settled on a plan, they immediately soared into the air and prepared to cross the sea.

Lu Yang took out the Qingfeng Sword and skimmed close to the sea’s surface, sending huge sprays of water splashing from both sides.

Meng Jingzhou ran swiftly across the sea surface. As a physique cultivator, he could run faster than flying.

Man Gu took out his hammer and unscrewed the head, leaving only the handle. The handle had small holes and could be used as a jade flute. As a Confucian cultivator, he couldn’t run on the sea surface like Meng Jingzhou; it was unbecoming of a Confucian cultivator’s status.

Tao Yaoye opened her red paper umbrella, and Li Haoran took out a precious gourd he had personally refined.

Displaying their mighty abilities, the five flew toward the depths of the sea, leaving the dumbstruck steward behind.

Just as Lu Yang had predicted, in the presence of five Nascent Soul old monsters, the edges of the East Sea had no dangerous zones.

If anything was dangerous, the five of them would be the greatest danger.

Those seafolk at the Level Nine Qi Training, Foundation Establishment, or even Golden Core stages trembled beneath the sea surface as they watched the five speed fast, fearing they might suddenly stop and pick a fight with them.

Even if a tribe had a Nascent Soul seafolk presiding, they didn’t dare to act rashly in the face of five Nascent Soul cultivators and simply let them fly overhead.

“The periphery of the East Sea is massive. We’ve flown for so long without a single Nascent Soul seafolk coming out to pick a fight with us.”

Lu Yang calculated that they had been flying for three days without even seeing a shadow of a sea tribe.

What the five didn’t know was that when they flew at high speeds, the aura they radiated demonstrated power far exceeding the Nascent Soul Stage. Never mind the Nascent Soul Stage, even those at the Divine Transfiguration Stage were unwilling to confront them head-on. As for the Void Refinement seafolk, they also didn’t dare to show themselves due to their fluctuating cultivation levels.

“Look, there are people over there!” Tao Yaoye exclaimed. It was a small group of people flying through the air like them.

“Let’s go ask them.” Lu Yang veered his Qingfeng Sword toward their direction and approached them. “Greetings, fellow Daoists. May I ask where you are headed?”

The three were amused. “We’re naturally on our way to attend a banquet. Is that not the case for you, fellow Daoists?”

“Banquet?”

“Yes, a banquet hosted by a Fusion old ancestor from a sea tribe. He has widely extended invitations to nearby factions. Anyone at the Nascent Soul Stage or above can attend, regardless of status. If you have the time, you can come along, fellow Daoists.”

“I can go too?” Lu Yang’s interest was piqued. The people before him were only at the Nascent Soul Stage. A banquet hosted by a Fusion old ancestor would surely have many powerful cultivators attending. They could seize this opportunity to find a more detailed map. Judging by this Fusion old ancestor’s magnanimity, he doesn’t appear to be the snobbish type.

This is also a chance to get to know East Sea cultivators.

“Of course. It’s said that old ancestor enjoys a lively atmosphere. As long as one’s cultivation is sufficient, they can attend even without an invitation.”

Lu Yang was elated. There’s such a good thing? “Wait a moment, I’ll call my companions to come along.” He immediately flew back and explained the situation.

“I’ve long heard that the East Sea frequently holds banquets. It’s a unique local trait; we must go.” Meng Jingzhou loved lively places the most and was the first to respond.

Tao Yaoye and the other two also agreed to go to the banquet.

On their way to the banquet, through their conversation, Lu Yang learned that the three were rogue cultivators who occupied an island and called themselves the Fangshan Island Three Heroes.

Lu Yang and the other four said they were from the Five-Elements Sect, which drew repeated exclamations of surprise from the Fangshan Island Three Heroes.

“By the way, I heard there’s a genius in Great Xia named Lu Yang. Do you know him?” they asked.

Lu Yang nodded steadily, ignoring the strange looks from Meng Jingzhou and the other three. “I don’t just know him; I’ve exchanged blows with him. He’s a formidable opponent. Moreover, he has an extremely high prestige in the Dao-Seeking Sect and is a humble person. I heard the Dao-Seeking Sect Leader intended for him to succeed as sect leader, but he refused.”

The Fangshan Island Three Heroes sighed with admiration again, feeling that the genius named Lu Yang was truly remarkable and in a different league from them.

As they approached the banquet venue, they began to see many seafolk and human cultivators in the surroundings.

The eight of them dove into the sea. The Water-Repelling Pearls allowed Lu Yang’s group to move freely underwater without any restrictions on their movement or breathing.

The seabed was covered with coral clusters of various shapes, resembling underwater palaces. Between them, schools of brightly colored fish darted and swam, as magnificent as a rainbow.

As they descended deeper, the light didn’t dim but instead grew brighter.

This wasn’t sunlight penetrating the sea, but rather a majestic and resplendent palace on the seabed that refracted countless light rays, complementing the surrounding underwater scenery to create an unimaginably beautiful sight. Around the palace, pearl oysters and luminous pearls were embedded, shining brilliantly and illuminating the surrounding waters.

Sea tribes of manifold shapes and sizes swam past the eight. This time, Lu Yang and the others finally recognized their origins: The Luoyu[2] Tribe, the Mirage-Clam Tribe, the Yaksha Tribe, the Giant Softshell Turtle[3]...

After confirming their cultivation levels, the eight entered the palace smoothly.

There were a number of Divine Transfiguration and Void Refinement cultivators attending the banquet. As Nascent Soul cultivators, Lu Yang and the others naturally sat at the very back.

With the banquet about to begin, an assortment of spirit fruits and fine wines was laid out on the table. Enhanced by arrays, the fruits didn’t float away, and the wine didn’t mix with the seawater.

“Red Sun Fruit, Energy-Boosting Fruit... This old ancestor is quite generous.” Meng Jingzhou chuckled. These fruits meant nothing to him, but for ordinary Nascent Soul cultivators, they were highly nourishing.

Surveying their surroundings, they saw a lavish display of rows upon rows of tables laden with countless spirit fruits.

Lu Yang overheard someone nearby whispering. “I heard that old ancestor was in Great Xia all this time. He only returned three days ago when his cultivation advanced by leaps and bounds.”

“Great Xia is truly a land of fortuitous opportunities. If it weren’t for their strict governance, I’d really like to go there and carve out a path for myself.”

“You don’t say! I also heard that old ancestor and the Meng Family’s head are sworn brothers. He can even enter and leave immortal sects at will.”

“I wonder if this old ancestor will stay here or return to Great Xia to continue cultivating.”

Lu Yang, “...”

Why does this old ancestor’s experience sound so familiar?

Before Lu Yang could inquire further, the sound of gongs and drums interrupted him, announcing the start of the banquet. A familiar figure appeared at the front of the banquet hall.

A stark contrast from his usual appearance, the old horse had a young mare on each side. The young mares looked shy, their cheeks flushed. The old horse occasionally teased the two mares, making them even more abashed.

With a hearty laughter, the old horse raised a wine cup high, appearing to be in a great mood. “This banquet is to celebrate my return from Great Xia. Everyone, feel free to relax and enjoy yourselves.”

“Old Ancestor, please share with us your experiences in Great Xia,” a planted shill requested loudly.

The old horse didn’t refuse and began narrating, with a hint of boasting. “My trip to Great Xia was immensely rewarding. Having lived in immortal sects for a long time, I encountered countless opportunities and met numerous Transcendent Tribulation cultivators. Even when I didn’t want to see those Transcendent Tribulation cultivators, they would rush over, and I couldn’t stop them at all.”

“Old Ancestor, then you must have seen Transcendent Tribulation cultivators in action, right?” the shill continued loudly, looking at the old horse in admiration.

“Battles between Transcendent Tribulation cultivators are nothing. This old ancestor has even seen half-immortals fight. It was truly an eye-opener, a scene one couldn’t imagine in a lifetime without witnessing it in person.

“Come come come, let’s drink!” The old horse raised his cup and downed it in one go.

“To the Old Ancestor!” the crowd below chorused in unison, also finishing their cups.

The old horse was in high spirits. He stepped down from the platform and clinked cups with cultivators one by one, drinking cup after cup until he was thoroughly drunk.

The cultivators were overwhelmed by the honor.

The old horse drank his way from the very front of the banquet to the very back.

“Come, drink!”

The old horse raised his cups and looked up, making eye contact with Lu Yang.

“...”

They gazed at each other in silence.

1. This is money given to children by elders during the Chinese New Year. They are often packed in red envelopes, which is why you may have seen the terms “hongbao” or “red envelope/packet.” The term “yasui (压岁)” is also a homophone for “yasui (压祟),” which means something like suppressing evil spirits. This tradition and the hongbao symbolize luck and prosperity. Nowadays, the hongbao can come in all sorts of shapes and designs. In fact, some even do away with the physical hongbao and send e-hongbao! ☜

2. The luoyu is a mythical fish with bird wings and cries like a yuanyang (mandarin duck). Its appearance heralds a flood, warning people to evacuate and seek shelter. ☜

3. Although the English name is Cantor’s giant softshell turtle, frog-faced softshell turtle, or simply Asian giant softshell turtle, and its scientific name is Pelochelys cantorii, the Chinese name is just one character: 鼋 (yuan). This is a rare character, and it only has one meaning—softshell turtles. ☜

Chapter 747: True Lord Horse

The moment the old horse saw Lu Yang, he mostly sobered up.

Although Lu Yang had altered his appearance, the old horse hadn’t just met him yesterday. He was always present when Lu Yang changed his appearance.

The old horse shifted his gaze to the four people beside Lu Yang, and he completely sobered up.

Wait, why are you five here?

Do you know how far this place is from where I dropped you off? Even if you had flown at full speed, it should have taken three days to get here!

Did you run straight to my home right after I dropped you off?

Although the Dragon-Horse Tribe couldn’t compare to the Ten Great Races like the Kunpeng and the Xuanwu, it still held considerable status in the East Sea. According to Great Xia’s sect ranking system, it could be classified as a first-class sect.

Along with the old horse’s return, the Dragon-Horse Tribe’s status among the sea tribes had risen by half a level.

After all these years of cultivation, the old horse had become the undisputed number one expert of the Dragon-Horse Tribe. Even the Chieftain or the Grand Elder was no match for him.

Now that the old horse had returned to his hometown in glory, he naturally wanted to show off wantonly.

For this end, he had specifically dropped Meng Jingzhou and the others off at the East Sea border. He figured that with their methods—asking for direction, finding a map, and so on—it would take at least ten days to reach the depths of the East Sea. This wasn’t even counting any trouble they might stir up along the way. If something else happened on the road, they might not even reach in half a month.

Unexpectedly, despite agreeing to meet again in two months, they had run into each other after only three days, and in such an awkward situation at that.

“Fellow Daoist, offer a toast to True Lord Horse,” the Fangshan Island Three Heroes reminded through an auditory message upon seeing Lu Yang frozen in place.

Although this True Lord Horse from the Dragon-Horse Tribe seems amiable, he is a Fusion cultivator after all. If he gets offended, even a minor action from him won’t be something a Nascent Soul cultivator can withstand.

“True Lord Horse, I offer you a toast,” Lu Yang said respectfully. As Yun Zhi’s junior brother, the Second-in-Command of the Everlasting Lineage, the Young Creed Leader of the Heavenly Court Creed, and the Phoenix Ancestor’s senior brother, he was affable and carried no airs, even treating seniors with utmost courtesy.

“True Lord Horse, we offer you a toast.” Meng Jingzhou and the other three came forward to join in on the fun, struggling to hold back their laughter.
