“True Lord Horse, do you know these five people?” The old horse’s follower, the Dragon-Horse tribesman who had earlier served as the straight man, asked perceptively. He noticed the odd atmosphere between the old horse and Lu Yang’s group.

“Of course, we know each other. We had the honor of meeting True Lord Horse at the Dao-Seeking Sect,” Lu Yang replied with a hearty laugh.

“Ah, yes, I know them. They are from Great Xia’s... Where in Great Xia are you from now?”

“The Five-Elements Sect.”

“Yes, they are prodigies from the Five-Elements Sect. They’re truly extraordinary, pillars of talent that will surely achieve great things in the future.” The old horse surmised that Lu Yang and the others wouldn’t dare reveal their true identities and praised them effusively.

“The Five-Elements Sect, one of the Five Great Immortal Sects?” someone exclaimed. This is an incredible background! No wonder the old ancestor values these five so highly.

A significant number of sea tribes even considered marrying off their younger generations as an investment.

One advantage of the seafolk was their high fertility. Even if the investment failed, it wouldn’t matter much, and if it succeeded, the benefits would be immense.

Meng Jingzhou nodded repeatedly. “True Lord Horse has a formidable reputation in our Great Xia. In recent years, there have been several battles involving Transcendent Tribulation cultivators and half-immortals in Great Xia, and True Lord Horse was present at all of them. He moved freely and remained unscathed in those battles, displaying extremely sophisticated methods. Even those Transcendent Tribulation cultivators addressed him respectfully by adding ‘old’ before his name.

“Despite the strict management of access to the Dao-Seeking Sect, True Lord Horse is an exception. He can enter the sect at will, with no one stopping him.”

The crowd let out gasps of surprise. Having disciples from a Great Xia immortal corroborate this further illustrates how successfully True Lord Horse is thriving in Great Xia.

~~~

After the banquet ended, the old horse secretly sought out Lu Yang’s group and transmitted an auditory message. Following the instructions, they came to a side hall of the palace.

“What are all of you doing here?” The old horse wore a strange expression. He had been holding this question back throughout the entire banquet and was dying to know the answer.

Lu Yang showed an innocent look. “Well, this is our first time in the East Sea. We’re unfamiliar with the place, so we figured we should find a place with many high-level cultivators to buy a map, and we coincidentally came here.”

“It was really a coincidence.” Lu Yang emphasized repeatedly that today’s meeting was an accident.

The old horse, “...”

Had I known earlier, I shouldn’t have left in such a hurry. If I’d left a map, nothing would have happened today.

“Wait here, I’ll get you a map.” The old horse’s face was dark. He hadn’t returned to the East Sea for over a hundred years and didn’t have a ready map on hand.

Before long, the old horse returned with five jade slips in his mouth. These jade slips contained the most detailed maps he could find in a short time.

Lu Yang and the other four activated the jade slips with their spiritual consciousness and finally saw the full view of the East Sea. It was indeed much more detailed than the map sold for ten spirit stones at the Treasure Pavilion. It depicted everything, including the Ten Great Races of the East Sea, islands inhabited by humans, and even those lesser sea tribes.

After seeing off Lu Yang’s group, the old horse’s mood improved tremendously. With Lu Yang’s group at the banquet, he had felt restrained and hadn’t been able to truly let loose.

“Should I find another reason to hold a banquet? What reason would be good...”

Sea tribes enjoyed holding banquets. This was a tradition left by the Dragon Tribe since ancient times.

~~~

“Back in ancient times, we also often held banquets,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy remarked. Witnessing the Dragon-Horse Tribe’s banquet, she couldn’t help but reminisce. “Especially Zhu Tian; he would sing and dance, making it especially lively.”

Since entering the East Sea, Lu Yang’s mental space had been transformed beyond recognition by the Everlasting Immortal Fairy again—it was now filled with seawater. The Everlasting Immortal Fairy had turned herself into a jiao-folk, with a human upper body and a fish tail, and was swimming around in the water leisurely.

A water bed floated on the sea surface. Whenever the Everlasting Immortal Fairy got tired from playing, she could just sleep on it. It was quite convenient.

Lu Yang felt that if he shook his head slightly, he could hear the sound of seawater.

“Second-in-Command, you need to cultivate diligently. Your current mental space still isn’t big enough,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy earnestly advised, urging Lu Yang not to grow complacent or lazy.

“Yes yes yes, I will definitely work hard in cultivating to clear out more space for you to play, Immortal Fairy.”

“What a pity, this place is too far from the Demon Region. Otherwise, we could call Zhu Tian over and organize a banquet in the East Sea.” The banquet the Everlasting Immortal Fairy referred to was the legendary banquets of immortals. They were grand and magnificent, on a scale completely different from the Dragon-Horse Tribe’s.

Lu Yang thought, Zhu Tian is the ruler of the Demon Region after all. Immortal Fairy, can’t you save some face for him?

He recalled Zhu Tian calling him “big brother” multiple times and stuffing four monarch chairs into his hands before departing. His attitude is extremely sincere.

“Fellow Daoists, are you planning on heading anywhere in the East Sea? If you don’t mind, why not come visit Fangshan Island?” The Fangshan Island Three Heroes invited Lu Yang and the others.

It was rare for them to encounter cultivators from Great Xia, especially those from a top-tier faction like the Five-Elements Sect. Naturally, they wanted to seize this opportunity to interact with the other party as much as possible.

“Sure,” Meng Jingzhou agreed readily. Since they had nothing else to do, they might as well visit Fangshan Island.

Chapter 748: Spirit Vein

Upon learning that Lu Yang and the others were disciples of the Five-Elements Sect, aside from the Fangshan Island Three Heroes, many other factions extended olive branches[1], hoping they would visit their territories. A number even hinted at marrying their daughters to them to form marriage alliances.

With such a comparison, Lu Yang and the others felt the Fangshan Island Three Heroes were more reliable.

When they arrived at Fangshan Island, Lu Yang discovered that the so-called Fangshan Island wasn’t a single island but the name of an archipelago, with numerous small islands surrounding the main island like stars.

According to the Three Heroes, the main island of Fangshan Island possessed an upper fourth-grade spirit vein, which made many Nascent Soul cultivators green with envy. Legend said that a natural treasure lay hidden beneath the spirit vein, but of course, that was merely a legend; no one had ever seen it.

Spirit veins were also a specialty of the East Sea. Lu Yang had heard that a first-grade spirit vein could aid a Qi Training cultivator in cultivation, a second-grade spirit vein could aid a Foundation Establishment cultivator in cultivation, and so on.

Spirit veins of the same grade could further be divided into upper, middle, and lower classes. An upper fourth-grade spirit vein was the best a Nascent Soul cultivator could obtain.

The Three Heroes were the masters of Fangshan Island. Several families, rogue cultivators, and countless mortals relied on them, totaling nearly a million people. The mortals lived by the sun, rising and resting with it, their primary purpose being to produce potential cultivation seedlings. Basic Qi Training cultivators filled various roles, such as serving as spirit farmers to plant spirit grains.

Fangshan Island was like a small kingdom, which astonished Lu Yang and the others.

“Masters.” Female attendants were already waiting on Fangshan Island for the Three Heroes’ return.

The female attendants were comely and had been carefully selected and trained by the families of Fangshan Island.

Hero Yan, the leader of the Three Heroes, invited the five to the main hall and had the female attendants bring tea.

“Wait a moment.” Lu Yang stopped the female attendant, making Hero Yan nervous, wondering if he had somehow offended Lu Yang.

Lu Yang covered his identity jade pendant with his hand. It bore the name ‘Dao-Seeking Sect’ and mustn’t be seen by Hero Yan.

“Let’s brew this instead. We’re more accustomed to drinking this,” Lu Yang said with a smile, handing the female attendant a packet of tea.

Catching a whiff of the tea’s fragrance, Hero Yan’s pupils constricted sharply. “This is...”

“Wudao Enlightenment Tea?”

“It really is Wudao Enlightenment Tea?!”

“What, have you drunk it before, Hero Yan?”

How could Hero Yan have had the privilege to drink such tea? He had been fortunate enough to attend a banquet organized by a few Fusion cultivators. One of the Fusion experts had mysteriously brought out a treasure, which was Wudao Enlightenment Tea. The other Fusion cultivators wanted some, but he refused. Only after much persuasion did he brew a pot for everyone to share.

On the other hand, the packet Lu Yang brought out wasn’t just enough to brew one pot—it would be more than sufficient to brew a whole basin.

Lu Yang didn’t lack Wudao Enlightenment Tea. Putting aside other sources, the herb garden had a Wudao Enlightenment Tea Tree King. The tea Yun Zhi drank was plucked from that tree king. With Lu Yang’s relationship with the little herb kings, obtaining a few packets of Wudao Enlightenment Tea was effortless. And this was without factoring in the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s innate suppressive effect on spirit plants.

After the Wudao Enlightenment Tree was brewed, the Three Heroes carefully lifted their cups to drink it, as if they were partaking of immortal pills and spirit medicine.

This fragrance is even more mellow than the one at the banquet!

Hero Yan gazed at Lu Yang and the others with more awe.

“Hero Yan, could you introduce us to the factions of the East Sea?” Lu Yang wanted to match them to the markings on the map.

Having received their generosity, Hero Yan shared everything he knew. “The East Sea can be divided into two major factions: the seafolk and the humans. The seafolk have ten supreme races: the Dragon Tribe, the Kunpeng Tribe, the Kui[2] Tribe... All these races have Transcendent Tribulation demon emperors, especially the Dragon Tribe, whose foundation is unfathomable. No one knows how many Transcendent Tribulation cultivators they have. It’s said the Old Dragon Emperor has lived for nine thousand years.

“Below the Ten Great Races are tribes like the Dragon-Horse Tribe, the Mirage-Clam Tribe, the Jiao-Folk Tribe, the Yaksha Tribe, the Dragon-Human Tribe, and so on. These sea tribes all have Fusion great demon kings presiding over them.

“The races below are too numerous to count, like the Sea Spider Tribe, the Spirit Fish Tribe, and whatnot. These tribes have Divine Transfiguration cultivators overseeing them, but whether they have any Divine Transfiguration cultivators is unknown.”

In the East Sea, Void Refinement cultivators would try their best to keep a low profile and hide news of their breakthrough to prevent enemies from learning they were at the Void Refinement Stage and coming for them.

“Compared to the seafolk, the human side is weaker. For self-protection, they formed the East Sea Cultivators Alliance. The main proponents of the alliance were the three immortal islands—Penglai, Fangzhang, and Yingzhou. These are also the three factions with the most say in the alliance. The Transcendent Tribulation old ancestors from these three sects serve as Alliance Leader and Vice Alliance Leaders.

“Among the alliance, the factions with Fusion cultivators include...

“The threshold for joining the alliance is the Foundation Establishment Stage. These people are considered ordinary members in the alliance. When they reach the Golden Core Stage, they will be considered senior members.

“We three brothers hold the position of administrators in the alliance. Above us are hall leaders, elders, and so on.”

After the series of explanations, Lu Yang gained a basic understanding of the East Sea’s factions. Your East Sea really has a lot of rank classifications. And after all these classifications, the Alliance Leader wouldn’t even qualify as one of the Four Regents in our Heavenly Court Creed.

Hero Yan seized the opportunity during the conversation to ask questions regarding cultivation.

In truth, they felt somewhat embarrassed. They had originally intended to bring out good things and show their hospitality in exchange for cultivation advice, but once Lu Yang brought out the Wudao Enlightenment Tea, none of their good things were of any use.

This one packet of tea could buy several Fangshan Islands.

They could only be thick-skinned and ask.

Although Lu Yang’s group cultivated strange nascent souls, they were fairly knowledgeable about traditional cultivation methods. Cultivation problems that had plagued the Three Heroes for decades were resolved with just a few words of guidance from Lu Yang’s side, and it earned deep admiration from the Three Heroes.

The only difficult question was the one Hero Yan asked. “How should one make use of the nascent soul in combat?”

Lu Yang contemplated. I’m still getting beaten up by my Unbeatable Nascent Soul, Meng Jingzhou’s dual nascent souls are unprecedented, Man Gu’s ancestor-manifesting nascent soul clearly doesn’t have reference value, and Li Haoran’s dismembered nascent soul isn’t much better.

After considering everyone, only Tao Yaoye’s nascent soul is reliable.

“By the way, we have always resided in the Central Continent and have never seen a spirit vein. Could you satisfy our curiosity, Hero Yan?” Meng Jingzhou asked.

Among the five, only Li Haoran had seen a spirit vein before from his past life memories.

“Of course,” Hero Yan agreed with a smile.

Generally speaking, a spirit vein was the lifeblood of an island, a forbidden area not to be shown to outsiders. But since Lu Yang had brought out Wudao Enlightenment Tea, the five couldn’t be considered outsiders anymore.

“This way, please.”

The Three Heroes personally led the way, inviting the five into a mountain cave. They held lamps to illuminate the path ahead.

The cave was winding. The deeper they went, the more they could feel the change in spirit qi concentration. After walking for about ten minutes, the cave gradually brightened, becoming even brighter than the Three Heroes’ lamps.

“We’re here.” The Three Heroes extinguished their lamps and gestured for the group to proceed.

Up ahead was a clear, azure spring protected by an array. The spring water emitted glowing spirit qi, which flowed through underground channels to various parts of Fangshan Island. The branching veins that extended from the spring water formed second and third-grade spirit veins.

Suddenly, the ground shook, and the spirit vein boiled. Abundant spirit qi burst through the array, and cyan-green ripples appeared in the sky.

Hero Yan’s expression changed. “Unusual phenomenon! A natural treasure is about to emerge!”

Lu Yang quickly raised his hand to prove his innocence. “This has nothing to do with me.”

1. The expression “extend/offer an olive branch” actually originates from the Noah’s ark in the Book of Genesis. After the flood receded, Noah released pigeons to check the situation. When the pigeons brought back fresh olive branches, it signified that the flood had subsided and symbolized peace. This phrase is now often used in diplomatic relations, where holding out an olive branch expresses one party’s wish to seek reconciliation or simply build friendly ties. ☜

2. The kui is a one-legged mythical beast that resembles a dragon. It is said to live in Liupo Mountain at the East Sea. The Yellow Emperor used its skin to make a war drum. The character is also used in classical texts to refer to a legendary musician. ☜

Chapter 749: Another Distinctive Feature of the East Sea

The Fangshan Island Three Heroes looked at Lu Yang in surprise, not understanding why he suddenly felt the need to prove he wasn’t involved.

Legends of a rare treasure have long existed on Fangshan Island. Now that it has finally emerged, how could it be related to newcomers?

“Uh, this might have something to do with me.” Tao Yaoye raised her hand awkwardly, looking somewhat embarrassed, attracting everyone’s attention.

“I felt something beneath the spirit establishing a connection with me.” As she spoke, the spirit vein boiled even more fiercely, bursting skyward.

A flash of blue light appeared, and a palm-sized, shimmering green grass with three leaves swayed in the air.

Lu Yang and the others didn’t recognize this green grass.

“Immortal Fairy, do you know what this is?”

“This thing is the Metamorphic Immortal Grass, I think. Judging by its appearance, it must be quite old.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy recognized its origin with a glance.

“Metamorphic Immortal Grass? What is its relation to Junior Sister Tao’s Metamorphic Immortal Physique?”

“The Metamorphic Immortal Grass is an immortal grass that someone with a Metamorphic Immortal Physique cultivated for themselves. Consuming it can greatly shorten the cultivation process, saving at least a hundred years of effort in cultivation, or even over a thousand years. I reckon this was left behind by someone with a Metamorphic Immortal Physique. Maybe they forgot to eat it or died before they could. It remained here until it sensed the Metamorphic Immortal Physique within Lass Tao, prompting it to emerge.

“Of course, others can consume this thing too.”

Lu Yang was slightly taken aback. Saving at least a hundred years of effort in cultivation? Isn’t it too effective?

After all, I’ve only been cultivating for three years.

“However, this immortal suggests you don’t consume it now. This Metamorphic Immortal Grass can still be replanted.”

Lu Yang appropriated the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s knowledge and shared it with everyone, drawing looks of admiration.

As the Metamorphic Immortal Grass emerged, the spirit vein became even more active, and the spirit qi concentration rose to an entirely new level.

Previously, the Metamorphic Immortal Grass was rooted deep within the spirit vein, absorbing spirit energy. Now that it had emerged, the spirit vein’s true grade was revealed.

Fangshan Island’s spirit vein wasn’t at the fourth grade, but at the fifth grade!

But the Three Heroes weren’t happy. Instead, they felt a sense of impending doom.

“Oh no!” Hero Yan’s expression shifted drastically.

“What’s wrong?” Lu Yang and the others didn’t understand.

“With a rare treasure emerging and causing an unusual phenomenon, the surrounding cultivators must have noticed.

“Although they may not recognize the Metamorphic Immortal Grass, when they discover the spirit vein has upgraded from fourth to fifth grade, they’ll definitely guess that the treasure had previously siphoned away most of the spirit vein’s power.

“Even if they don’t know what it is, they can tell that it is a treasure capable of absorbing vast amounts of spirit energy. They will realize it’s something priceless.

“You live in Great Xia, so you don’t understand the East Sea’s rules. In the East Sea, the rule is that treasures belong to the capable! People will come to seize the immortal grass!”

As East Sea cultivators, the Three Heroes were the first to detect the underlying danger. The emergence of the immortal grass is a calamity, not a blessing! This was also a distinctive trait of the East Sea.

A terrifying oppressive pressure descended, accompanied by an aged voice.

“Yan Chuan, this old man has arrived. Why are you not coming out to greet me?!”

“It’s the alliance’s hall leader, Gao Feng! He lives near Fangshan Island!” Hero Yan recognized the other party’s identity just by the voice.

“What’s his cultivation level?” Lu Yang asked with interest.

“Apex Basic Divine Transfiguration Stage!”

The Three Heroes dared not slight Gao Feng and hurriedly left the spirit vein to go out and greet him.

Gao Feng’s gaze was cold as he hovered in the air, staring icily at the Three Heroes. “A rare treasure has emerged in Fangshan Island. Hand it over to spare your island from unnecessary disaster.”

Hero Yan trembled, steeling himself despite his fear. “Senior Gao, the alliance’s rules stipulate that members are not to forcibly seize things from each other.”

Gao Feng was unmoved. “Forcibly seize? If you willingly give it to me, how can that be considered forcibly seizing?”

As he spoke, a figure burst forth from the sea, looking at the Three Heroes with a smirk. “Yan Chuan, Fangshan Island is fortunate. As your neighbor, it’s not too much to ask for a share of the soup, right?”

It was the Tiger Shark Tribe Chieftain, Fangshan Island’s neighbor. His cultivation was at the upper-level Basic Divine Transfiguration Stage.

These two were the closest Divine Transfiguration cultivators in the area.

“Heh, this is something our Five-Elements Sect has set our sights on. How dare some random thing have designs on it?” Lu Yang sneered.

Meng Jingzhou and the others walked out of the cave one after another to keep up appearances.

“You’re the Five-Elements Sect disciples from True Lord Horse’s banquet!” Gao Feng wavered upon seeing Lu Yang, and so did the Tiger Shark Tribe Chieftain.

I’m not afraid of the Five-Elements Sect. The East Sea is far away. Surely they won’t dare to extend their reach here just because I bullied a few disciples?

Although the East Sea was chaotic internally, it was united against outsiders. The alliance’s higher-ups wouldn’t allow the Five-Elements Sect to interfere.

Who I fear is True Lord Horse.

Gao Feng gritted his teeth and didn’t even leave a threatening remark before turning to leave.

The Tiger Shark Tribe Chieftain’s face was so dark that water could drip from it. He jumped back into the sea, pretending nothing had happened.

Seeing the two great Divine Transfiguration cultivators leave, the Three Heroes heaved a sigh of relief. What a close shave.

“Is that it?” Man Gu scratched his head. Given the earlier atmosphere, he thought a fight was inevitable.

“It’s naturally not that simple.” Lu Yang shook his head. “Gao Feng temporarily left because he was afraid of angering the old horse. In that case, wouldn’t it be fine as long as he doesn’t let the old horse find out it was him?

“If it were me, I wouldn’t rob openly. I’d wait until night, cover my face, rob, and then run. Who would know it was me?”

Meng Jingzhou shook his head lightly, thinking that Gao Feng’s approach was quite unskilled. “That shows a lack of experience. Attempting robbery during the day and then succeeding at night with a covered face still makes you a suspect.

“If it were me, I wouldn’t come during the day at all. I’d just rob at night with my face covered. I’d be clear of suspicion then.”

Li Haoran added, “But there’s also a chance to salvage it. Gather more people at night to increase the number of suspects. That way, Gao Feng becomes relatively safer.”

Lu Yang, Meng Jingzhou, and Li Haoran discussed criminal methods back and forth, leaving the Three Heroes stunned.

Aren’t you disciples of the righteous path? I thought you’d never been to the East Sea before. Why are you so familiar with all this?

Man Gu hurriedly took out paper and brush to record the trio’s discussion. As expected of role models, adapting to the local way of thinking so quickly.

Tao Yaoye stared at Man Gu with a peculiar expression. Are you learning their methods, or are you taking notes on them?

Sure enough, as darkness fell, figures clad in black robes and with their faces covered appeared one after another. They stared at Fangshan Island with greedy expressions, like grim reapers.

“So Fangshan Island has a rare treasure that is comparable to a fifth-grade spirit vein.”

“Why not take Fangshan Island for ourselves while we’re at it? Yan Chuan’s trio is only at the Nascent Soul Stage. It’s such a waste for them to occupy such a good spirit vein.”

Following Lu Yang’s instructions, the Three Heroes had evacuated the people from the main islands to the smaller surrounding islands in advance.

“One, two, three... twelve. That’s quite a few people, and they’re all at the Divine Transfiguration Stage.” Lu Yang stretched his limbs, a smile on his visage.

“Since we’ve come to the East Sea, we should naturally enjoy its distinctive culture. We’ve already enjoyed the banquets; now it’s time to try out the fighting.”

Chapter 750: Did You Think Our Five-Elements Sect is Easy to Bully?!

“Twelve Divine Transfiguration cultivators—fighting them will be a bit difficult.” Despite saying it was difficult, the smile on Lu Yang’s visage was impossible to conceal.

In Great Xia, it was rare to encounter anyone willing to fight with him, especially in a life-or-death struggle.

It’s a pity that I can’t fully display my cultivation.

Lu Yang fondly remembered the Qingzhou Grand Ceremony, where he fought peers around his age, going up against Foundation Establishment cultivators as a Golden Core cultivator.

The East Sea’s conditions were crude; if he couldn’t find Foundation Establishment cultivators, he would have to make do with Divine Transfiguration cultivators.

Meng Jingzhou and the others were excited. It was a rare chance for them to fight to their hearts’ content.

“I thought they would bring Nascent Soul cultivators too.” Tao Yaoye was puzzled since this differed from her expectations.

Lu Yang explained, “This is a covert operation. The fewer people involved, the better. Moreover, those who participate in the covert operation must share the spoils; it’s hush money. If the Divine Transfiguration cultivators can handle it themselves, why bring Nascent Soul cultivators to make up the numbers?”

Although Lu Yang had never done such things before, that didn’t prevent him from putting himself in their shoes.

Among the twelve Divine Transfiguration cultivators, some were at the intermediate or advanced stage. They probably weren’t all human, with some being seafolk. Lu Yang guessed the organizer wasn’t Gao Feng, for the latter couldn’t command so many Divine Transfiguration cultivators.

It was likely the emergence of the rare treasure that attracted Divine Transfiguration cultivators from farther away, and they arrived later simply due to the distance. After rushing over, they heard from Gao Feng that the Five-Elements Sect was here, so they devised this plan.

Lu Yang didn’t bother with the accuracy of his speculations. He would fight first and think later.

Despite facing the encirclement of twelve Divine Transfiguration cultivators, Lu Yang dared to strike first. The Qingfeng Sword reflected the moonlight overhead, shining frighteningly bright.

Aside from knowledgeable cultivators like the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord, few noticed what sword Lu Yang was using. Even if he claimed to be from the Five-Elements Sect, he could still use the Qingfeng Sword.

Sword qi shot out like a silk ribbon. The sword’s momentum resembled a rainbow, and the sword intent pierced through the air. Upon seeing the sword qi approach, those Divine Transfiguration cultivators lost their composure and hastily dodged.

“As expected of a disciple from a Great Xia immortal sect! A mere Nascent Soul cultivator can unleash sword qi capable of injuring us!”

“I heard the Five-Elements Sect is internally divided into five branches based on the five elements. He seems to be from the Metal Branch of the sect!”

Noticing the Divine Transfiguration cultivators thrown into disarray, Meng Jingzhou and the others seized the opportunity to attack.

Meng Jingzhou transformed into a Buddhist protector, performing Three Heads Six Arms and sweeping everything before him.

Man Gu invoked his ancestors to possess him, wielding his massive hammer with tiger-like might. Someone like Gao Feng would have their bones broken upon contact.

Li Haoran’s entire body blazed with true fire, splitting into six parts that attacked from different directions.

Tao Yaoye’s red paper umbrella opened, setting up an illusory domain. She moved effortlessly within the illusions, constantly pulling opponents into them.

However, these Divine Transfigurations were not to be belittled; there was a reason they had thrived in the East Sea. Upon discerning that Lu Yang’s and Meng Jingzhou’s combat prowess surpassed the others, they sent six Divine Transfiguration cultivators to engage them. On the other hand, Tao Yaoye and the others had to fight one against two.

“Blue Sea Tide Surge Mantra!”

The calm sea surface surged with colossal waves, forming walls of water. The sharp sword qi collided with the water walls, dividing them into two, but the sword qi was significantly diminished.

“Frenzied Whale Subjugation Fist!”

The Whale and Shark tribes had always been enemies. This was a lethal fist technique developed by the Whale Tribe to deal with the Shark Tribe. However, to the Three Heroes’ knowledge, there were no Divine Transfiguration cultivators in the nearby Whale Tribe.

“Abyssal Chains!”

The cultivator flicked his sleeves, and black, barbed chains clattered out. Li Haoran’s sharp eyes instantly recognized that these chains had weathered endless trials. They were overflowing with baleful energy, and one could only wonder how many people it had whipped to death.

The chains were agile, flying through the air and lashing out at Li Haoran until he was covered in wounds.

East Sea cultivators often practiced multiple combat techniques in secret. The moves they used tonight were the ones they wouldn’t normally employ. Regardless of whether they succeed, their identities wouldn’t be traced.

“Ice Dragon Roar!” The sea surface froze, and an ice dragon suddenly burst forth, repelling Lu Yang.

“Whale Devours Heaven and Earth Fist!”

“Frenzied Shark Subjugation Fist!”

“Luminous Long Fist!”

Three Divine Transfiguration cultivators dragged Meng Jingzhou into the sea, executing three different fist techniques. They stealthily activated secret arts, stimulating their bloodlines, and their combat power instantly soared. Meng Jingzhou was caught off guard and knocked into the bottom of the ocean.

“The so-called immortal sect disciples are nothing special.” The cultivator who had used the Blue Sea Tide Surge Mantra laughed, a hint of mockery in his eyes. Fortunately, I had prepared thoroughly and brought enough people. Otherwise, if only five Divine Transfiguration cultivators had come, we really couldn’t have handled these immortal sect prodigies.

“We don’t wish to antagonize the immortal sects either. As long as you hand over the newly emerged treasure and leave Fangshan Island right away, we’ll let this matter pass!”

They wanted not only the immortal grass but also the fifth-grade spirit vein!

Lu Yang stabilized himself in the air, glaring coldly at his three opponents. “East Sea cultivators are truly something else. How dare you look down on our Five-Elements Sect? Do you think we’re made of clay?!

“Everyone, where are you?!” Lu Yang hollered.

“Here!”

Meng Jingzhou burst out from the sea, steam rising from his body as his abundant yang energy evaporated the seawater.

Man Gu’s eyes were blood-red. This time, he had invoked a Barbarian general who was a subordinate to the first Xia Emperor and had fought on the battlefield.

Li Haoran blazed with fire, the wounds from the chains’ whips healing rapidly.

Tao Yaoye closed her red paper umbrella. Two Divine Transfiguration cultivators with vacant eyes fell into illusions and dropped into the sea. The East Sea cultivators focused on cultivation but neglected their mental state, resulting in their weakness with illusions.

“Form the array!”

As if they had practiced it a thousand times, the five took their respective positions.

“This is...the Five-Elements Sect’s Five-Elements Combat Tactic?!” One of the Divine Transfiguration cultivators gasped. He had once seen Five-Elements Sect cultivators in action in Great Xia. Those five disciples are at the Basic Nascent Soul Stage, yet after deploying the Five-Elements Combat Tactic, they defeated five Advanced Divine Transfiguration cultivators!

“Didn’t expect someone knowledgeable. Arhat Fist!” Lu Yang stood in the Metal position, focusing on offense.

Enhanced by the Five-Elements Sect Battle Tactic, his speed and strength multiplied exponentially. His movements were as swift as lightning, each punch accurately striking the abdomen and causing his opponent’s organs to churn in excruciating pain.

Their hair also fell out in clumps.

“Stop him quickly!”

“Blue Sea Tide Surge Mantra!”

The three Divine Transfiguration cultivators tried to repeat their tactic, but Lu Yang’s combat prowess was far beyond what it was before. Each punch and kick was unstoppable, like the impact from a mountain. His sword qi was even sharper, slicing through layers of water curtains. The sword’s surface reflected the terrified faces of the three Divine Transfiguration cultivators.

“Twin Ice Dragon Roar!”

Two ice dragons burst from the water, aiming to bite Lu Yang. Man Gu performed Shadow-Swap Teleportation, switching positions with Lu Yang. With a loud shout, he withstood the two ice dragons head-on.

Meng Jingzhou employed Nirvana True Fire to rapidly heal Man Gu’s frostbite.

Man Gu stood in the Earth position, focusing on defense.

Meng Jingzhou stood in the Water position, focusing on recovery.

Tao Yaoye in the Wood position, focusing on changes. She could instantly teleport the five anywhere within the great array and also coordinate the combat of the other four.

“Don’t think only you can use combination techniques! Boundless Sea!”

Five Divine Transfiguration cultivators had been secretly charging up power for a long time. The vast sea surged with a tsunami that was a hundred meters high. It faintly grew ghostly faces and hands and was accompanied by mournful shrieks as it lunged toward Lu Yang and the others.

If Lu Yang’s group dodged, the Fangshan Island behind them would be submerged in the sea!

“Let me handle this!” Li Haoran yelled as several types of flames appeared around him.

Three Flavor True Fire, Golden Bird True Flame, Nirvana True Flame, Six Ding Divine Fire, Extreme Calculation True Fire, Three Esse True Fire, and the Nanming Li Fire!

Most of these flames were what the five had learned from the Fire Branch of the Five-Elements Sect. The seven flames resembled a blooming lotus. Under the enhancement from the Five Elements Combat Tactic, he could use all the true fires mastered by everyone!

Li Haoran stood in the Fire Position, assisting in offense.

The seven flames intertwined, transforming into a towering fire tornado that soared skyward, carrying intense heat and destruction as it collided with the ghost-faced tsunami.

Boom!

The tsunami collapsed, and the ghosts hidden within it died amidst anguished wails. These were ghosts accumulated by those Five Divine Transfiguration cultivators over centuries, yet they had all turned to ashes!

“Attack together!”

The twelve Divine Transfiguration cultivators attacked simultaneously, attempting to find flaws in the Five Elements Battle Tactic. But how could they find flaws in a technique passed down by the Five-Elements Sect for a hundred thousand years? Moreover, Lu Yang and the other four coordinated seamlessly, as if they had practiced for many years.

The twelve Divine Transfiguration cultivators fled. They employed techniques like the Heavenly Devil Grand Art, escaping in blood and looking utterly disheveled.

The Five Elements Combat Tactic excelled in combat power but not in speed. Catching one or two Divine Transfiguration cultivators was feasible, but the remaining ten would definitely escape.

The corners of Lu Yang’s mouth curled into a smirk. “Thinking of running after losing? Perfect, I just learned a new move from Shifu. I’ll practice it on all of you!

“Old Meng, lend me!”

Meng Jingzhou was stunned, not understanding what Lu Yang wanted to borrow from him. Then, his body tilted as Lu Yang grabbed his ankle and lifted him up.

“Hey hey hey, what are you doing?”

“Spare the nonsense; quickly perform Three Heads Six Arms! One Sword Into Ten Thousand Swords!”

“Why did the sky turn dark?” Gao Feng was perplexed. The moonlight seemed to vanish suddenly. Even in the midst of his frantic escape, he couldn’t help but look up.

The sight chilled him to the bones.

Dense shadows blotted out the moonlight. Upon closer examination, those shadows were none other than Meng Jingzhou!

Thousands of Meng Jingzhous, using Three Heads Six Arms, descended from the sky. They shouted and swung their fists as they fell, crashing toward the twelve fleeing Divine Transfiguration cultivators!

Chapter 751: One Meng Into Ten Thousand Mengs

The East Sea had always been renowned for its vast territory, abundant resources, and endless wonders. The twelve Divine Transfiguration cultivators were all considered local leaders of their own areas. They attended various banquets year-round and had ample experience, having even seen many of the bizarre seafolk dwelling in the deep sea.

But they had truly never seen hordes of Meng Jingzhous descending from the sky.

They wouldn’t even encounter such a scene in their nightmares.

The sky was filled with Meng Jingzhous performing Three Heads Six Arms. Even if the twelve Divine Transfiguration cultivators scattered and fled, it was useless—they were all within the attack range of One Sword Into Ten Thousand Swords.

Watching the battle from a distance, the Fangshan Island Three Heroes were utterly dumbfounded.

Lu Yang panted heavily. This terrifying move wasn’t easy to execute. Performing the normal One Sword Into Ten Thousand Swords involved solidifying sword intent into physical swords. Since it could transform into swords, it could also transform into the Sword-Cleansing Pond and Meng Jingzhou.

The normal “One Sword Into Ten Thousand Swords” didn’t have high requirements for the strength of one’s spiritual consciousness. The main attack method was simply using piles of swords to smash the enemy.

But “One Meng Into Ten Thousand Mengs” wasn’t so easy. It was equivalent to thousands of Meng Jingzhous striking simultaneously, placing high demands on one’s spiritual consciousness. Even with the strength of Lu Yang’s spiritual consciousness, he couldn’t perform it alone.

Fortunately, they were currently using the Five Elements Combat Tactic, which could allow them to share not only power but also spiritual consciousness.

Lu Yang’s spiritual consciousness needed no further mention; it was number one among his peers at the same level.

Due to Meng Jingzhou’s long-term conflict with Lu Yang, the former had also trained his spiritual consciousness to be sufficiently strong.

Tao Yaoye was adept at illusions, so the strength of her spiritual consciousness was equally impressive.

When Li Haoran obtained Qin Haoran’s memories, his spiritual consciousness had also expanded accordingly.

Man Gu... Man Gu’s spiritual consciousness strength was rather average.

Only by amalgamating the spiritual consciousness of Lu Yang and the other three could “One Meng Into Ten Thousand Mengs” be performed.

“I was originally thinking of trying it and switching to the Sword-Cleansing Pond if it didn’t work. I didn’t expect it to succeed.” Lu Yang stroked his chin. This was a move I thought of on the spot, and it seems quite effective now.

Meng Jingzhou swung his fists with strange cries, not bothering with any style. His spiritual consciousness strength also didn’t allow for such precise control.

He just had to fight.

Those Divine Transfiguration cultivators were already injured, and with the barrage of assaults from the numerous Meng Jingzhous, they fell into the sea like dumplings dropping into a pot.

The thousands of Meng Jingzhous vanished.

“That’s what you get for running!” When Meng Jingzhou returned, his six hands held six Divine Transfiguration cultivators.

Lu Yang and the others also sprang into action, retrieving the Divine Transfiguration cultivators who had fallen into the sea.

“One, two, three... All twelve accounted for.” Lu Yang wore an accomplished expression. He clapped his hands and ingested a pill to recover his stamina.

Having witnessed the entire process, the Fangshan Island Three Heroes widened their eyes, their eyeballs almost popping out of their sockets. These are twelve Divine Transfiguration cultivators!

They had heard that immortal sect disciples possessed extraordinary combat prowess and were unbeatable among peers of the same level, facing no difficulty in challenging those at higher levels. But they never expected it to be this exaggerated. Despite facing opponents who far surpassed them in both cultivation and numbers, they not only won but also captured them all alive?!

Seeing the battle end, the Three Heroes were about to approach when they heard Lu Yang’s auditory message.

“Don’t come over yet. If you three come now, you’ll know their identities, and it will inevitably lead to revenge in the future.”

The Three Heroes immediately understood and halted.

Lu Yang pulled down the masks of each person one by one and snorted coldly. “How dare you oppose our Five-Elements Sect? You really have a death wish. Haven’t you asked around? In Great Xia, apart from the Dao-Seeking Sect, who dares to provoke our Five-Elements Sect members?

“Or do you also have half-immortals backing you?”

The Divine Transfiguration cultivators broke out in cold sweat upon hearing this and kowtowed repeatedly. Let alone having half-immortals backing us, we haven’t even heard of there being any half-immortals in the East Sea.

“All you know is kowtowing for mercy. You don’t understand how things work. Hand over all your valuables.” Meng Jingzhou kicked Gao Feng over, warning them to be more cooperative.

Robbery was also a distinctive feature of the East Sea; one had to experience it at least once.

The Divine Transfiguration cultivators were filled with regret. Isn’t it said that Great Xia is peaceful and that cultivators fought with restraint, never killing their opponents? Why does this situation seem completely different?

Even native East Sea cultivators can’t compete with them.

As captives, keeping our lives is already extremely fortunate; wealth is merely external possessions... They comforted themselves with this thought while bearing the pain of taking out their most precious treasures.

Cultivation manuals, maps, information on secret domains, magical treasures, spirit stones...

Li Haoran shook his head in disappointment. “You East Sea cultivators aren’t very skilled. You handed over your storage rings just like that? If it were me, I’d definitely have prepared one official and one secret storage ring. The secret one would be concealed inside my body. I’d tear open a wound, put the ring in, then let the body heal.”

Due to personal reasons, Li Haoran had extensive experience in hiding things.

Upon hearing Li Haoran’s remark, the Divine Transfiguration cultivators hung their heads in shame. To think that we’re outmatched by a Five-Elements Sect disciple in our experience of hiding things...

“Alright, the rare treasure of Fangshan Island now belongs to our Five-Elements Sect. Get lost!”

“Yes yes yes.” Feeling like they had been granted amnesty, the Divine Transfiguration cultivators nodded and bowed.

“Wait, don’t leave yet. There’s one more thing.”

“Please speak.” The Divine Transfiguration cultivators thought Meng Jingzhou was going to renege on the decision to let them go, and their hearts almost leaped to their throats.

“The Fangshan Island Three Heroes have done us a huge favor. I’ve memorized all your faces. If I ever hear that something happened to Fangshan Island in the future, regardless of whether you’re suspected or not, every single one of you will be held accountable! Don’t dream of getting away!”

Meng Jingzhou paused, then glared and roared, “What are you still standing around for? Get lost! Did you think I was going to ask you to stay for dinner?!”

The Divine Transfiguration cultivators immediately scrambled away. These five are too sinister; staying even a moment longer is terrifying.

Only then did the matter conclude, and the Fangshan Island Three Heroes flew over timidly.

“Is...is it over?” Hero Yan still found it hard to believe.

“It’s over. If anyone asks you about the rare treasure in the future, just tell them the truth,” Lu Yang said. The Metamorphic Immortal Grass was too precious; it was a treasure that could tempt even Fusion cultivators. It would be a calamity and not a blessing for it to be in the Three Heroes’ possession.

The immortal grass wasn’t something they were qualified to possess in the first place. Obtaining a fifth-grade spirit vein was already tremendously fortunate. The Three Heroes were extremely grateful to Lu Yang and the others.

Lu Yang suddenly thought of another safety issue. “If I recall correctly, fifth-grade spirit veins are usually held by Fusion cultivators. Would it be unsafe for the three of you to possess it?”

Territorial disputes occurred frequently in the East Sea; otherwise, the map from a hundred years ago wouldn’t be vastly different from the current one. Even if Lu Yang had warned those twelve Divine Transfiguration cultivators, there was no guarantee that other Divine Transfiguration cultivators wouldn’t covet this place.

Hero Yan sighed. “It is indeed not quite safe, but there’s no other way. The current plan is to rely on the fifth-grade spirit vein for me to reach the Divine Transfiguration Stage as soon as possible. Only then will Fangshan Island be truly safe.”

“I see that your cultivation is already at the Advanced Nascent Soul Stage?” Lu Yang suddenly said.

Hero Yan replied truthfully, “Previously, I was at the Great Perfection Advanced Nascent Soul Stage, but after drinking the Wudao Enlightenment Tea, I’m now at the Half-Step Divine Transfiguration Stage. I just don’t know when I’ll be able to cross the other half-step.”

Lu Yang smiled. “There’s no better day than today. How about letting you advance to the Divine Transfiguration Stage tonight?”

Chapter 752: Divine Concentration Pill

“To-tonight?!” Yan Chuan thought he was hearing things.

We’re talking about advancing to the Divine Transfiguration Stage! Is this something one can just decide to do today?

I’ve already prepared myself to advance within twenty years.

Taking a step back, advancing to the Divine Transfiguration Stage requires enduring a lightning tribulation. One will need to prepare many contingencies for that; there is no room for carelessness.

Helping someone advance to the Divine Transfiguration Stage, especially someone at the Half-Step Divine Transfiguration Stage, was quite simple for Lu Yang. It was just a matter of a pill.

Immortal sect disciples focused on their own cultivation realms, at most using pills as supplements. After all, pills were external aids. Power gained by relying on external support often had flaws and was detrimental to future cultivation.

But Yan Chuan was different. For a rogue cultivator like him, reaching the Nascent Soul Stage was already an extremely lucky feat. He had lost count of how many cultivation methods he had switched between to cultivate to the Nascent Soul Stage. That resulted in his qi becoming adulterated, making it difficult for him to raise his cultivation realm further.

Consuming pills could actually help him purify and regulate his qi.

“Senior Brother Lu, do you have pills that help people break through to the Divine Transfiguration Stage?” Tao Yaoye asked. If they were at Pill Cauldron Peak, such pills would be plentiful, but they were now in the East Sea. Who would carry pills they didn’t need?

“By chance, yes.” Lu Yang felt around his identity jade tablet a few times and pulled out a bottle of pills.

A round pill rolled out, causing Yan Chuan’s eyes to go wide. “Di-Divine Concentration Pills?”

This was a priceless pill. He had seen it twice at auctions, where it fetched astronomical prices. Once, even a disciple from Yingzhou Island was among the bidders. If even Yingzhou Island disciples had to obtain the Divine Concentration Pill from outside, it showed how valuable it was.

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou had obtained this Divine Concentration Pill when they went to the Demon Region. Gan Tian didn’t have a meeting gift on hand and took the two to rummage through the inheritance of a certain Suanni. That Suanni was one she had killed when she first arrived in the Demon Region, and its bequest included a Divine Concentration Pill.

Lu Yang had never seen what a lightning tribulation for the Divine Transfiguration Stage looked like, so this was a good chance for him to broaden his horizons.

“It’s useless for me to keep it. Hero Yan, it’s yours.” Lu Yang nonchalantly tossed the Divine Concentration Pill to Yan Chuan, his action as casual as throwing a jelly bean.

Hero Yan caught the Divine Concentration Pill with both hands, treating it as a supreme treasure.

“But...but I’m not prepared to face the lightning tribulation!” The hope of advancing to the Divine Transfiguration Stage was in his hands, but Yan Chuan knew his worth. I’m just an ordinary Nascent Soul cultivator. Without preparation, the probability of being struck dead by the lightning tribulation is extremely high.

“Oh right, lightning tribulations can actually kill people.” Lu Yang finally remembered a fact he had long overlooked.

He mentally went through the list of people he knew and finally thought of an example. “Speaking of which, the only person I know who was struck dead during a tribulation was Qin Haoran.”

If Qin Haoran hadn’t been struck dead, there wouldn’t be the current Li Haoran.

“Immortal Fairy, do you have any solutions?” After pondering for a long time, Lu Yang decided to consult the ever-resourceful Everlasting Immortal Fairy for ideas.

“The most important thing when facing a lightning tribulation is confidence. With enough confidence, the lightning tribulation is just a formality.”

“Really? There’s such a saying?” Lu Yang asked. How come I’ve never heard of this theory?

“At the very least, that’s how this immortal passed all my lightning tribulations in the past, including the Immortal Ascension Tribulation.”

Lu Yang, “...”

Is this related to confidence? Isn’t it because you’re too powerful, Immortal Fairy?

If I were to tell this method to Hero Yan, he’d probably be struck dead by the lightning tribulation with full confidence.

Since I can’t count on the Immortal Fairy, I must rely on myself.

“Junior Brother Li, you have the most experience. Do you have any ideas?”

Li Haoran contemplated. “Facing a tribulation ultimately depends on oneself. If others help, it will only increase the lightning tribulation’s power, so we can’t interfere when Hero Yan undergoes his lightning tribulation.

“However, given Hero Yan’s cultivation, passing the lightning tribulation is indeed challenging. In that case, he could try using magical treasures to block the lightning. But using magical treasures isn’t a good idea, for it negates the body-tempering effect of the lightning. When he becomes a Divine Transfiguration cultivator, he’ll be inherently weaker than others.

“We should find a method to enhance Hero Yan’s physique temporarily.”

Right then, Meng Jingzhou thought of an idea. “How about this? Hero Yan can temporarily take over my body and control my body to face the lightning tribulation. That way, he will temper his soul. At the same time, he can place his own corpse on my head. That way, he will also temper his physical body.

“After tempering both his soul and body, he just has to combine them, and it will count as having tempered everything.”

Hero Yan felt this method wasn’t very reliable.

Everyone discussed back and forth before finally choosing the most basic method—feeding him pills.

The storage rings they had just confiscated contained pills that provided temporary bursts of power. They were all for the Divine Transfiguration Stage, and their effects were absolutely reliable. If Hero Yan felt he couldn’t make it, he could ingest one.

“Hero Yan, relax, believe in yourself.” Lu Yang ultimately didn’t forget the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s method and encouraged Yan Chuan before his tribulation.

“I will not let you down!” Hero Yan cupped his fists, his expression resolute. He was filled with unprecedented confidence.

The Five-Elements Sect disciples have wholeheartedly helped me; it’s inexcusable for me to lack confidence now.

Yan Chuan went to the mountain summit and asked everyone to stay away.

He first ingested the Divine Concentration Pill, and the half-step that had lingered before the Divine Transfiguration Stage finally crossed the threshold! His entire body felt like searing fire, heating up from the inside out.

Boom!

Dark clouds gathered, rolling like splashed ink. Lightning flashed and thunder clapped like madly dancing dragons and snakes, illuminating the whole night sky as bright as day.

“Come on!” Yan Chuan shouted with the momentum of sinking his boats and cutting off all means of retreat.

A fierce purple thunderbolt descended from the clouds high above in the ninth heaven, its force unstoppable and its power peerless. Carrying the power to annihilate everything, it struck directly at Yan Chuan.

He slowly closed his eyes and uttered something in a low voice as he formed hand seals. Instantly, golden light blazed around him, transforming into a huge golden shield that forcefully withstood this heavenly lightning that was capable of destroying mountains.

The other two heroes’ hearts palpitated as they witnessed this scene. The lightning tribulation’s power is terrifying; can Big Brother really withstand it?

“This lightning tribulation doesn’t look very powerful?” Man Gu transmitted an auditory message.

“Ordinary lightning tribulations at the Divine Transfiguration Stage are like this,” Li Haoran explained. This lightning tribulation was like a drizzle for them but a monumental trial for Yan Chuan.

As the thunderclouds churned, increasingly powerful lightning bolts fell one after another, each more frightening than the last, as if they were trying to shatter both Yan Chuan’s Dao heart and physical body. Yet, Yan Chuan didn’t consume any pills. Relying solely on his cultivation, he withstood the repeated cleansing from the lightning tribulation.

After the lightning tribulation ended, the dark clouds dispersed.

Yan Chuan sat cross-legged on the mountaintop, his clothes tattered and his hair scorched black, resembling a beggar. He opened his eyes and felt the newly acquired power. Unable to suppress his joy, he laughed heartily.

He flew down the mountain and bowed to Lu Yang and the others. “Thank you all for your help. This great favor is something I can never repay!”

“Big Brother, you succeeded?!” The other two heroes’ voices quivered as they hugged Yan Chuan, crying and laughing.

Yan Chuan also couldn’t help but cry.

He had thought he would waste the rest of his life at the Nascent Soul Stage, with no hope of reaching the Divine Transfiguration Stage. Yet, with the help of Lu Yang and the others, he had successfully advanced to the Divine Transfiguration Stage without even taking any pills!

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was smug, not surprised by this. “See? I told you one could get through with confidence alone.”

Lu Yang was truly astonished. He hadn’t expected confidence to be so effective. Does this mean I can also pass tribulations this way?

“With this immortal protecting you, you’ll definitely be full of confidence. Facing tribulations won’t be a problem!”

Lu Yang’s steadfast confidence began to waver.
